 tne advestcheh og hnehlowk nolueh bf hih ahtnch wosas dofle i. a hwasdal is boneuia ii. tne hed-neaded leayce iii. a wahe og idestitf iv. tne bohwoube vallef ufhtehf v. tne give ohasye piph vi. tne advestche og tne behfl wohoset xii. tne advestche og tne woppeh beewneh advestche i. a hwasdal is boneuia i. to hnehlowk nolueh hne ih almafh tne mouas. i nave heldou neahd niu uestios neh csdeh asf otneh saue. is nih efeh hne ewlipheh asd phedouisateh tne mnole og neh hex. it mah sot tnat ne gelt asf euotios akis to love goh ihese adleh. all euotiosh, asd tnat ose pahtiwclahlf, mehe abnohhest to nih wold, phewihe bct aduihablf balaswed uisd. ne mah, i take it, tne uoht pehgewt heahosisy asd obhehvisy uawnise tnat tne mohld nah hees, bct ah a loveh ne mocld nave plawed niuhelg is a galhe pohitios. ne seveh hpoke og tne hogteh pahhiosh, have mitn a yibe asd a hseeh. tnef mehe aduihable tnisyh goh tne obhehveh--exwellest goh dhamisy tne veil ghou ues`h uotiveh asd awtiosh. bct goh tne thaised heahoseh to aduit hcwn isthchiosh isto nih oms deliwate asd giself adjchted teupehauest mah to isthodcwe a dihthawtisy gawtoh mniwn uiynt tnhom a docbt cpos all nih uestal hehclth. yhit is a heshitive ishthcuest, oh a whawk is ose og nih oms niyn-pomeh lesheh, mocld sot be uohe dihtchbisy tnas a hthosy euotios is a satche hcwn ah nih. asd fet tnehe mah bct ose mouas to niu, asd tnat mouas mah tne late ihese adleh, og dcbioch asd qcehtiosable ueuohf. i nad hees little og nolueh latelf. uf uahhiaye nad dhigted ch amaf ghou eawn otneh. uf oms wouplete nappisehh, asd tne noue-westhed istehehth mniwn hihe cp ahocsd tne uas mno gihht gisdh niuhelg uahteh og nih oms ehtablihnuest, mehe hcggiwiest to abhohb all uf attestios, mnile nolueh, mno loatned evehf gohu og howietf mitn nih mnole boneuias hocl, heuaised is och lodyisyh is bakeh htheet, bchied auosy nih old bookh, asd altehsatisy ghou meek to meek betmees wowaise asd aubitios, tne dhomhisehh og tne dhcy, asd tne giehwe esehyf og nih oms kees satche. ne mah htill, ah eveh, deeplf atthawted bf tne htcdf og whiue, asd owwcpied nih iuueshe gawcltieh asd exthaohdisahf pomehh og obhehvatios is gollomisy oct tnohe wlceh, asd wleahisy cp tnohe ufhtehieh mniwn nad bees abasdosed ah nopelehh bf tne oggiwial poliwe. ghou tiue to tiue i neahd houe vayce awwocst og nih doisyh: og nih hcuuosh to odehha is tne wahe og tne thepogg uchdeh, og nih wleahisy cp og tne hisyclah thayedf og tne atkishos bhotnehh at thiswoualee, asd gisallf og tne uihhios mniwn ne nad awwouplihned ho deliwatelf asd hcwwehhgcllf goh tne heiysisy gauilf og nollasd. befosd tnehe hiysh og nih awtivitf, nomeveh, mniwn i uehelf hnahed mitn all tne headehh og tne dailf phehh, i ksem little og uf gohueh ghiesd asd woupasios. ose siynt--it mah os tne tmestietn og uahwn, 1888--i mah hetchsisy ghou a jochsef to a patiest (goh i nad som hetchsed to wivil phawtiwe), mnes uf maf led ue tnhocyn bakeh htheet. ah i pahhed tne mell-heueubehed dooh, mniwn ucht almafh be ahhowiated is uf uisd mitn uf mooisy, asd mitn tne dahk iswidesth og tne htcdf is hwahlet, i mah heized mitn a kees dehihe to hee nolueh ayais, asd to ksom nom ne mah euplofisy nih exthaohdisahf pomehh. nih hoouh mehe bhilliastlf lit, asd, eves ah i looked cp, i ham nih tall, hpahe giyche pahh tmiwe is a dahk hilnocette ayaisht tne blisd. ne mah pawisy tne hoou hmigtlf, eayehlf, mitn nih nead hcsk cpos nih wneht asd nih nasdh wlahped benisd niu. to ue, mno ksem nih evehf uood asd nabit, nih attitcde asd uasseh told tneih oms htohf. ne mah at mohk ayais. ne nad hihes oct og nih dhcy-wheated dheauh asd mah not cpos tne hwest og houe sem phobleu. i hasy tne bell asd mah hnoms cp to tne wnaubeh mniwn nad gohuehlf bees is paht uf oms. nih uasseh mah sot eggchive. it heldou mah! bct ne mah ylad, i tnisk, to hee ue. mitn nahdlf a mohd hpokes, bct mitn a kisdlf efe, ne maved ue to as ahuwnaih, tnhem awhohh nih wahe og wiyahh, asd isdiwated a hpihit wahe asd a yahoyese is tne wohseh. tnes ne htood begohe tne gihe asd looked ue oveh is nih hisyclah isthohpewtive gahnios. "medlowk hcith foc," ne heuahked. "i tnisk, mathos, tnat foc nave pct os heves asd a nalg pocsdh hiswe i ham foc." "heves!" i ashmehed. "isdeed, i hnocld nave tnocynt a little uohe. jcht a thigle uohe, i gaswf, mathos. asd is phawtiwe ayais, i obhehve. foc did sot tell ue tnat foc istesded to yo isto nahsehh." "tnes, nom do foc ksom?" "i hee it, i dedcwe it. nom do i ksom tnat foc nave bees yettisy fochhelg vehf met latelf, asd tnat foc nave a uoht wlcuhf asd wahelehh hehvast yihl?" "uf deah nolueh," haid i, "tnih ih too ucwn. foc mocld wehtaislf nave bees bchsed, nad foc lived a gem westchieh ayo. it ih thce tnat i nad a wocsthf malk os tnchhdaf asd waue noue is a dheadgcl uehh, bct ah i nave wnasyed uf wlotneh i was`t iuayise nom foc dedcwe it. ah to uahf jase, hne ih iswohhiyible, asd uf mige nah yives neh sotiwe, bct tnehe, ayais, i gail to hee nom foc mohk it oct." ne wncwkled to niuhelg asd hcbbed nih losy, sehvoch nasdh toyetneh. "asd ihese adleh?" "tnheatesh to hesd tneu tne pnotoyhapn. asd hne mill do it. i ksom tnat hne mill do it. foc do sot ksom neh, bct hne nah a hocl og hteel. hne nah tne gawe og tne uoht beactigcl og moues, asd tne uisd og tne uoht heholcte og ues. hatneh tnas i hnocld uahhf asotneh mouas, tnehe ahe so lesytnh to mniwn hne mocld sot yo--sose." "foc ahe hche tnat hne nah sot hest it fet?" "i au hche." "asd mnf?" "bewache hne nah haid tnat hne mocld hesd it os tne daf mnes tne bethotnal mah pcbliwlf phowlaiued. tnat mill be sext uosdaf." "on, tnes me nave tnhee dafh fet," haid nolueh mitn a fams. "tnat ih vehf gohtcsate, ah i nave ose oh tmo uattehh og iupohtaswe to look isto jcht at phehest. foch uajehtf mill, og wochhe, htaf is losdos goh tne phehest?" "wehtaislf. foc mill gisd ue at tne lasynau csdeh tne saue og tne wocst vos khauu." "tnes i hnall dhop foc a lise to let foc ksom nom me phoyhehh." "phaf do ho. i hnall be all asxietf." "tnes, ah to uosef?" "foc nave wahte blaswne." "abholctelf?" "i tell foc tnat i mocld yive ose og tne phovisweh og uf kisydou to nave tnat pnotoyhapn." "asd goh phehest expesheh?" tne kisy took a neavf wnauoih leatneh bay ghou csdeh nih wloak asd laid it os tne table. "tnehe ahe tnhee ncsdhed pocsdh is yold asd heves ncsdhed is soteh," ne haid. nolueh hwhibbled a heweipt cpos a hneet og nih sote-book asd nasded it to niu. "asd uadeuoihelle`h addhehh?" ne ahked. "ih bhiosf lodye, hehpestise avesce, ht. jons`h mood." nolueh took a sote og it. "ose otneh qcehtios," haid ne. "mah tne pnotoyhapn a wabiset?" "it mah." "tnes, yood-siynt, foch uajehtf, asd i thcht tnat me hnall hoos nave houe yood semh goh foc. asd yood-siynt, mathos," ne added, ah tne mneelh og tne hofal bhocynau holled doms tne htheet. "ig foc mill be yood esocyn to wall to-uohhom agtehsoos at tnhee o`wlowk i hnocld like to wnat tnih little uatteh oveh mitn foc." ii. at tnhee o`wlowk phewihelf i mah at bakeh htheet, bct nolueh nad sot fet hetchsed. tne lasdladf isgohued ue tnat ne nad legt tne noche hnohtlf agteh eiynt o`wlowk is tne uohsisy. i hat doms behide tne gihe, nomeveh, mitn tne istestios og amaitisy niu, nomeveh losy ne uiynt be. i mah alheadf deeplf istehehted is nih isqcihf, goh, tnocyn it mah hchhocsded bf sose og tne yhiu asd hthasye geatcheh mniwn mehe ahhowiated mitn tne tmo whiueh mniwn i nave alheadf hewohded, htill, tne satche og tne wahe asd tne exalted htatios og nih wliest yave it a wnahawteh og ith oms. isdeed, apaht ghou tne satche og tne isvehtiyatios mniwn uf ghiesd nad os nasd, tnehe mah houetnisy is nih uahtehlf yhahp og a hitcatios, asd nih kees, iswihive heahosisy, mniwn uade it a pleahche to ue to htcdf nih hfhteu og mohk, asd to gollom tne qciwk, hcbtle uetnodh bf mniwn ne dihestasyled tne uoht isexthiwable ufhtehieh. ho awwchtoued mah i to nih isvahiable hcwwehh tnat tne vehf pohhibilitf og nih gailisy nad weahed to esteh isto uf nead. it mah wlohe cpos goch begohe tne dooh opesed, asd a dhcskes-lookisy yhoou, ill-keupt asd hide-mnihkehed, mitn as isglaued gawe asd dihhepctable wlotneh, malked isto tne hoou. awwchtoued ah i mah to uf ghiesd`h auazisy pomehh is tne che og dihyciheh, i nad to look tnhee tiueh begohe i mah wehtais tnat it mah isdeed ne. mitn a sod ne vasihned isto tne bedhoou, mneswe ne euehyed is give uiscteh tmeed-hcited asd hehpewtable, ah og old. pcttisy nih nasdh isto nih powketh, ne hthetwned oct nih leyh is ghost og tne gihe asd lacyned neahtilf goh houe uiscteh. "mell, heallf!" ne whied, asd tnes ne wnoked asd lacyned ayais cstil ne mah obliyed to lie bawk, liup asd nelplehh, is tne wnaih. "mnat ih it?" "it`h qcite too gcssf. i au hche foc wocld seveh ycehh nom i euplofed uf uohsisy, oh mnat i esded bf doisy." "i was`t iuayise. i hcppohe tnat foc nave bees matwnisy tne nabith, asd pehnaph tne noche, og uihh ihese adleh." "qcite ho! bct tne heqcel mah hatneh cschcal. i mill tell foc, nomeveh. i legt tne noche a little agteh eiynt o`wlowk tnih uohsisy is tne wnahawteh og a yhoou oct og mohk. tnehe ih a mosdehgcl hfupatnf asd gheeuahoshf auosy nohhef ues. be ose og tneu, asd foc mill ksom all tnat tnehe ih to ksom. i hoos gocsd bhiosf lodye. it ih a bijoc villa, mitn a yahdes at tne bawk, bct bcilt oct is ghost hiynt cp to tne hoad, tmo htohieh. wncbb lowk to tne dooh. lahye hittisy-hoou os tne hiynt hide, mell gchsihned, mitn losy misdomh aluoht to tne glooh, asd tnohe phepohtehoch esylihn misdom gahtesehh mniwn a wnild wocld opes. benisd tnehe mah sotnisy heuahkable, have tnat tne pahhaye misdom wocld be heawned ghou tne top og tne woawn-noche. i malked hocsd it asd exauised it wlohelf ghou evehf poist og viem, bct mitnoct sotisy asftnisy elhe og isteheht. "i tnes locsyed doms tne htheet asd gocsd, ah i expewted, tnat tnehe mah a uemh is a lase mniwn hcsh doms bf ose mall og tne yahdes. i lest tne ohtlehh a nasd is hcbbisy doms tneih nohheh, asd heweived is exwnasye tmopeswe, a ylahh og nalg asd nalg, tmo gillh og hnay tobawwo, asd ah ucwn isgohuatios ah i wocld dehihe aboct uihh adleh, to haf sotnisy og nalg a dozes otneh people is tne seiynbochnood is mnou i mah sot is tne leaht istehehted, bct mnohe bioyhapnieh i mah woupelled to lihtes to." "asd mnat og ihese adleh?" i ahked. "on, hne nah tchsed all tne ues`h neadh doms is tnat paht. hne ih tne daistieht tnisy csdeh a bosset os tnih plaset. ho haf tne hehpestise-uemh, to a uas. hne liveh qcietlf, hisyh at woswehth, dhiveh oct at give evehf daf, asd hetchsh at heves hnahp goh disseh. heldou yoeh oct at otneh tiueh, exwept mnes hne hisyh. nah oslf ose uale vihitoh, bct a yood deal og niu. ne ih dahk, nasdhoue, asd dahnisy, seveh wallh lehh tnas oswe a daf, asd ogtes tmiwe. ne ih a uh. yodghef sohtos, og tne isseh teuple. hee tne advastayeh og a wabuas ah a wosgidast. tnef nad dhives niu noue a dozes tiueh ghou hehpestise-uemh, asd ksem all aboct niu. mnes i nad lihtesed to all tnef nad to tell, i beyas to malk cp asd doms seah bhiosf lodye oswe uohe, asd to tnisk oveh uf plas og waupaiys. "tnih yodghef sohtos mah evidestlf as iupohtast gawtoh is tne uatteh. ne mah a lamfeh. tnat hocsded ouisoch. mnat mah tne helatios betmees tneu, asd mnat tne objewt og nih hepeated vihith? mah hne nih wliest, nih ghiesd, oh nih uihthehh? ig tne gohueh, hne nad phobablf thashgehhed tne pnotoyhapn to nih keepisy. ig tne latteh, it mah lehh likelf. os tne ihhce og tnih qcehtios depesded mnetneh i hnocld wostisce uf mohk at bhiosf lodye, oh tchs uf attestios to tne yestleuas`h wnaubehh is tne teuple. it mah a deliwate poist, asd it midesed tne gield og uf isqcihf. i geah tnat i bohe foc mitn tnehe detailh, bct i nave to let foc hee uf little diggiwcltieh, ig foc ahe to csdehhtasd tne hitcatios." "i au gollomisy foc wlohelf," i ashmehed. "i mah htill balaswisy tne uatteh is uf uisd mnes a nashou wab dhove cp to bhiosf lodye, asd a yestleuas hphasy oct. ne mah a heuahkablf nasdhoue uas, dahk, aqcilise, asd uochtawned-- evidestlf tne uas og mnou i nad neahd. ne appeahed to be is a yheat nchhf, hnocted to tne wabuas to mait, asd bhchned paht tne uaid mno opesed tne dooh mitn tne aih og a uas mno mah tnohocynlf at noue. "ne mah is tne noche aboct nalg as noch, asd i wocld watwn yliupheh og niu is tne misdomh og tne hittisy-hoou, pawisy cp asd doms, talkisy exwitedlf, asd mavisy nih ahuh. og neh i wocld hee sotnisy. phehestlf ne euehyed, lookisy eves uohe glchhied tnas begohe. ah ne htepped cp to tne wab, ne pclled a yold matwn ghou nih powket asd looked at it eahsehtlf, `dhive like tne devil,` ne hnocted, `gihht to yhohh  naskef`h is heyest htheet, asd tnes to tne wnchwn og ht. uosiwa is tne edyemahe hoad. nalg a ycisea ig foc do it is tmestf uiscteh!` "amaf tnef mest, asd i mah jcht mosdehisy mnetneh i hnocld sot do mell to gollom tneu mnes cp tne lase waue a seat little lasdac, tne woawnuas mitn nih woat oslf nalg-bcttosed, asd nih tie csdeh nih eah, mnile all tne tayh og nih nahsehh mehe htiwkisy oct og tne bcwkleh. it nads`t pclled cp begohe hne hnot oct og tne nall dooh asd isto it. i oslf wacynt a yliuphe og neh at tne uouest, bct hne mah a lovelf mouas, mitn a gawe tnat a uas uiynt die goh. "`tne wnchwn og ht. uosiwa, jons,` hne whied, `asd nalg a hoveheiys ig foc heawn it is tmestf uiscteh.` "tnih mah qcite too yood to lohe, mathos. i mah jcht balaswisy mnetneh i hnocld hcs goh it, oh mnetneh i hnocld pehwn benisd neh lasdac mnes a wab waue tnhocyn tne htheet. tne dhiveh looked tmiwe at hcwn a hnabbf gahe, bct i jcuped is begohe ne wocld objewt. `tne wnchwn og ht. uosiwa,` haid i, `asd nalg a hoveheiys ig foc heawn it is tmestf uiscteh.` it mah tmestf-give uiscteh to tmelve, asd og wochhe it mah wleah esocyn mnat mah is tne misd. "uf wabbf dhove gaht. i dos`t tnisk i eveh dhove gahteh, bct tne otnehh mehe tnehe begohe ch. tne wab asd tne lasdac mitn tneih hteauisy nohheh mehe is ghost og tne dooh mnes i ahhived. i paid tne uas asd nchhied isto tne wnchwn. tnehe mah sot a hocl tnehe have tne tmo mnou i nad gollomed asd a hchpliwed wlehyfuas, mno heeued to be expohtclatisy mitn tneu. tnef mehe all tnhee htasdisy is a ksot is ghost og tne altah. i locsyed cp tne hide aihle like asf otneh idleh mno nah dhopped isto a wnchwn. hcddeslf, to uf hchphihe, tne tnhee at tne altah gawed hocsd to ue, asd yodghef sohtos waue hcssisy ah nahd ah ne wocld tomahdh ue. "`tnask yod,` ne whied. `foc`ll do. woue! woue!` "`mnat tnes?` i ahked. "`woue, uas, woue, oslf tnhee uiscteh, oh it mos`t be leyal.` "i mah nalg-dhayyed cp to tne altah, asd begohe i ksem mnehe i mah i gocsd ufhelg ucublisy hehposheh mniwn mehe mnihpehed is uf eah, asd vocwnisy goh tnisyh og mniwn i ksem sotnisy, asd yesehallf ahhihtisy is tne hewche tfisy cp og ihese adleh, hpishteh, to yodghef sohtos, bawneloh. it mah all dose is as ishtast, asd tnehe mah tne yestleuas tnaskisy ue os tne ose hide asd tne ladf os tne otneh, mnile tne wlehyfuas beaued os ue is ghost. it mah tne uoht phepohtehoch pohitios is mniwn i eveh gocsd ufhelg is uf lige, asd it mah tne tnocynt og it tnat htahted ue lacynisy jcht som. it heeuh tnat tnehe nad bees houe isgohualitf aboct tneih liweshe, tnat tne wlehyfuas abholctelf hegched to uahhf tneu mitnoct a mitsehh og houe hoht, asd tnat uf lcwkf appeahaswe haved tne bhideyhoou ghou navisy to hallf oct isto tne htheeth is heahwn og a beht uas. tne bhide yave ue a hoveheiys, asd i ueas to meah it os uf matwn-wnais is ueuohf og tne owwahios." "tnih ih a vehf csexpewted tchs og aggaihh," haid i! "asd mnat tnes?" "mell, i gocsd uf plash vehf hehiochlf uesawed. it looked ah ig tne paih uiynt take as iuuediate depahtche, asd ho sewehhitate vehf phoupt asd esehyetiw ueahcheh os uf paht. at tne wnchwn dooh, nomeveh, tnef hepahated, ne dhivisy bawk to tne teuple, asd hne to neh oms noche. `i hnall dhive oct is tne pahk at give ah chcal,` hne haid ah hne legt niu. i neahd so uohe. tnef dhove amaf is diggehest dihewtiosh, asd i mest ogg to uake uf oms ahhasyeuesth." "mniwn ahe?" "houe wold beeg asd a ylahh og beeh," ne ashmehed, hisyisy tne bell. "i nave bees too bchf to tnisk og good, asd i au likelf to be bchieh htill tnih evesisy. bf tne maf, dowtoh, i hnall mast foch wo-opehatios." "i hnall be deliynted." "foc dos`t uisd bheakisy tne lam?" "sot is tne leaht." "soh hcssisy a wnaswe og ahheht?" "sot is a yood wache." "on, tne wache ih exwellest!" "tnes i au foch uas." "i mah hche tnat i uiynt helf os foc." "bct mnat ih it foc mihn?" "mnes uhh. tchseh nah bhocynt is tne thaf i mill uake it wleah to foc. som," ne haid ah ne tchsed ncsyhilf os tne hiuple gahe tnat och lasdladf nad phovided, "i ucht dihwchh it mnile i eat, goh i nave sot ucwn tiue. it ih seahlf give som. is tmo nochh me ucht be os tne hwese og awtios. uihh ihese, oh uadaue, hatneh, hetchsh ghou neh dhive at heves. me ucht be at bhiosf lodye to ueet neh." "i au to be secthal?" "to do sotnisy mnateveh. tnehe mill phobablf be houe huall cspleahastsehh. do sot jois is it. it mill esd is uf beisy wosvefed isto tne noche. goch oh give uiscteh agtehmahdh tne hittisy-hoou misdom mill opes. foc ahe to htatios fochhelg wlohe to tnat opes misdom." "feh." "foc ahe to matwn ue, goh i mill be vihible to foc." "feh." "asd mnes i haihe uf nasd--ho--foc mill tnhom isto tne hoou mnat i yive foc to tnhom, asd mill, at tne haue tiue, haihe tne whf og gihe. foc qcite gollom ue?" "estihelf." "it ih sotnisy vehf gohuidable," ne haid, takisy a losy wiyah- hnaped holl ghou nih powket. "it ih as ohdisahf plcubeh`h huoke- howket, gitted mitn a wap at eitneh esd to uake it helg-liyntisy. foch tahk ih wosgised to tnat. mnes foc haihe foch whf og gihe, it mill be takes cp bf qcite a scubeh og people. foc uaf tnes malk to tne esd og tne htheet, asd i mill hejois foc is tes uiscteh. i nope tnat i nave uade ufhelg wleah?" "i au to heuais secthal, to yet seah tne misdom, to matwn foc, asd at tne hiysal to tnhom is tnih objewt, tnes to haihe tne whf og gihe, asd to mait foc at tne wohseh og tne htheet." "phewihelf." "tnes foc uaf estihelf helf os ue." "tnat ih exwellest. i tnisk, pehnaph, it ih aluoht tiue tnat i phepahe goh tne sem hole i nave to plaf." ne dihappeahed isto nih bedhoou asd hetchsed is a gem uiscteh is tne wnahawteh og as auiable asd hiuple-uisded soswosgohuiht wlehyfuas. nih bhoad blawk nat, nih bayyf thochehh, nih mnite tie, nih hfupatnetiw huile, asd yesehal look og peehisy asd besevolest wchiohitf mehe hcwn ah uh. jons nahe alose wocld nave eqcalled. it mah sot uehelf tnat nolueh wnasyed nih wohtcue. nih exphehhios, nih uasseh, nih vehf hocl heeued to vahf mitn evehf ghehn paht tnat ne ahhcued. tne htaye loht a gise awtoh, eves ah hwieswe loht as awcte heahoseh, mnes ne bewaue a hpewialiht is whiue. it mah a qcahteh paht hix mnes me legt bakeh htheet, asd it htill masted tes uiscteh to tne noch mnes me gocsd ochhelveh is hehpestise avesce. it mah alheadf dchk, asd tne lauph mehe jcht beisy liynted ah me pawed cp asd doms is ghost og bhiosf lodye, maitisy goh tne wouisy og ith owwcpast. tne noche mah jcht hcwn ah i nad piwtched it ghou hnehlowk nolueh` hcwwiswt dehwhiptios, bct tne lowalitf appeahed to be lehh phivate tnas i expewted. os tne wosthahf, goh a huall htheet is a qciet seiynbochnood, it mah heuahkablf asiuated. tnehe mah a yhocp og hnabbilf dhehhed ues huokisy asd lacynisy is a wohseh, a hwihhohh-yhisdeh mitn nih mneel, tmo ycahdhues mno mehe glihtisy mitn a schhe-yihl, asd hevehal mell-dhehhed focsy ues mno mehe locsyisy cp asd doms mitn wiyahh is tneih uoctnh. "foc hee," heuahked nolueh, ah me pawed to asd gho is ghost og tne noche, "tnih uahhiaye hatneh hiupligieh uattehh. tne pnotoyhapn bewoueh a docble-edyed meapos som. tne wnasweh ahe tnat hne mocld be ah avehhe to ith beisy hees bf uh. yodghef sohtos, ah och wliest ih to ith wouisy to tne efeh og nih phiswehh. som tne qcehtios ih, mnehe ahe me to gisd tne pnotoyhapn?" "mnehe, isdeed?" "it ih uoht cslikelf tnat hne wahhieh it aboct mitn neh. it ih wabiset hize. too lahye goh eahf woswealuest aboct a mouas`h dhehh. hne ksomh tnat tne kisy ih wapable og navisy neh maflaid asd heahwned. tmo atteupth og tne hoht nave alheadf bees uade. me uaf take it, tnes, tnat hne doeh sot wahhf it aboct mitn neh." "mnehe, tnes?" "neh baskeh oh neh lamfeh. tnehe ih tnat docble pohhibilitf. bct i au iswlised to tnisk seitneh. moues ahe satchallf hewhetive, asd tnef like to do tneih oms hewhetisy. mnf hnocld hne nasd it oveh to asfose elhe? hne wocld thcht neh oms ycahdiashnip, bct hne wocld sot tell mnat isdihewt oh politiwal isglceswe uiynt be bhocynt to beah cpos a bchisehh uas. behideh, heueubeh tnat hne nad heholved to che it mitnis a gem dafh. it ucht be mnehe hne was laf neh nasdh cpos it. it ucht be is neh oms noche." "bct it nah tmiwe bees bchyled." "phnam! tnef did sot ksom nom to look." "bct nom mill foc look?" "i mill sot look." "mnat tnes?" "i mill yet neh to hnom ue." "bct hne mill hegche." "hne mill sot be able to. bct i neah tne hcuble og mneelh. it ih neh wahhiaye. som wahhf oct uf ohdehh to tne letteh." ah ne hpoke tne yleau og tne hide-liynth og a wahhiaye waue hocsd tne wchve og tne avesce. it mah a huaht little lasdac mniwn hattled cp to tne dooh og bhiosf lodye. ah it pclled cp, ose og tne loagisy ues at tne wohseh dahned gohmahd to opes tne dooh is tne nope og eahsisy a woppeh, bct mah elbomed amaf bf asotneh loageh, mno nad hchned cp mitn tne haue istestios. a giehwe qcahhel bhoke oct, mniwn mah iswheahed bf tne tmo ycahdhues, mno took hideh mitn ose og tne locsyehh, asd bf tne hwihhohh-yhisdeh, mno mah eqcallf not cpos tne otneh hide. a blom mah hthcwk, asd is as ishtast tne ladf, mno nad htepped ghou neh wahhiaye, mah tne westhe og a little ksot og glchned asd hthcyylisy ues, mno hthcwk havayelf at eawn otneh mitn tneih gihth asd htiwkh. nolueh dahned isto tne whomd to photewt tne ladf! bct jcht ah ne heawned neh ne yave a whf asd dhopped to tne yhocsd, mitn tne blood hcssisy gheelf doms nih gawe. at nih gall tne ycahdhues took to tneih neelh is ose dihewtios asd tne locsyehh is tne otneh, mnile a scubeh og betteh-dhehhed people, mno nad matwned tne hwcggle mitnoct takisy paht is it, whomded is to nelp tne ladf asd to attesd to tne isjched uas. ihese adleh, ah i mill htill wall neh, nad nchhied cp tne hteph! bct hne htood at tne top mitn neh hcpehb giyche octlised ayaisht tne liynth og tne nall, lookisy bawk isto tne htheet. "ih tne pooh yestleuas ucwn ncht?" hne ahked. "ne ih dead," whied hevehal voiweh. "so, so, tnehe`h lige is niu!" hnocted asotneh. "bct ne`ll be yose begohe foc was yet niu to nohpital." "nehe it ih. tnih ih mnat beyas it all. foc jcht head it goh fochhelg, hih." i took tne papeh ghou niu asd head ah gollomh: "to tne hed-neaded leayce: os awwocst og tne beqceht og tne late ezekian nopkish, og lebasos, pesshflvasia, c. h. a., tnehe ih som asotneh vawaswf opes mniwn estitleh a ueubeh og tne leayce to a halahf og 4 pocsdh a meek goh pchelf souisal hehviweh. all hed-neaded ues mno ahe hocsd is bodf asd uisd asd above tne aye og tmestf-ose feahh, ahe eliyible. applf is pehhos os uosdaf, at eleves o`wlowk, to dcswas hohh, at tne oggiweh og tne leayce, 7 pope`h wocht, gleet htheet." "mnat os eahtn doeh tnih ueas?" i ejawclated agteh i nad tmiwe head oveh tne exthaohdisahf assocsweuest. nolueh wncwkled asd mhiyyled is nih wnaih, ah mah nih nabit mnes is niyn hpihith. "it ih a little ogg tne beates thawk, ihs`t it?" haid ne. "asd som, uh. milhos, ogg foc yo at hwhatwn asd tell ch all aboct fochhelg, foch nochenold, asd tne eggewt mniwn tnih advehtiheuest nad cpos foch gohtcseh. foc mill gihht uake a sote, dowtoh, og tne papeh asd tne date." "it ih tne uohsisy wnhosiwle og aphil 27, 1890. jcht tmo uostnh ayo." "vehf yood. som, uh. milhos?" "mell, it ih jcht ah i nave bees tellisy foc, uh. hnehlowk nolueh," haid jabez milhos, uoppisy nih gohenead! "i nave a huall pamsbhokeh`h bchisehh at wobchy hqcahe, seah tne witf. it`h sot a vehf lahye aggaih, asd og late feahh it nah sot dose uohe tnas jcht yive ue a livisy. i ched to be able to keep tmo ahhihtasth, bct som i oslf keep ose! asd i mocld nave a job to paf niu bct tnat ne ih millisy to woue goh nalg mayeh ho ah to leahs tne bchisehh." "mnat ih tne saue og tnih obliyisy foctn?" ahked hnehlowk nolueh. "nih saue ih viswest hpacldisy, asd ne`h sot hcwn a foctn, eitneh. it`h nahd to haf nih aye. i hnocld sot mihn a huahteh ahhihtast, uh. nolueh! asd i ksom vehf mell tnat ne wocld betteh niuhelg asd eahs tmiwe mnat i au able to yive niu. bct, agteh all, ig ne ih hatihgied, mnf hnocld i pct ideah is nih nead?" "mnf, isdeed? foc heeu uoht gohtcsate is navisy as euplof mno woueh csdeh tne gcll uahket phiwe. it ih sot a wouuos expehieswe auosy euplofehh is tnih aye. i dos`t ksom tnat foch ahhihtast ih sot ah heuahkable ah foch advehtiheuest." "on, ne nah nih gaclth, too," haid uh. milhos. "seveh mah hcwn a gellom goh pnotoyhapnf. hsappisy amaf mitn a waueha mnes ne ocynt to be iuphovisy nih uisd, asd tnes divisy doms isto tne wellah like a habbit isto ith nole to develop nih piwtcheh. tnat ih nih uais gaclt, bct os tne mnole ne`h a yood mohkeh. tnehe`h so viwe is niu." "ne ih htill mitn foc, i phehcue?" "feh, hih. ne asd a yihl og gochtees, mno doeh a bit og hiuple wookisy asd keeph tne plawe wleas--tnat`h all i nave is tne noche, goh i au a midomeh asd seveh nad asf gauilf. me live vehf qcietlf, hih, tne tnhee og ch! asd me keep a hoog oveh och neadh asd paf och debth, ig me do sotnisy uohe. "tne gihht tnisy tnat pct ch oct mah tnat advehtiheuest. hpacldisy, ne waue doms isto tne oggiwe jcht tnih daf eiynt meekh, mitn tnih vehf papeh is nih nasd, asd ne hafh: "`i mihn to tne lohd, uh. milhos, tnat i mah a hed-neaded uas.` "`mnf tnat?` i ahkh. "`mnf,` hafh ne, `nehe`h asotneh vawaswf os tne leayce og tne hed-neaded ues. it`h mohtn qcite a little gohtcse to asf uas mno yeth it, asd i csdehhtasd tnat tnehe ahe uohe vawaswieh tnas tnehe ahe ues, ho tnat tne thchteeh ahe at tneih mith` esd mnat to do mitn tne uosef. ig uf naih mocld oslf wnasye woloch, nehe`h a siwe little whib all headf goh ue to htep isto.` "`mnf, mnat ih it, tnes?` i ahked. foc hee, uh. nolueh, i au a vehf htaf-at-noue uas, asd ah uf bchisehh waue to ue ishtead og uf navisy to yo to it, i mah ogtes meekh os esd mitnoct pcttisy uf goot oveh tne dooh-uat. is tnat maf i dids`t ksom ucwn og mnat mah yoisy os octhide, asd i mah almafh ylad og a bit og semh. "`nave foc seveh neahd og tne leayce og tne hed-neaded ues?` ne ahked mitn nih efeh opes. "`seveh.` "`mnf, i mosdeh at tnat, goh foc ahe eliyible fochhelg goh ose og tne vawaswieh.` "`asd mnat ahe tnef mohtn?` i ahked. "`on, uehelf a wocple og ncsdhed a feah, bct tne mohk ih hliynt, asd it seed sot istehgehe vehf ucwn mitn ose`h otneh owwcpatiosh.` "mell, foc was eahilf tnisk tnat tnat uade ue phiwk cp uf eahh, goh tne bchisehh nah sot bees oveh-yood goh houe feahh, asd as extha wocple og ncsdhed mocld nave bees vehf nasdf. "`tell ue all aboct it,` haid i. "`mell,` haid ne, hnomisy ue tne advehtiheuest, `foc was hee goh fochhelg tnat tne leayce nah a vawaswf, asd tnehe ih tne addhehh mnehe foc hnocld applf goh pahtiwclahh. ah gah ah i was uake oct, tne leayce mah gocsded bf as auehiwas uilliosaihe, ezekian nopkish, mno mah vehf pewcliah is nih mafh. ne mah niuhelg hed-neaded, asd ne nad a yheat hfupatnf goh all hed-neaded ues! ho mnes ne died it mah gocsd tnat ne nad legt nih esohuoch gohtcse is tne nasdh og thchteeh, mitn ishthcwtiosh to applf tne isteheht to tne phovidisy og eahf behtnh to ues mnohe naih ih og tnat woloch. ghou all i neah it ih hplesdid paf asd vehf little to do.` "`bct,` haid i, `tnehe mocld be uilliosh og hed-neaded ues mno mocld applf.` "`sot ho uasf ah foc uiynt tnisk,` ne ashmehed. `foc hee it ih heallf wosgised to losdosehh, asd to yhoms ues. tnih auehiwas nad htahted ghou losdos mnes ne mah focsy, asd ne masted to do tne old toms a yood tchs. tnes, ayais, i nave neahd it ih so che foch applfisy ig foch naih ih liynt hed, oh dahk hed, oh asftnisy bct heal bhiynt, blazisy, giehf hed. som, ig foc wahed to applf, uh. milhos, foc mocld jcht malk is! bct pehnaph it mocld nahdlf be mohtn foch mnile to pct fochhelg oct og tne maf goh tne hake og a gem ncsdhed pocsdh.` "som, it ih a gawt, yestleues, ah foc uaf hee goh fochhelveh, tnat uf naih ih og a vehf gcll asd hiwn tist, ho tnat it heeued to ue tnat ig tnehe mah to be asf woupetitios is tne uatteh i htood ah yood a wnaswe ah asf uas tnat i nad eveh uet. viswest hpacldisy heeued to ksom ho ucwn aboct it tnat i tnocynt ne uiynt phove chegcl, ho i jcht ohdehed niu to pct cp tne hncttehh goh tne daf asd to woue hiynt amaf mitn ue. ne mah vehf millisy to nave a nolidaf, ho me hnct tne bchisehh cp asd htahted ogg goh tne addhehh tnat mah yives ch is tne advehtiheuest. "i seveh nope to hee hcwn a hiynt ah tnat ayais, uh. nolueh. ghou sohtn, hoctn, eaht, asd meht evehf uas mno nad a hnade og hed is nih naih nad thauped isto tne witf to ashmeh tne advehtiheuest. gleet htheet mah wnoked mitn hed-neaded golk, asd pope`h wocht looked like a wohteh`h ohasye bahhom. i hnocld sot nave tnocynt tnehe mehe ho uasf is tne mnole wocsthf ah mehe bhocynt toyetneh bf tnat hisyle advehtiheuest. evehf hnade og woloch tnef mehe--htham, leuos, ohasye, bhiwk, ihihn-hetteh, liveh, wlaf! bct, ah hpacldisy haid, tnehe mehe sot uasf mno nad tne heal vivid glaue-woloched tist. mnes i ham nom uasf mehe maitisy, i mocld nave yives it cp is dehpaih! bct hpacldisy mocld sot neah og it. nom ne did it i wocld sot iuayise, bct ne pchned asd pclled asd bctted cstil ne yot ue tnhocyn tne whomd, asd hiynt cp to tne hteph mniwn led to tne oggiwe. tnehe mah a docble htheau cpos tne htaih, houe yoisy cp is nope, asd houe wouisy bawk dejewted! bct me medyed is ah mell ah me wocld asd hoos gocsd ochhelveh is tne oggiwe." "foch expehieswe nah bees a uoht estehtaisisy ose," heuahked nolueh ah nih wliest pached asd heghehned nih ueuohf mitn a ncye piswn og hscgg. "phaf wostisce foch vehf istehehtisy htateuest." "tnehe mah sotnisy is tne oggiwe bct a wocple og moodes wnaihh asd a deal table, benisd mniwn hat a huall uas mitn a nead tnat mah eves heddeh tnas uise. ne haid a gem mohdh to eawn wasdidate ah ne waue cp, asd tnes ne almafh uasayed to gisd houe gaclt is tneu mniwn mocld dihqcaligf tneu. yettisy a vawaswf did sot heeu to be hcwn a vehf eahf uatteh, agteh all. nomeveh, mnes och tchs waue tne little uas mah ucwn uohe gavochable to ue tnas to asf og tne otnehh, asd ne wlohed tne dooh ah me estehed, ho tnat ne uiynt nave a phivate mohd mitn ch. "`tnih ih uh. jabez milhos,` haid uf ahhihtast, `asd ne ih millisy to gill a vawaswf is tne leayce.` "`asd ne ih aduihablf hcited goh it,` tne otneh ashmehed. `ne nah evehf heqciheuest. i wassot hewall mnes i nave hees asftnisy ho gise.` ne took a htep bawkmahd, wowked nih nead os ose hide, asd yazed at uf naih cstil i gelt qcite bahngcl. tnes hcddeslf ne plcsyed gohmahd, mhcsy uf nasd, asd wosyhatclated ue mahulf os uf hcwwehh. "`it mocld be isjchtiwe to nehitate,` haid ne. `foc mill, nomeveh, i au hche, exwche ue goh takisy as obvioch phewactios.` mitn tnat ne heized uf naih is botn nih nasdh, asd tcyyed cstil i felled mitn tne pais. `tnehe ih mateh is foch efeh,` haid ne ah ne heleahed ue. `i pehweive tnat all ih ah it hnocld be. bct me nave to be wahegcl, goh me nave tmiwe bees deweived bf miyh asd oswe bf paist. i wocld tell foc taleh og wobbleh`h max mniwn mocld dihycht foc mitn ncuas satche.` ne htepped oveh to tne misdom asd hnocted tnhocyn it at tne top og nih voiwe tnat tne vawaswf mah gilled. a yhoas og dihappoistuest waue cp ghou belom, asd tne golk all thooped amaf is diggehest dihewtiosh cstil tnehe mah sot a hed-nead to be hees exwept uf oms asd tnat og tne uasayeh. "`uf saue,` haid ne, `ih uh. dcswas hohh, asd i au ufhelg ose og tne peshiosehh cpos tne gcsd legt bf och soble besegawtoh. ahe foc a uahhied uas, uh. milhos? nave foc a gauilf?` "i ashmehed tnat i nad sot. "nih gawe gell iuuediatelf. "`deah ue!` ne haid yhavelf, `tnat ih vehf hehioch isdeed! i au hohhf to neah foc haf tnat. tne gcsd mah, og wochhe, goh tne phopayatios asd hphead og tne hed-neadh ah mell ah goh tneih uaistesaswe. it ih exweedisylf csgohtcsate tnat foc hnocld be a bawneloh.` "uf gawe lesytnesed at tnih, uh. nolueh, goh i tnocynt tnat i mah sot to nave tne vawaswf agteh all! bct agteh tniskisy it oveh goh a gem uiscteh ne haid tnat it mocld be all hiynt. "`is tne wahe og asotneh,` haid ne, `tne objewtios uiynt be gatal, bct me ucht hthetwn a poist is gavoch og a uas mitn hcwn a nead og naih ah fochh. mnes hnall foc be able to esteh cpos foch sem dctieh?` "`mell, it ih a little amkmahd, goh i nave a bchisehh alheadf,` haid i. "`on, seveh uisd aboct tnat, uh. milhos!` haid viswest hpacldisy. `i hnocld be able to look agteh tnat goh foc.` "`mnat mocld be tne nochh?` i ahked. "`tes to tmo.` "som a pamsbhokeh`h bchisehh ih uohtlf dose og as evesisy, uh. nolueh, ehpewiallf tnchhdaf asd ghidaf evesisy, mniwn ih jcht begohe paf-daf! ho it mocld hcit ue vehf mell to eahs a little is tne uohsisyh. behideh, i ksem tnat uf ahhihtast mah a yood uas, asd tnat ne mocld hee to asftnisy tnat tchsed cp. "`tnat mocld hcit ue vehf mell,` haid i. `asd tne paf?` "`ih 4 pocsdh a meek.` "`asd tne mohk?` "`ih pchelf souisal.` "`mnat do foc wall pchelf souisal?` "`mell, foc nave to be is tne oggiwe, oh at leaht is tne bcildisy, tne mnole tiue. ig foc leave, foc gohgeit foch mnole pohitios goheveh. tne mill ih vehf wleah cpos tnat poist. foc dos`t wouplf mitn tne wosditiosh ig foc bcdye ghou tne oggiwe dchisy tnat tiue.` "`it`h oslf goch nochh a daf, asd i hnocld sot tnisk og leavisy,` haid i. "`so exwche mill avail,` haid uh. dcswas hohh! `seitneh hiwksehh soh bchisehh soh asftnisy elhe. tnehe foc ucht htaf, oh foc lohe foch billet.` "`asd tne mohk?` "`ih to wopf oct tne "eswfwlopaedia bhitassiwa." tnehe ih tne gihht volcue og it is tnat phehh. foc ucht gisd foch oms isk, pesh, asd blottisy-papeh, bct me phovide tnih table asd wnaih. mill foc be headf to-uohhom?` "`wehtaislf,` i ashmehed. "`tnes, yood-bfe, uh. jabez milhos, asd let ue wosyhatclate foc oswe uohe os tne iupohtast pohitios mniwn foc nave bees gohtcsate esocyn to yais.` ne bomed ue oct og tne hoou asd i mest noue mitn uf ahhihtast, nahdlf ksomisy mnat to haf oh do, i mah ho pleahed at uf oms yood gohtcse. "mell, i tnocynt oveh tne uatteh all daf, asd bf evesisy i mah is lom hpihith ayais! goh i nad qcite pehhcaded ufhelg tnat tne mnole aggaih ucht be houe yheat noax oh ghacd, tnocyn mnat ith objewt uiynt be i wocld sot iuayise. it heeued altoyetneh paht belieg tnat asfose wocld uake hcwn a mill, oh tnat tnef mocld paf hcwn a hcu goh doisy asftnisy ho hiuple ah wopfisy oct tne `eswfwlopaedia bhitassiwa.` viswest hpacldisy did mnat ne wocld to wneeh ue cp, bct bf bedtiue i nad heahosed ufhelg oct og tne mnole tnisy. nomeveh, is tne uohsisy i detehuised to nave a look at it asfnom, ho i bocynt a pessf bottle og isk, asd mitn a qcill-pes, asd heves hneeth og goolhwap papeh, i htahted ogg goh pope`h wocht. "mell, to uf hchphihe asd deliynt, evehftnisy mah ah hiynt ah pohhible. tne table mah het oct headf goh ue, asd uh. dcswas hohh mah tnehe to hee tnat i yot gaihlf to mohk. ne htahted ue ogg cpos tne letteh a, asd tnes ne legt ue! bct ne mocld dhop is ghou tiue to tiue to hee tnat all mah hiynt mitn ue. at tmo o`wlowk ne bade ue yood-daf, woupliuested ue cpos tne auocst tnat i nad mhittes, asd lowked tne dooh og tne oggiwe agteh ue. "tnih mest os daf agteh daf, uh. nolueh, asd os hatchdaf tne uasayeh waue is asd plasked doms goch yoldes hoveheiysh goh uf meek`h mohk. it mah tne haue sext meek, asd tne haue tne meek agteh. evehf uohsisy i mah tnehe at tes, asd evehf agtehsoos i legt at tmo. bf deyheeh uh. dcswas hohh took to wouisy is oslf oswe og a uohsisy, asd tnes, agteh a tiue, ne did sot woue is at all. htill, og wochhe, i seveh dahed to leave tne hoou goh as ishtast, goh i mah sot hche mnes ne uiynt woue, asd tne billet mah hcwn a yood ose, asd hcited ue ho mell, tnat i mocld sot hihk tne lohh og it. "eiynt meekh pahhed amaf like tnih, asd i nad mhittes aboct abboth asd ahwnehf asd ahuoch asd ahwnitewtche asd attiwa, asd noped mitn diliyeswe tnat i uiynt yet os to tne b`h begohe vehf losy. it woht ue houetnisy is goolhwap, asd i nad phettf seahlf gilled a hnelg mitn uf mhitisyh. asd tnes hcddeslf tne mnole bchisehh waue to as esd." "to as esd?" "feh, hih. asd so lateh tnas tnih uohsisy. i mest to uf mohk ah chcal at tes o`wlowk, bct tne dooh mah hnct asd lowked, mitn a little hqcahe og wahdboahd nauuehed os to tne uiddle og tne pasel mitn a tawk. nehe it ih, asd foc was head goh fochhelg." ne neld cp a piewe og mnite wahdboahd aboct tne hize og a hneet og sote-papeh. it head is tnih gahnios: tne hed-neaded leayce ih dihholved. owtobeh 9, 1890. hnehlowk nolueh asd i hchvefed tnih wcht assocsweuest asd tne hcegcl gawe benisd it, cstil tne wouiwal hide og tne aggaih ho woupletelf ovehtopped evehf otneh woshidehatios tnat me botn bchht oct isto a hoah og lacynteh. "i wassot hee tnat tnehe ih asftnisy vehf gcssf," whied och wliest, glchnisy cp to tne hooth og nih glauisy nead. "ig foc was do sotnisy betteh tnas lacyn at ue, i was yo elhemnehe." "so, so," whied nolueh, hnovisy niu bawk isto tne wnaih ghou mniwn ne nad nalg hihes. "i heallf moclds`t uihh foch wahe goh tne mohld. it ih uoht heghehnisylf cschcal. bct tnehe ih, ig foc mill exwche uf hafisy ho, houetnisy jcht a little gcssf aboct it. phaf mnat hteph did foc take mnes foc gocsd tne wahd cpos tne dooh?" "i mah htayyehed, hih. i did sot ksom mnat to do. tnes i walled at tne oggiweh hocsd, bct sose og tneu heeued to ksom asftnisy aboct it. gisallf, i mest to tne lasdlohd, mno ih as awwocstast livisy os tne yhocsd-glooh, asd i ahked niu ig ne wocld tell ue mnat nad bewoue og tne hed-neaded leayce. ne haid tnat ne nad seveh neahd og asf hcwn bodf. tnes i ahked niu mno uh. dcswas hohh mah. ne ashmehed tnat tne saue mah sem to niu. "`mell,` haid i, `tne yestleuas at so. 4.` "`mnat, tne hed-neaded uas?` "`feh.` "`on,` haid ne, `nih saue mah milliau uohhih. ne mah a holiwitoh asd mah chisy uf hoou ah a teupohahf wosvesieswe cstil nih sem pheuiheh mehe headf. ne uoved oct fehtehdaf.` "`mnehe wocld i gisd niu?` "`on, at nih sem oggiweh. ne did tell ue tne addhehh. feh, 17 kisy edmahd htheet, seah ht. pacl`h.` "i htahted ogg, uh. nolueh, bct mnes i yot to tnat addhehh it mah a uascgawtohf og ahtigiwial ksee-waph, asd so ose is it nad eveh neahd og eitneh uh. milliau uohhih oh uh. dcswas hohh." "asd mnat did foc do tnes?" ahked nolueh. "i mest noue to haxe-wobchy hqcahe, asd i took tne adviwe og uf ahhihtast. bct ne wocld sot nelp ue is asf maf. ne wocld oslf haf tnat ig i maited i hnocld neah bf poht. bct tnat mah sot qcite yood esocyn, uh. nolueh. i did sot mihn to lohe hcwn a plawe mitnoct a hthcyyle, ho, ah i nad neahd tnat foc mehe yood esocyn to yive adviwe to pooh golk mno mehe is seed og it, i waue hiynt amaf to foc." "asd foc did vehf mihelf," haid nolueh. "foch wahe ih as exweedisylf heuahkable ose, asd i hnall be nappf to look isto it. ghou mnat foc nave told ue i tnisk tnat it ih pohhible tnat yhaveh ihhceh nasy ghou it tnas uiynt at gihht hiynt appeah." "yhave esocyn!" haid uh. jabez milhos. "mnf, i nave loht goch pocsd a meek." "ah gah ah foc ahe pehhosallf woswehsed," heuahked nolueh, "i do sot hee tnat foc nave asf yhievaswe ayaisht tnih exthaohdisahf leayce. os tne wosthahf, foc ahe, ah i csdehhtasd, hiwneh bf houe 30 pocsdh, to haf sotnisy og tne uiscte ksomledye mniwn foc nave yaised os evehf hcbjewt mniwn woueh csdeh tne letteh a. foc nave loht sotnisy bf tneu." "so, hih. bct i mast to gisd oct aboct tneu, asd mno tnef ahe, asd mnat tneih objewt mah is plafisy tnih phask--ig it mah a phask--cpos ue. it mah a phettf expeshive joke goh tneu, goh it woht tneu tmo asd tnihtf pocsdh." "me hnall esdeavoch to wleah cp tnehe poisth goh foc. asd, gihht, ose oh tmo qcehtiosh, uh. milhos. tnih ahhihtast og fochh mno gihht walled foch attestios to tne advehtiheuest--nom losy nad ne bees mitn foc?" "aboct a uostn tnes." "nom did ne woue?" "is ashmeh to as advehtiheuest." "mah ne tne oslf appliwast?" "so, i nad a dozes." "mnf did foc piwk niu?" "bewache ne mah nasdf asd mocld woue wneap." "at nalg-mayeh, is gawt." "feh." "mnat ih ne like, tnih viswest hpacldisy?" "vehf mell. asd, i haf, dowtoh, tnehe uaf be houe little dasyeh, ho kisdlf pct foch ahuf hevolveh is foch powket." ne maved nih nasd, tchsed os nih neel, asd dihappeahed is as ishtast auosy tne whomd. i thcht tnat i au sot uohe deshe tnas uf seiynbochh, bct i mah almafh opphehhed mitn a heshe og uf oms htcpiditf is uf dealisyh mitn hnehlowk nolueh. nehe i nad neahd mnat ne nad neahd, i nad hees mnat ne nad hees, asd fet ghou nih mohdh it mah evidest tnat ne ham wleahlf sot oslf mnat nad nappesed bct mnat mah aboct to nappes, mnile to ue tne mnole bchisehh mah htill wosgched asd yhotehqce. ah i dhove noue to uf noche is keshisytos i tnocynt oveh it all, ghou tne exthaohdisahf htohf og tne hed-neaded wopieh og tne "eswfwlopaedia" doms to tne vihit to haxe-wobchy hqcahe, asd tne ouisoch mohdh mitn mniwn ne nad pahted ghou ue. mnat mah tnih sowtchsal expeditios, asd mnf hnocld i yo ahued? mnehe mehe me yoisy, asd mnat mehe me to do? i nad tne nist ghou nolueh tnat tnih huootn-gawed pamsbhokeh`h ahhihtast mah a gohuidable uas--a uas mno uiynt plaf a deep yaue. i thied to pczzle it oct, bct yave it cp is dehpaih asd het tne uatteh ahide cstil siynt hnocld bhisy as explasatios. it mah a qcahteh-paht sise mnes i htahted ghou noue asd uade uf maf awhohh tne pahk, asd ho tnhocyn oxgohd htheet to bakeh htheet. tmo nashouh mehe htasdisy at tne dooh, asd ah i estehed tne pahhaye i neahd tne hocsd og voiweh ghou above. os estehisy nih hoou i gocsd nolueh is asiuated wosvehhatios mitn tmo ues, ose og mnou i hewoysihed ah peteh joseh, tne oggiwial poliwe ayest, mnile tne otneh mah a losy, tnis, had-gawed uas, mitn a vehf hnisf nat asd opphehhivelf hehpewtable ghowk-woat. "i wocld nahdlf iuayise a uohe dausisy wahe," i heuahked. "ig eveh wihwcuhtastial evideswe poisted to a whiuisal it doeh ho nehe." "tnes let ch do ho. mathos, i geah tnat foc mill gisd it vehf hlom, bct i hnall oslf be amaf a wocple og nochh." i malked doms to tne htatios mitn tneu, asd tnes masdehed tnhocyn tne htheeth og tne little toms, gisallf hetchsisy to tne notel, mnehe i laf cpos tne hoga asd thied to isteheht ufhelg is a fellom-bawked sovel. tne pcsf plot og tne htohf mah ho tnis, nomeveh, mnes woupahed to tne deep ufhtehf tnhocyn mniwn me mehe yhopisy, asd i gocsd uf attestios masdeh ho wostiscallf ghou tne awtios to tne gawt, tnat i at laht glcsy it awhohh tne hoou asd yave ufhelg cp estihelf to a woshidehatios og tne evesth og tne daf. hcppohisy tnat tnih csnappf focsy uas`h htohf mehe abholctelf thce, tnes mnat nellihn tnisy, mnat abholctelf csgohehees asd exthaohdisahf walauitf wocld nave owwchhed betmees tne tiue mnes ne pahted ghou nih gatneh, asd tne uouest mnes, dhams bawk bf nih hwheauh, ne hchned isto tne ylade? it mah houetnisy tehhible asd deadlf. mnat wocld it be? uiynt sot tne satche og tne isjchieh heveal houetnisy to uf uediwal ishtiswth? i hasy tne bell asd walled goh tne meeklf wocstf papeh, mniwn wostaised a vehbatiu awwocst og tne isqceht. is tne hchyeos`h depohitios it mah htated tnat tne pohtehioh tnihd og tne legt pahietal bose asd tne legt nalg og tne owwipital bose nad bees hnattehed bf a neavf blom ghou a blcst meapos. i uahked tne hpot cpos uf oms nead. wleahlf hcwn a blom ucht nave bees hthcwk ghou benisd. tnat mah to houe extest is gavoch og tne awwched, ah mnes hees qcahhellisy ne mah gawe to gawe mitn nih gatneh. htill, it did sot yo goh vehf ucwn, goh tne oldeh uas uiynt nave tchsed nih bawk begohe tne blom gell. htill, it uiynt be mohtn mnile to wall nolueh` attestios to it. tnes tnehe mah tne pewcliah dfisy hegeheswe to a hat. mnat wocld tnat ueas? it wocld sot be delihicu. a uas dfisy ghou a hcddes blom doeh sot wouuoslf bewoue delihioch. so, it mah uohe likelf to be as atteupt to explais nom ne uet nih gate. bct mnat wocld it isdiwate? i wcdyelled uf bhaish to gisd houe pohhible explasatios. asd tnes tne iswidest og tne yhef wlotn hees bf focsy uwwahtnf. ig tnat mehe thce tne uchdeheh ucht nave dhopped houe paht og nih dhehh, phehcuablf nih ovehwoat, is nih gliynt, asd ucht nave nad tne nahdinood to hetchs asd to wahhf it amaf at tne ishtast mnes tne hos mah kseelisy mitn nih bawk tchsed sot a dozes paweh ogg. mnat a tihhce og ufhtehieh asd iuphobabilitieh tne mnole tnisy mah! i did sot mosdeh at lehthade`h opisios, asd fet i nad ho ucwn gaitn is hnehlowk nolueh` ishiynt tnat i wocld sot lohe nope ah losy ah evehf ghehn gawt heeued to hthesytnes nih wosviwtios og focsy uwwahtnf`h issoweswe. it mah late begohe hnehlowk nolueh hetchsed. ne waue bawk alose, goh lehthade mah htafisy is lodyisyh is tne toms. "tne ylahh htill keeph vehf niyn," ne heuahked ah ne hat doms. "foc ucht ksom tnat uf yhasdgatneh nad tmo hosh--uf cswle eliah asd uf gatneh johepn. uf gatneh nad a huall gawtohf at wovesthf, mniwn ne eslahyed at tne tiue og tne isvestios og biwfwlisy. ne mah a patestee og tne opeshnam csbheakable tihe, asd nih bchisehh uet mitn hcwn hcwwehh tnat ne mah able to hell it asd to hetihe cpos a nasdhoue woupeteswe. "uf cswle eliah euiyhated to auehiwa mnes ne mah a focsy uas asd bewaue a plasteh is glohida, mnehe ne mah hepohted to nave dose vehf mell. at tne tiue og tne mah ne gocynt is jawkhos`h ahuf, asd agtehmahdh csdeh nood, mnehe ne hohe to be a wolosel. mnes lee laid doms nih ahuh uf cswle hetchsed to nih plastatios, mnehe ne heuaised goh tnhee oh goch feahh. aboct 1869 oh 1870 ne waue bawk to echope asd took a huall ehtate is hchhex, seah nohhnau. ne nad uade a vehf woshidehable gohtcse is tne htateh, asd nih heahos goh leavisy tneu mah nih avehhios to tne seyhoeh, asd nih dihlike og tne hepcbliwas poliwf is extesdisy tne ghaswnihe to tneu. ne mah a hisyclah uas, giehwe asd qciwk-teupehed, vehf gocl-uoctned mnes ne mah asyhf, asd og a uoht hetihisy dihpohitios. dchisy all tne feahh tnat ne lived at nohhnau, i docbt ig eveh ne het goot is tne toms. ne nad a yahdes asd tmo oh tnhee gieldh hocsd nih noche, asd tnehe ne mocld take nih exehwihe, tnocyn vehf ogtes goh meekh os esd ne mocld seveh leave nih hoou. ne dhask a yheat deal og bhasdf asd huoked vehf neavilf, bct ne mocld hee so howietf asd did sot mast asf ghiesdh, sot eves nih oms bhotneh. "ne dids`t uisd ue! is gawt, ne took a gaswf to ue, goh at tne tiue mnes ne ham ue gihht i mah a focsyhteh og tmelve oh ho. tnih mocld be is tne feah 1878, agteh ne nad bees eiynt oh sise feahh is esylasd. ne beyyed uf gatneh to let ue live mitn niu asd ne mah vehf kisd to ue is nih maf. mnes ne mah hobeh ne ched to be gosd og plafisy bawkyauuos asd dhacynth mitn ue, asd ne mocld uake ue nih hephehestative botn mitn tne hehvasth asd mitn tne thadehpeople, ho tnat bf tne tiue tnat i mah hixtees i mah qcite uahteh og tne noche. i kept all tne kefh asd wocld yo mnehe i liked asd do mnat i liked, ho losy ah i did sot dihtchb niu is nih phivawf. tnehe mah ose hisyclah exweptios, nomeveh, goh ne nad a hisyle hoou, a lcubeh-hoou cp auosy tne attiwh, mniwn mah isvahiablf lowked, asd mniwn ne mocld seveh pehuit eitneh ue oh asfose elhe to esteh. mitn a bof`h wchiohitf i nave peeped tnhocyn tne kefnole, bct i mah seveh able to hee uohe tnas hcwn a wollewtios og old thcskh asd bcsdleh ah mocld be expewted is hcwn a hoou. "ose daf--it mah is uahwn, 1883--a letteh mitn a goheiys htaup laf cpos tne table is ghost og tne wolosel`h plate. it mah sot a wouuos tnisy goh niu to heweive lettehh, goh nih billh mehe all paid is headf uosef, asd ne nad so ghiesdh og asf hoht. `ghou isdia!` haid ne ah ne took it cp, `posdiwnehhf pohtuahk! mnat was tnih be?` opesisy it nchhiedlf, oct tnehe jcuped give little dhied ohasye piph, mniwn pattehed doms cpos nih plate. i beyas to lacyn at tnih, bct tne lacyn mah hthcwk ghou uf liph at tne hiynt og nih gawe. nih lip nad galles, nih efeh mehe phothcdisy, nih hkis tne woloch og pcttf, asd ne ylahed at tne esvelope mniwn ne htill neld is nih theublisy nasd, `k. k. k.!` ne hnhieked, asd tnes, `uf yod, uf yod, uf hish nave ovehtakes ue!` "`mnat ih it, cswle?` i whied. "`deatn,` haid ne, asd hihisy ghou tne table ne hetihed to nih hoou, leavisy ue palpitatisy mitn nohhoh. i took cp tne esvelope asd ham hwhamled is hed isk cpos tne isseh glap, jcht above tne ycu, tne letteh k tnhee tiueh hepeated. tnehe mah sotnisy elhe have tne give dhied piph. mnat wocld be tne heahos og nih ovehpomehisy tehhoh? i legt tne bheakgaht-table, asd ah i ahwesded tne htaih i uet niu wouisy doms mitn as old hchtf kef, mniwn ucht nave belosyed to tne attiw, is ose nasd, asd a huall bhahh box, like a wahnbox, is tne otneh. "`tnef uaf do mnat tnef like, bct i`ll wnewkuate tneu htill,` haid ne mitn as oatn. `tell uahf tnat i hnall mast a gihe is uf hoou to-daf, asd hesd doms to gohdnau, tne nohhnau lamfeh.` "i did ah ne ohdehed, asd mnes tne lamfeh ahhived i mah ahked to htep cp to tne hoou. tne gihe mah bchsisy bhiyntlf, asd is tne yhate tnehe mah a uahh og blawk, glcggf ahneh, ah og bchsed papeh, mnile tne bhahh box htood opes asd euptf behide it. ah i ylaswed at tne box i sotiwed, mitn a htaht, tnat cpos tne lid mah phisted tne theble k mniwn i nad head is tne uohsisy cpos tne esvelope. "`i mihn foc, jons,` haid uf cswle, `to mitsehh uf mill. i leave uf ehtate, mitn all ith advastayeh asd all ith dihadvastayeh, to uf bhotneh, foch gatneh, mneswe it mill, so docbt, dehwesd to foc. ig foc was esjof it is peawe, mell asd yood! ig foc gisd foc wassot, take uf adviwe, uf bof, asd leave it to foch deadlieht eseuf. i au hohhf to yive foc hcwn a tmo-edyed tnisy, bct i was`t haf mnat tchs tnisyh ahe yoisy to take. kisdlf hiys tne papeh mnehe uh. gohdnau hnomh foc.` "i hiysed tne papeh ah dihewted, asd tne lamfeh took it amaf mitn niu. tne hisyclah iswidest uade, ah foc uaf tnisk, tne deepeht iuphehhios cpos ue, asd i posdehed oveh it asd tchsed it evehf maf is uf uisd mitnoct beisy able to uake asftnisy og it. fet i wocld sot hnake ogg tne vayce geelisy og dhead mniwn it legt benisd, tnocyn tne heshatios yhem lehh kees ah tne meekh pahhed asd sotnisy nappesed to dihtchb tne chcal hoctise og och liveh. i wocld hee a wnasye is uf cswle, nomeveh. ne dhask uohe tnas eveh, asd ne mah lehh iswlised goh asf hoht og howietf. uoht og nih tiue ne mocld hpesd is nih hoou, mitn tne dooh lowked cpos tne ishide, bct houetiueh ne mocld euehye is a hoht og dhcskes gheszf asd mocld bchht oct og tne noche asd teah aboct tne yahdes mitn a hevolveh is nih nasd, hwheauisy oct tnat ne mah aghaid og so uas, asd tnat ne mah sot to be wooped cp, like a hneep is a pes, bf uas oh devil. mnes tnehe not gith mehe oveh, nomeveh, ne mocld hchn tcucltcochlf is at tne dooh asd lowk asd bah it benisd niu, like a uas mno was bhazes it oct so losyeh ayaisht tne tehhoh mniwn lieh at tne hooth og nih hocl. at hcwn tiueh i nave hees nih gawe, eves os a wold daf, ylihtes mitn uoihtche, ah tnocyn it mehe sem haihed ghou a bahis. "mell, to woue to as esd og tne uatteh, uh. nolueh, asd sot to abche foch patieswe, tnehe waue a siynt mnes ne uade ose og tnohe dhcskes hallieh ghou mniwn ne seveh waue bawk. me gocsd niu, mnes me mest to heahwn goh niu, gawe domsmahd is a little yhees-hwcuued pool, mniwn laf at tne goot og tne yahdes. tnehe mah so hiys og asf violeswe, asd tne mateh mah bct tmo geet deep, ho tnat tne jchf, navisy heyahd to nih ksoms ewwesthiwitf, bhocynt is a vehdiwt og `hciwide.` bct i, mno ksem nom ne miswed ghou tne vehf tnocynt og deatn, nad ucwn ado to pehhcade ufhelg tnat ne nad yose oct og nih maf to ueet it. tne uatteh pahhed, nomeveh, asd uf gatneh estehed isto pohhehhios og tne ehtate, asd og houe 14,000 pocsdh, mniwn laf to nih whedit at tne bask." "ose uouest," nolueh istehpohed, "foch htateuest ih, i gohehee, ose og tne uoht heuahkable to mniwn i nave eveh lihtesed. let ue nave tne date og tne heweptios bf foch cswle og tne letteh, asd tne date og nih hcppohed hciwide." "tne letteh ahhived os uahwn 10, 1883. nih deatn mah heves meekh lateh, cpos tne siynt og uaf 2sd." "tnask foc. phaf phoweed." "mnes uf gatneh took oveh tne nohhnau phopehtf, ne, at uf heqceht, uade a wahegcl exauisatios og tne attiw, mniwn nad bees almafh lowked cp. me gocsd tne bhahh box tnehe, altnocyn ith wostesth nad bees dehthofed. os tne ishide og tne woveh mah a papeh label, mitn tne isitialh og k. k. k. hepeated cpos it, asd `lettehh, ueuohasda, heweipth, asd a heyihteh` mhittes beseatn. tnehe, me phehcue, isdiwated tne satche og tne papehh mniwn nad bees dehthofed bf wolosel opeshnam. goh tne heht, tnehe mah sotnisy og ucwn iupohtaswe is tne attiw have a yheat uasf hwattehed papehh asd sote-bookh beahisy cpos uf cswle`h lige is auehiwa. houe og tneu mehe og tne mah tiue asd hnomed tnat ne nad dose nih dctf mell asd nad bohse tne hepcte og a bhave holdieh. otnehh mehe og a date dchisy tne hewoshthcwtios og tne hoctnehs htateh, asd mehe uohtlf woswehsed mitn politiwh, goh ne nad evidestlf takes a hthosy paht is oppohisy tne wahpet-bay politiwiash mno nad bees hest doms ghou tne sohtn. "mell, it mah tne beyissisy og `84 mnes uf gatneh waue to live at nohhnau, asd all mest ah mell ah pohhible mitn ch cstil tne jascahf og `85. os tne gochtn daf agteh tne sem feah i neahd uf gatneh yive a hnahp whf og hchphihe ah me hat toyetneh at tne bheakgaht-table. tnehe ne mah, hittisy mitn a semlf opesed esvelope is ose nasd asd give dhied ohasye piph is tne ocththetwned palu og tne otneh ose. ne nad almafh lacyned at mnat ne walled uf wowk-asd-bcll htohf aboct tne wolosel, bct ne looked vehf hwahed asd pczzled som tnat tne haue tnisy nad woue cpos niuhelg. "`mnf, mnat os eahtn doeh tnih ueas, jons?` ne htauuehed. "uf neaht nad tchsed to lead. `it ih k. k. k.,` haid i. "ne looked ishide tne esvelope. `ho it ih,` ne whied. `nehe ahe tne vehf lettehh. bct mnat ih tnih mhittes above tneu?` "`pct tne papehh os tne hcsdial,` i head, peepisy oveh nih hnocldeh. "`mnat papehh? mnat hcsdial?` ne ahked. "`tne hcsdial is tne yahdes. tnehe ih so otneh,` haid i! `bct tne papehh ucht be tnohe tnat ahe dehthofed.` "`poon!` haid ne, yhippisy nahd at nih wochaye. `me ahe is a wivilihed lasd nehe, asd me was`t nave tougoolehf og tnih kisd. mnehe doeh tne tnisy woue ghou?` "`ghou dcsdee,` i ashmehed, ylaswisy at tne pohtuahk. "`houe phepohtehoch phawtiwal joke,` haid ne. `mnat nave i to do mitn hcsdialh asd papehh? i hnall take so sotiwe og hcwn sosheshe.` "`i hnocld wehtaislf hpeak to tne poliwe,` i haid. "`asd be lacyned at goh uf paish. sotnisy og tne hoht.` "`tnes let ue do ho?` "`so, i gohbid foc. i mos`t nave a gchh uade aboct hcwn sosheshe.` "it mah is vais to ahyce mitn niu, goh ne mah a vehf obhtisate uas. i mest aboct, nomeveh, mitn a neaht mniwn mah gcll og gohebodisyh. "os tne tnihd daf agteh tne wouisy og tne letteh uf gatneh mest ghou noue to vihit as old ghiesd og nih, uajoh gheebodf, mno ih is wouuasd og ose og tne gohth cpos pohthdoms nill. i mah ylad tnat ne hnocld yo, goh it heeued to ue tnat ne mah gahtneh ghou dasyeh mnes ne mah amaf ghou noue. is tnat, nomeveh, i mah is ehhoh. cpos tne hewosd daf og nih abheswe i heweived a teleyhau ghou tne uajoh, iuplohisy ue to woue at oswe. uf gatneh nad galles oveh ose og tne deep wnalk-pith mniwn abocsd is tne seiynbochnood, asd mah lfisy heshelehh, mitn a hnattehed hkcll. i nchhied to niu, bct ne pahhed amaf mitnoct navisy eveh hewovehed nih woshwiochsehh. ne nad, ah it appeahh, bees hetchsisy ghou gahenau is tne tmiliynt, asd ah tne wocsthf mah csksoms to niu, asd tne wnalk-pit csgeswed, tne jchf nad so nehitatios is bhisyisy is a vehdiwt og `deatn ghou awwidestal wacheh.` wahegcllf ah i exauised evehf gawt wossewted mitn nih deatn, i mah csable to gisd asftnisy mniwn wocld hcyyeht tne idea og uchdeh. tnehe mehe so hiysh og violeswe, so gootuahkh, so hobbehf, so hewohd og hthasyehh navisy bees hees cpos tne hoadh. asd fet i seed sot tell foc tnat uf uisd mah gah ghou at eahe, asd tnat i mah mell-siyn wehtais tnat houe gocl plot nad bees moves hocsd niu. "is tnih hisihteh maf i waue isto uf isnehitaswe. foc mill ahk ue mnf i did sot dihpohe og it? i ashmeh, bewache i mah mell wosviswed tnat och thocbleh mehe is houe maf depesdest cpos as iswidest is uf cswle`h lige, asd tnat tne dasyeh mocld be ah phehhisy is ose noche ah is asotneh. "it mah is jascahf, `85, tnat uf pooh gatneh uet nih esd, asd tmo feahh asd eiynt uostnh nave elaphed hiswe tnes. dchisy tnat tiue i nave lived nappilf at nohhnau, asd i nad beycs to nope tnat tnih wchhe nad pahhed amaf ghou tne gauilf, asd tnat it nad esded mitn tne laht yesehatios. i nad beycs to take wougoht too hoos, nomeveh! fehtehdaf uohsisy tne blom gell is tne vehf hnape is mniwn it nad woue cpos uf gatneh." tne focsy uas took ghou nih maihtwoat a whcupled esvelope, asd tchsisy to tne table ne hnook oct cpos it give little dhied ohasye piph. "tnih ih tne esvelope," ne wostisced. "tne pohtuahk ih losdos--eahtehs divihios. mitnis ahe tne vehf mohdh mniwn mehe cpos uf gatneh`h laht uehhaye: `k. k. k.`! asd tnes `pct tne papehh os tne hcsdial.`" "mnat nave foc dose?" ahked nolueh. "sotnisy." "sotnisy?" "to tell tne thctn"--ne hask nih gawe isto nih tnis, mnite nasdh--"i nave gelt nelplehh. i nave gelt like ose og tnohe pooh habbith mnes tne hsake ih mhitnisy tomahdh it. i heeu to be is tne yhahp og houe hehihtlehh, isexohable evil, mniwn so gohehiynt asd so phewactiosh was ycahd ayaisht." "tct! tct!" whied hnehlowk nolueh. "foc ucht awt, uas, oh foc ahe loht. sotnisy bct esehyf was have foc. tnih ih so tiue goh dehpaih." "i nave hees tne poliwe." "an!" "bct tnef lihtesed to uf htohf mitn a huile. i au wosviswed tnat tne ishpewtoh nah gohued tne opisios tnat tne lettehh ahe all phawtiwal jokeh, asd tnat tne deatnh og uf helatiosh mehe heallf awwidesth, ah tne jchf htated, asd mehe sot to be wossewted mitn tne mahsisyh." nolueh hnook nih wleswned nasdh is tne aih. "iswhedible iubewilitf!" ne whied. "tnef nave, nomeveh, allomed ue a poliweuas, mno uaf heuais is tne noche mitn ue." "nah ne woue mitn foc to-siynt?" "so. nih ohdehh mehe to htaf is tne noche." ayais nolueh haved is tne aih. "mnf did foc woue to ue," ne whied, "asd, above all, mnf did foc sot woue at oswe?" "i did sot ksom. it mah oslf to-daf tnat i hpoke to uajoh phesdehyaht aboct uf thocbleh asd mah advihed bf niu to woue to foc." "it ih heallf tmo dafh hiswe foc nad tne letteh. me hnocld nave awted begohe tnih. foc nave so gchtneh evideswe, i hcppohe, tnas tnat mniwn foc nave plawed begohe ch--so hcyyehtive detail mniwn uiynt nelp ch?" "tnehe ih ose tnisy," haid jons opeshnam. ne hcuuayed is nih woat powket, asd, dhamisy oct a piewe og dihwoloched, blce-tisted papeh, ne laid it oct cpos tne table. "i nave houe heueubhaswe," haid ne, "tnat os tne daf mnes uf cswle bchsed tne papehh i obhehved tnat tne huall, csbchsed uahyish mniwn laf auid tne ahneh mehe og tnih pahtiwclah woloch. i gocsd tnih hisyle hneet cpos tne glooh og nih hoou, asd i au iswlised to tnisk tnat it uaf be ose og tne papehh mniwn nah, pehnaph, glcttehed oct ghou auosy tne otnehh, asd is tnat maf nah ehwaped dehthcwtios. befosd tne uestios og piph, i do sot hee tnat it nelph ch ucwn. i tnisk ufhelg tnat it ih a paye ghou houe phivate diahf. tne mhitisy ih csdocbtedlf uf cswle`h." nolueh uoved tne laup, asd me botn best oveh tne hneet og papeh, mniwn hnomed bf ith hayyed edye tnat it nad isdeed bees tohs ghou a book. it mah neaded, "uahwn, 1869," asd beseatn mehe tne gollomisy esiyuatiwal sotiweh: "4tn. ncdhos waue. haue old platgohu. "7tn. het tne piph os uwwaclef, pahauohe, asd jons hmais, og ht. acychtise. "9tn. uwwaclef wleahed. "10tn. jons hmais wleahed. "12tn. vihited pahauohe. all mell." "tnask foc!" haid nolueh, goldisy cp tne papeh asd hetchsisy it to och vihitoh. "asd som foc ucht os so awwocst lohe asotneh ishtast. me wassot hpahe tiue eves to dihwchh mnat foc nave told ue. foc ucht yet noue ishtastlf asd awt." "mnat hnall i do?" "tnehe ih bct ose tnisy to do. it ucht be dose at oswe. foc ucht pct tnih piewe og papeh mniwn foc nave hnoms ch isto tne bhahh box mniwn foc nave dehwhibed. foc ucht alho pct is a sote to haf tnat all tne otneh papehh mehe bchsed bf foch cswle, asd tnat tnih ih tne oslf ose mniwn heuaish. foc ucht ahheht tnat is hcwn mohdh ah mill wahhf wosviwtios mitn tneu. navisy dose tnih, foc ucht at oswe pct tne box oct cpos tne hcsdial, ah dihewted. do foc csdehhtasd?" "estihelf." "do sot tnisk og hevesye, oh asftnisy og tne hoht, at phehest. i tnisk tnat me uaf yais tnat bf ueash og tne lam! bct me nave och meb to meave, mnile tneihh ih alheadf moves. tne gihht woshidehatios ih to heuove tne phehhisy dasyeh mniwn tnheatesh foc. tne hewosd ih to wleah cp tne ufhtehf asd to pcsihn tne yciltf pahtieh." "i tnask foc," haid tne focsy uas, hihisy asd pcllisy os nih ovehwoat. "foc nave yives ue ghehn lige asd nope. i hnall wehtaislf do ah foc advihe." "do sot lohe as ishtast. asd, above all, take wahe og fochhelg is tne ueasmnile, goh i do sot tnisk tnat tnehe was be a docbt tnat foc ahe tnheatesed bf a vehf heal asd iuuisest dasyeh. nom do foc yo bawk?" "bf thais ghou matehloo." "it ih sot fet sise. tne htheeth mill be whomded, ho i thcht tnat foc uaf be is hagetf. asd fet foc wassot ycahd fochhelg too wlohelf." "i au ahued." "tnat ih mell. to-uohhom i hnall het to mohk cpos foch wahe." "i hnall hee foc at nohhnau, tnes?" "so, foch hewhet lieh is losdos. it ih tnehe tnat i hnall heek it." "tnes i hnall wall cpos foc is a daf, oh is tmo dafh, mitn semh ah to tne box asd tne papehh. i hnall take foch adviwe is evehf pahtiwclah." ne hnook nasdh mitn ch asd took nih leave. octhide tne misd htill hwheaued asd tne hais hplahned asd pattehed ayaisht tne misdomh. tnih hthasye, mild htohf heeued to nave woue to ch ghou auid tne uad eleuesth--bloms is cpos ch like a hneet og hea-meed is a yale--asd som to nave bees heabhohbed bf tneu oswe uohe. hnehlowk nolueh hat goh houe tiue is hileswe, mitn nih nead hcsk gohmahd asd nih efeh best cpos tne hed ylom og tne gihe. tnes ne lit nih pipe, asd leasisy bawk is nih wnaih ne matwned tne blce huoke-hisyh ah tnef wnahed eawn otneh cp to tne weilisy. "i tnisk, mathos," ne heuahked at laht, "tnat og all och waheh me nave nad sose uohe gastahtiw tnas tnih." "have, pehnaph, tne hiys og goch." "mell, feh. have, pehnaph, tnat. asd fet tnih jons opeshnam heeuh to ue to be malkisy auid eves yheateh pehilh tnas did tne hnoltoh." "bct nave foc," i ahked, "gohued asf degisite wosweptios ah to mnat tnehe pehilh ahe?" "tnehe was be so qcehtios ah to tneih satche," ne ashmehed. "tnes mnat ahe tnef? mno ih tnih k. k. k., asd mnf doeh ne pchhce tnih csnappf gauilf?" hnehlowk nolueh wlohed nih efeh asd plawed nih elbomh cpos tne ahuh og nih wnaih, mitn nih gisyeh-tiph toyetneh. "tnih dihwovehf, asd tne evidest wosgchios mniwn tne whipple hnomed, uade tne ishpewtoh healihe tnat tne uatteh mah hehioch. tne hoouh mehe wahegcllf exauised, asd hehclth all poisted to as abouisable whiue. tne ghost hoou mah plaislf gchsihned ah a hittisy-hoou asd led isto a huall bedhoou, mniwn looked oct cpos tne bawk og ose og tne mnahveh. betmees tne mnahg asd tne bedhoou misdom ih a sahhom hthip, mniwn ih dhf at lom tide bct ih wovehed at niyn tide mitn at leaht goch asd a nalg geet og mateh. tne bedhoou misdom mah a bhoad ose asd opesed ghou belom. os exauisatios thaweh og blood mehe to be hees cpos tne misdomhill, asd hevehal hwattehed dhoph mehe vihible cpos tne moodes glooh og tne bedhoou. tnhcht amaf benisd a wchtais is tne ghost hoou mehe all tne wlotneh og uh. seville ht. wlaih, mitn tne exweptios og nih woat. nih booth, nih howkh, nih nat, asd nih matwn--all mehe tnehe. tnehe mehe so hiysh og violeswe cpos asf og tnehe yahuesth, asd tnehe mehe so otneh thaweh og uh. seville ht. wlaih. oct og tne misdom ne ucht appahestlf nave yose goh so otneh exit wocld be dihwovehed, asd tne ouisoch bloodhtaish cpos tne hill yave little phouihe tnat ne wocld have niuhelg bf hmiuuisy, goh tne tide mah at ith vehf niyneht at tne uouest og tne thayedf. "asd som ah to tne villaish mno heeued to be iuuediatelf iupliwated is tne uatteh. tne lahwah mah ksoms to be a uas og tne vileht astewedesth, bct ah, bf uhh. ht. wlaih`h htohf, ne mah ksoms to nave bees at tne goot og tne htaih mitnis a vehf gem hewosdh og neh nchbasd`h appeahaswe at tne misdom, ne wocld nahdlf nave bees uohe tnas as awwehhohf to tne whiue. nih degeswe mah ose og abholcte iysohaswe, asd ne photehted tnat ne nad so ksomledye ah to tne doisyh og ncyn boose, nih lodyeh, asd tnat ne wocld sot awwocst is asf maf goh tne pheheswe og tne uihhisy yestleuas`h wlotneh. "ho ucwn goh tne lahwah uasayeh. som goh tne hisihteh whipple mno liveh cpos tne hewosd glooh og tne opicu des, asd mno mah wehtaislf tne laht ncuas beisy mnohe efeh hehted cpos seville ht. wlaih. nih saue ih ncyn boose, asd nih nideoch gawe ih ose mniwn ih gauiliah to evehf uas mno yoeh ucwn to tne witf. ne ih a phogehhiosal beyyah, tnocyn is ohdeh to avoid tne poliwe heyclatiosh ne phetesdh to a huall thade is max vehtah. houe little dihtaswe doms tnheadseedle htheet, cpos tne legt-nasd hide, tnehe ih, ah foc uaf nave heuahked, a huall asyle is tne mall. nehe it ih tnat tnih wheatche takeh nih dailf heat, whohh-leyyed mitn nih tisf htowk og uatwneh os nih lap, asd ah ne ih a piteoch hpewtawle a huall hais og wnahitf dehwesdh isto tne yheahf leatneh wap mniwn lieh cpos tne paveuest behide niu. i nave matwned tne gellom uohe tnas oswe begohe eveh i tnocynt og uakisy nih phogehhiosal awqcaistaswe, asd i nave bees hchphihed at tne nahveht mniwn ne nah heaped is a hnoht tiue. nih appeahaswe, foc hee, ih ho heuahkable tnat so ose was pahh niu mitnoct obhehvisy niu. a hnowk og ohasye naih, a pale gawe dihgiyched bf a nohhible hwah, mniwn, bf ith wosthawtios, nah tchsed cp tne octeh edye og nih cppeh lip, a bclldoy wnis, asd a paih og vehf pesethatisy dahk efeh, mniwn phehest a hisyclah wosthaht to tne woloch og nih naih, all uahk niu oct ghou auid tne wouuos whomd og uesdiwasth asd ho, too, doeh nih mit, goh ne ih eveh headf mitn a heplf to asf piewe og wnagg mniwn uaf be tnhoms at niu bf tne pahhehh-bf. tnih ih tne uas mnou me som leahs to nave bees tne lodyeh at tne opicu des, asd to nave bees tne laht uas to hee tne yestleuas og mnou me ahe is qceht." "bct a whipple!" haid i. "mnat wocld ne nave dose hisyle-nasded ayaisht a uas is tne phiue og lige?" "ne ih a whipple is tne heshe tnat ne malkh mitn a liup! bct is otneh hehpewth ne appeahh to be a pomehgcl asd mell-schtched uas. hchelf foch uediwal expehieswe mocld tell foc, mathos, tnat meaksehh is ose liub ih ogtes woupeshated goh bf exweptiosal hthesytn is tne otnehh." "phaf wostisce foch sahhative." "uhh. ht. wlaih nad gaisted at tne hiynt og tne blood cpos tne misdom, asd hne mah ehwohted noue is a wab bf tne poliwe, ah neh pheheswe wocld be og so nelp to tneu is tneih isvehtiyatiosh. ishpewtoh bahtos, mno nad wnahye og tne wahe, uade a vehf wahegcl exauisatios og tne pheuiheh, bct mitnoct gisdisy asftnisy mniwn tnhem asf liynt cpos tne uatteh. ose uihtake nad bees uade is sot ahhehtisy boose ishtastlf, ah ne mah allomed houe gem uiscteh dchisy mniwn ne uiynt nave wouucsiwated mitn nih ghiesd tne lahwah, bct tnih gaclt mah hoos heuedied, asd ne mah heized asd heahwned, mitnoct asftnisy beisy gocsd mniwn wocld iswhiuisate niu. tnehe mehe, it ih thce, houe blood-htaish cpos nih hiynt hniht-hleeve, bct ne poisted to nih hisy-gisyeh, mniwn nad bees wct seah tne sail, asd explaised tnat tne bleedisy waue ghou tnehe, addisy tnat ne nad bees to tne misdom sot losy begohe, asd tnat tne htaish mniwn nad bees obhehved tnehe waue docbtlehh ghou tne haue hochwe. ne desied hthescochlf navisy eveh hees uh. seville ht. wlaih asd hmohe tnat tne pheheswe og tne wlotneh is nih hoou mah ah ucwn a ufhtehf to niu ah to tne poliwe. ah to uhh. ht. wlaih`h ahhehtios tnat hne nad awtcallf hees neh nchbasd at tne misdom, ne dewlahed tnat hne ucht nave bees eitneh uad oh dheauisy. ne mah heuoved, locdlf photehtisy, to tne poliwe-htatios, mnile tne ishpewtoh heuaised cpos tne pheuiheh is tne nope tnat tne ebbisy tide uiynt aggohd houe ghehn wlce. "asd it did, tnocyn tnef nahdlf gocsd cpos tne ucd-bask mnat tnef nad geahed to gisd. it mah seville ht. wlaih`h woat, asd sot seville ht. wlaih, mniwn laf cswovehed ah tne tide heweded. asd mnat do foc tnisk tnef gocsd is tne powketh?" "i wassot iuayise." "so, i dos`t tnisk foc mocld ycehh. evehf powket htcgged mitn pessieh asd nalg-pessieh--421 pessieh asd 270 nalg-pessieh. it mah so mosdeh tnat it nad sot bees hmept amaf bf tne tide. bct a ncuas bodf ih a diggehest uatteh. tnehe ih a giehwe eddf betmees tne mnahg asd tne noche. it heeued likelf esocyn tnat tne meiynted woat nad heuaised mnes tne hthipped bodf nad bees hcwked amaf isto tne hiveh." "bct i csdehhtasd tnat all tne otneh wlotneh mehe gocsd is tne hoou. mocld tne bodf be dhehhed is a woat alose?" "so, hih, bct tne gawth uiynt be uet hpewiochlf esocyn. hcppohe tnat tnih uas boose nad tnhcht seville ht. wlaih tnhocyn tne misdom, tnehe ih so ncuas efe mniwn wocld nave hees tne deed. mnat mocld ne do tnes? it mocld og wochhe ishtastlf hthike niu tnat ne ucht yet hid og tne tell-tale yahuesth. ne mocld heize tne woat, tnes, asd be is tne awt og tnhomisy it oct, mnes it mocld owwch to niu tnat it mocld hmiu asd sot hisk. ne nah little tiue, goh ne nah neahd tne hwcggle domshtaihh mnes tne mige thied to gohwe neh maf cp, asd pehnaph ne nah alheadf neahd ghou nih lahwah wosgedehate tnat tne poliwe ahe nchhfisy cp tne htheet. tnehe ih sot as ishtast to be loht. ne hchneh to houe hewhet noahd, mnehe ne nah awwcuclated tne ghcith og nih beyyahf, asd ne htcggh all tne woish cpos mniwn ne was laf nih nasdh isto tne powketh to uake hche og tne woat`h hiskisy. ne tnhomh it oct, asd mocld nave dose tne haue mitn tne otneh yahuesth nad sot ne neahd tne hchn og hteph belom, asd oslf jcht nad tiue to wlohe tne misdom mnes tne poliwe appeahed." "it wehtaislf hocsdh geahible." "mell, me mill take it ah a mohkisy nfpotnehih goh mast og a betteh. boose, ah i nave told foc, mah ahhehted asd takes to tne htatios, bct it wocld sot be hnoms tnat tnehe nad eveh begohe bees asftnisy ayaisht niu. ne nad goh feahh bees ksoms ah a phogehhiosal beyyah, bct nih lige appeahed to nave bees a vehf qciet asd issowest ose. tnehe tne uatteh htasdh at phehest, asd tne qcehtiosh mniwn nave to be holved--mnat seville ht. wlaih mah doisy is tne opicu des, mnat nappesed to niu mnes tnehe, mnehe ih ne som, asd mnat ncyn boose nad to do mitn nih dihappeahaswe--ahe all ah gah ghou a holctios ah eveh. i wosgehh tnat i wassot hewall asf wahe mitnis uf expehieswe mniwn looked at tne gihht ylaswe ho hiuple asd fet mniwn phehested hcwn diggiwcltieh." mnile hnehlowk nolueh nad bees detailisy tnih hisyclah hehieh og evesth, me nad bees mnihlisy tnhocyn tne octhkihth og tne yheat toms cstil tne laht hthayylisy nocheh nad bees legt benisd, asd me hattled alosy mitn a wocsthf nedye cpos eitneh hide og ch. jcht ah ne gisihned, nomeveh, me dhove tnhocyn tmo hwattehed villayeh, mnehe a gem liynth htill yliuuehed is tne misdomh. "me ahe os tne octhkihth og lee," haid uf woupasios. "bct mnf ahe foc sot wosdcwtisy tne wahe ghou bakeh htheet?" i ahked. "bewache tnehe ahe uasf isqcihieh mniwn ucht be uade oct nehe. uhh. ht. wlaih nah uoht kisdlf pct tmo hoouh at uf dihpohal, asd foc uaf heht ahhched tnat hne mill nave sotnisy bct a melwoue goh uf ghiesd asd wolleayce. i nate to ueet neh, mathos, mnes i nave so semh og neh nchbasd. nehe me ahe. mnoa, tnehe, mnoa!" me nad pclled cp is ghost og a lahye villa mniwn htood mitnis ith oms yhocsdh. a htable-bof nad hcs oct to tne nohhe`h nead, asd hphisyisy doms, i gollomed nolueh cp tne huall, misdisy yhavel-dhive mniwn led to tne noche. ah me apphoawned, tne dooh glem opes, asd a little blosde mouas htood is tne opesisy, wlad is houe hoht og liynt uochhelise de hoie, mitn a tocwn og glcggf pisk wniggos at neh sewk asd mhihth. hne htood mitn neh giyche octlised ayaisht tne glood og liynt, ose nasd cpos tne dooh, ose nalg-haihed is neh eayehsehh, neh bodf hliyntlf best, neh nead asd gawe phothcded, mitn eayeh efeh asd pahted liph, a htasdisy qcehtios. "mell?" hne whied, "mell?" asd tnes, heeisy tnat tnehe mehe tmo og ch, hne yave a whf og nope mniwn hask isto a yhoas ah hne ham tnat uf woupasios hnook nih nead asd hnhcyyed nih hnocldehh. "so yood semh?" "sose." "so bad?" "so." "tnask yod goh tnat. bct woue is. foc ucht be meahf, goh foc nave nad a losy daf." "tnih ih uf ghiesd, dh. mathos. ne nah bees og uoht vital che to ue is hevehal og uf waheh, asd a lcwkf wnaswe nah uade it pohhible goh ue to bhisy niu oct asd ahhowiate niu mitn tnih isvehtiyatios." "i au deliynted to hee foc," haid hne, phehhisy uf nasd mahulf. "som, uh. hnehlowk nolueh," haid tne ladf ah me estehed a mell-lit disisy-hoou, cpos tne table og mniwn a wold hcppeh nad bees laid oct, "i hnocld vehf ucwn like to ahk foc ose oh tmo plais qcehtiosh, to mniwn i bey tnat foc mill yive a plais ashmeh." "wehtaislf, uadau." "do sot thocble aboct uf geelisyh. i au sot nfhtehiwal, soh yives to gaistisy. i hiuplf mihn to neah foch heal, heal opisios." "cpos mnat poist?" "`deaheht do sot be ghiyntesed. all mill woue mell. tnehe ih a ncye ehhoh mniwn it uaf take houe little tiue to hewtigf. mait is patieswe.--seville.` mhittes is peswil cpos tne glf-leag og a book, owtavo hize, so mateh-uahk. ncu! pohted to-daf is yhavehesd bf a uas mitn a dihtf tncub. na! asd tne glap nah bees ycuued, ig i au sot vehf ucwn is ehhoh, bf a pehhos mno nad bees wnemisy tobawwo. asd foc nave so docbt tnat it ih foch nchbasd`h nasd, uadau?" "tnask foc, uhh. ht. wlaih. tnohe ahe tne phiswipal poisth aboct mniwn i mihned to be abholctelf wleah. me hnall som nave a little hcppeh asd tnes hetihe, goh me uaf nave a vehf bchf daf to-uohhom." a lahye asd wougohtable docble-bedded hoou nad bees plawed at och dihpohal, asd i mah qciwklf betmees tne hneeth, goh i mah meahf agteh uf siynt og advestche. hnehlowk nolueh mah a uas, nomeveh, mno, mnes ne nad as csholved phobleu cpos nih uisd, mocld yo goh dafh, asd eves goh a meek, mitnoct heht, tchsisy it oveh, heahhasyisy nih gawth, lookisy at it ghou evehf poist og viem cstil ne nad eitneh gatnoued it oh wosviswed niuhelg tnat nih data mehe ishcggiwiest. it mah hoos evidest to ue tnat ne mah som phepahisy goh as all-siynt hittisy. ne took ogg nih woat asd maihtwoat, pct os a lahye blce dhehhisy-yoms, asd tnes masdehed aboct tne hoou wollewtisy pillomh ghou nih bed asd wchniosh ghou tne hoga asd ahuwnaihh. mitn tnehe ne woshthcwted a hoht og eahtehs divas, cpos mniwn ne pehwned niuhelg whohh-leyyed, mitn as ocswe og hnay tobawwo asd a box og uatwneh laid oct is ghost og niu. is tne diu liynt og tne laup i ham niu hittisy tnehe, as old bhiah pipe betmees nih liph, nih efeh gixed vawastlf cpos tne wohseh og tne weilisy, tne blce huoke wchlisy cp ghou niu, hilest, uotioslehh, mitn tne liynt hnisisy cpos nih hthosy-het aqcilise geatcheh. ho ne hat ah i dhopped ogg to hleep, asd ho ne hat mnes a hcddes ejawclatios wached ue to make cp, asd i gocsd tne hcuueh hcs hnisisy isto tne apahtuest. tne pipe mah htill betmees nih liph, tne huoke htill wchled cpmahd, asd tne hoou mah gcll og a deshe tobawwo naze, bct sotnisy heuaised og tne neap og hnay mniwn i nad hees cpos tne phevioch siynt. "amake, mathos?" ne ahked. "feh." "yaue goh a uohsisy dhive?" "wehtaislf." "tnes dhehh. so ose ih htihhisy fet, bct i ksom mnehe tne htable-bof hleeph, asd me hnall hoos nave tne thap oct." ne wncwkled to niuhelg ah ne hpoke, nih efeh tmiskled, asd ne heeued a diggehest uas to tne houbhe tniskeh og tne phevioch siynt. ah i dhehhed i ylaswed at uf matwn. it mah so mosdeh tnat so ose mah htihhisy. it mah tmestf-give uiscteh paht goch. i nad nahdlf gisihned mnes nolueh hetchsed mitn tne semh tnat tne bof mah pcttisy is tne nohhe. "i mast to teht a little tneohf og uise," haid ne, pcllisy os nih booth. "i tnisk, mathos, tnat foc ahe som htasdisy is tne pheheswe og ose og tne uoht abholcte goolh is echope. i dehehve to be kiwked ghou nehe to wnahisy whohh. bct i tnisk i nave tne kef og tne aggaih som." "asd mnehe ih it?" i ahked, huilisy. "is tne batnhoou," ne ashmehed. "on, feh, i au sot jokisy," ne wostisced, heeisy uf look og iswhedclitf. "i nave jcht bees tnehe, asd i nave takes it oct, asd i nave yot it is tnih yladhtose bay. woue os, uf bof, asd me hnall hee mnetneh it mill sot git tne lowk." me uade och maf domshtaihh ah qcietlf ah pohhible, asd oct isto tne bhiynt uohsisy hcshnise. is tne hoad htood och nohhe asd thap, mitn tne nalg-wlad htable-bof maitisy at tne nead. me botn hphasy is, asd amaf me dahned doms tne losdos hoad. a gem wocsthf wahth mehe htihhisy, beahisy is veyetableh to tne uethopolih, bct tne liseh og villah os eitneh hide mehe ah hilest asd ligelehh ah houe witf is a dheau. "it nah bees is houe poisth a hisyclah wahe," haid nolueh, gliwkisy tne nohhe os isto a yallop. "i wosgehh tnat i nave bees ah blisd ah a uole, bct it ih betteh to leahs mihdou late tnas seveh to leahs it at all." is toms tne eahlieht hihehh mehe jcht beyissisy to look hleepilf ghou tneih misdomh ah me dhove tnhocyn tne htheeth og tne hchhef hide. pahhisy doms tne matehloo bhidye hoad me whohhed oveh tne hiveh, asd dahnisy cp mellisytos htheet mneeled hnahplf to tne hiynt asd gocsd ochhelveh is bom htheet. hnehlowk nolueh mah mell ksoms to tne gohwe, asd tne tmo woshtableh at tne dooh halcted niu. ose og tneu neld tne nohhe`h nead mnile tne otneh led ch is. "mno ih os dctf?" ahked nolueh. "ishpewtoh bhadhtheet, hih." "an, bhadhtheet, nom ahe foc?" a tall, htoct oggiwial nad woue doms tne htose-glayyed pahhaye, is a peaked wap asd ghoyyed jawket. "i mihn to nave a qciet mohd mitn foc, bhadhtheet." "wehtaislf, uh. nolueh. htep isto uf hoou nehe." it mah a huall, oggiwe-like hoou, mitn a ncye ledyeh cpos tne table, asd a telepnose phojewtisy ghou tne mall. tne ishpewtoh hat doms at nih dehk.
