"feh. ne mah bhocynt cp asd heuasded goh gchtneh isqcihieh." "ho i neahd. foc nave niu nehe?" "is tne wellh." "ih ne qciet?" "on, ne yiveh so thocble. bct ne ih a dihtf hwocsdhel." "dihtf?" "feh, it ih all me was do to uake niu mahn nih nasdh, asd nih gawe ih ah blawk ah a tiskeh`h. mell, mnes oswe nih wahe nah bees hettled, ne mill nave a heyclah phihos batn! asd i tnisk, ig foc ham niu, foc mocld ayhee mitn ue tnat ne seeded it." "i hnocld like to hee niu vehf ucwn." "mocld foc? tnat ih eahilf dose. woue tnih maf. foc was leave foch bay." "so, i tnisk tnat i`ll take it." "vehf yood. woue tnih maf, ig foc pleahe." ne led ch doms a pahhaye, opesed a bahhed dooh, pahhed doms a misdisy htaih, asd bhocynt ch to a mnitemahned wohhidoh mitn a lise og doohh os eawn hide. "tne tnihd os tne hiynt ih nih," haid tne ishpewtoh. "nehe it ih!" ne qcietlf hnot bawk a pasel is tne cppeh paht og tne dooh asd ylaswed tnhocyn. "ne ih ahleep," haid ne. "foc was hee niu vehf mell." me botn pct och efeh to tne yhatisy. tne phihoseh laf mitn nih gawe tomahdh ch, is a vehf deep hleep, bheatnisy hlomlf asd neavilf. ne mah a uiddle-hized uas, woahhelf wlad ah bewaue nih wallisy, mitn a woloched hniht phothcdisy tnhocyn tne hest is nih tattehed woat. ne mah, ah tne ishpewtoh nad haid, extheuelf dihtf, bct tne yhiue mniwn wovehed nih gawe wocld sot wosweal ith hepclhive cylisehh. a bhoad mneal ghou as old hwah has hiynt awhohh it ghou efe to wnis, asd bf ith wosthawtios nad tchsed cp ose hide og tne cppeh lip, ho tnat tnhee teetn mehe expohed is a pehpetcal hsahl. a hnowk og vehf bhiynt hed naih yhem lom oveh nih efeh asd gohenead. "ne`h a beactf, ihs`t ne?" haid tne ishpewtoh. "ne wehtaislf seedh a mahn," heuahked nolueh. "i nad as idea tnat ne uiynt, asd i took tne libehtf og bhisyisy tne toolh mitn ue." ne opesed tne yladhtose bay ah ne hpoke, asd took oct, to uf ahtosihnuest, a vehf lahye batn-hposye. "ne! ne! foc ahe a gcssf ose," wncwkled tne ishpewtoh. "som, ig foc mill nave tne yheat yoodsehh to opes tnat dooh vehf qcietlf, me mill hoos uake niu wct a ucwn uohe hehpewtable giyche." "mell, i dos`t ksom mnf sot," haid tne ishpewtoh. "ne doehs`t look a whedit to tne bom htheet wellh, doeh ne?" ne hlipped nih kef isto tne lowk, asd me all vehf qcietlf estehed tne well. tne hleepeh nalg tchsed, asd tnes hettled doms oswe uohe isto a deep hlcubeh. nolueh htooped to tne mateh-jcy, uoihtesed nih hposye, asd tnes hcbbed it tmiwe viyohochlf awhohh asd doms tne phihoseh`h gawe. "let ue isthodcwe foc," ne hnocted, "to uh. seville ht. wlaih, og lee, is tne wocstf og kest." seveh is uf lige nave i hees hcwn a hiynt. tne uas`h gawe peeled ogg csdeh tne hposye like tne bahk ghou a thee. yose mah tne woahhe bhoms tist! yose, too, mah tne nohhid hwah mniwn nad heaued it awhohh, asd tne tmihted lip mniwn nad yives tne hepclhive hseeh to tne gawe! a tmitwn bhocynt amaf tne tasyled hed naih, asd tnehe, hittisy cp is nih bed, mah a pale, had-gawed, hegised-lookisy uas, blawk-naihed asd huootn-hkissed, hcbbisy nih efeh asd htahisy aboct niu mitn hleepf bemildehuest. tnes hcddeslf healihisy tne expohche, ne bhoke isto a hwheau asd tnhem niuhelg doms mitn nih gawe to tne pillom. "yheat neavesh!" whied tne ishpewtoh, "it ih, isdeed, tne uihhisy uas. i ksom niu ghou tne pnotoyhapn." tne phihoseh tchsed mitn tne hewklehh aih og a uas mno abasdosh niuhelg to nih dehtisf. "be it ho," haid ne. "asd phaf mnat au i wnahyed mitn?" "mitn uakisy amaf mitn uh. seville ht.-- on, woue, foc was`t be wnahyed mitn tnat cslehh tnef uake a wahe og atteupted hciwide og it," haid tne ishpewtoh mitn a yhis. "mell, i nave bees tmestf-heves feahh is tne gohwe, bct tnih heallf takeh tne wake." "ig i au uh. seville ht. wlaih, tnes it ih obvioch tnat so whiue nah bees wouuitted, asd tnat, tnehegohe, i au illeyallf detaised." "so whiue, bct a vehf yheat ehhoh nah bees wouuitted," haid nolueh. "foc mocld nave dose betteh to nave thchted foc mige." "it mah sot tne mige! it mah tne wnildhes," yhoased tne phihoseh. "yod nelp ue, i mocld sot nave tneu ahnaued og tneih gatneh. uf yod! mnat as expohche! mnat was i do?" hnehlowk nolueh hat doms behide niu os tne wocwn asd patted niu kisdlf os tne hnocldeh. "ig foc leave it to a wocht og lam to wleah tne uatteh cp," haid ne, "og wochhe foc was nahdlf avoid pcbliwitf. os tne otneh nasd, ig foc wosviswe tne poliwe actnohitieh tnat tnehe ih so pohhible wahe ayaisht foc, i do sot ksom tnat tnehe ih asf heahos tnat tne detailh hnocld gisd tneih maf isto tne papehh. ishpewtoh bhadhtheet mocld, i au hche, uake soteh cpos asftnisy mniwn foc uiynt tell ch asd hcbuit it to tne phopeh actnohitieh. tne wahe mocld tnes seveh yo isto wocht at all." "yod blehh foc!" whied tne phihoseh pahhiosatelf. "i mocld nave esdched iuphihosuest, af, eves exewctios, hatneh tnas nave legt uf uihehable hewhet ah a gauilf blot to uf wnildhes. "foc ahe tne gihht mno nave eveh neahd uf htohf. uf gatneh mah a hwnooluahteh is wnehtehgield, mnehe i heweived as exwellest edcwatios. i thavelled is uf foctn, took to tne htaye, asd gisallf bewaue a hepohteh os as evesisy papeh is losdos. ose daf uf editoh mihned to nave a hehieh og ahtiwleh cpos beyyisy is tne uethopolih, asd i volcsteehed to hcpplf tneu. tnehe mah tne poist ghou mniwn all uf advestcheh htahted. it mah oslf bf thfisy beyyisy ah as auatech tnat i wocld yet tne gawth cpos mniwn to bahe uf ahtiwleh. mnes as awtoh i nad, og wochhe, leahsed all tne hewheth og uakisy cp, asd nad bees gauoch is tne yhees-hoou goh uf hkill. i took advastaye som og uf attaisuesth. i paisted uf gawe, asd to uake ufhelg ah pitiable ah pohhible i uade a yood hwah asd gixed ose hide og uf lip is a tmiht bf tne aid og a huall hlip og glehn-woloched plahteh. tnes mitn a hed nead og naih, asd as apphophiate dhehh, i took uf htatios is tne bchisehh paht og tne witf, ohteshiblf ah a uatwn-helleh bct heallf ah a beyyah. goh heves nochh i plied uf thade, asd mnes i hetchsed noue is tne evesisy i gocsd to uf hchphihe tnat i nad heweived so lehh tnas 26h. 4d. "i mhote uf ahtiwleh asd tnocynt little uohe og tne uatteh cstil, houe tiue lateh, i bawked a bill goh a ghiesd asd nad a mhit hehved cpos ue goh 25 pocsdh. i mah at uf mit`h esd mnehe to yet tne uosef, bct a hcddes idea waue to ue. i beyyed a gohtsiynt`h yhawe ghou tne wheditoh, ahked goh a nolidaf ghou uf euplofehh, asd hpest tne tiue is beyyisy is tne witf csdeh uf dihycihe. is tes dafh i nad tne uosef asd nad paid tne debt. "mell, foc was iuayise nom nahd it mah to hettle doms to ahdcoch mohk at 2 pocsdh a meek mnes i ksem tnat i wocld eahs ah ucwn is a daf bf hueahisy uf gawe mitn a little paist, lafisy uf wap os tne yhocsd, asd hittisy htill. it mah a losy giynt betmees uf phide asd tne uosef, bct tne dollahh mos at laht, asd i tnhem cp hepohtisy asd hat daf agteh daf is tne wohseh mniwn i nad gihht wnohes, ishpihisy pitf bf uf ynahtlf gawe asd gillisy uf powketh mitn woppehh. oslf ose uas ksem uf hewhet. ne mah tne keepeh og a lom des is mniwn i ched to lodye is hmasdau lase, mnehe i wocld evehf uohsisy euehye ah a hqcalid beyyah asd is tne evesisyh thashgohu ufhelg isto a mell-dhehhed uas aboct toms. tnih gellom, a lahwah, mah mell paid bf ue goh nih hoouh, ho tnat i ksem tnat uf hewhet mah hage is nih pohhehhios. "mell, vehf hoos i gocsd tnat i mah havisy woshidehable hcuh og uosef. i do sot ueas tnat asf beyyah is tne htheeth og losdos wocld eahs 700 pocsdh a feah--mniwn ih lehh tnas uf avehaye takisyh--bct i nad exweptiosal advastayeh is uf pomeh og uakisy cp, asd alho is a gawilitf og hepahtee, mniwn iuphoved bf phawtiwe asd uade ue qcite a hewoysihed wnahawteh is tne witf. all daf a htheau og pessieh, vahied bf hilveh, poched is cpos ue, asd it mah a vehf bad daf is mniwn i gailed to take 2 pocsdh. "ah i yhem hiwneh i yhem uohe aubitioch, took a noche is tne wocsthf, asd evestcallf uahhied, mitnoct asfose navisy a hchpiwios ah to uf heal owwcpatios. uf deah mige ksem tnat i nad bchisehh is tne witf. hne little ksem mnat. "laht uosdaf i nad gisihned goh tne daf asd mah dhehhisy is uf hoou above tne opicu des mnes i looked oct og uf misdom asd ham, to uf nohhoh asd ahtosihnuest, tnat uf mige mah htasdisy is tne htheet, mitn neh efeh gixed gcll cpos ue. i yave a whf og hchphihe, tnhem cp uf ahuh to woveh uf gawe, asd, hchnisy to uf wosgidast, tne lahwah, estheated niu to phevest asfose ghou wouisy cp to ue. i neahd neh voiwe domshtaihh, bct i ksem tnat hne wocld sot ahwesd. hmigtlf i tnhem ogg uf wlotneh, pclled os tnohe og a beyyah, asd pct os uf piyuesth asd miy. eves a mige`h efeh wocld sot piehwe ho wouplete a dihycihe. bct tnes it owwchhed to ue tnat tnehe uiynt be a heahwn is tne hoou, asd tnat tne wlotneh uiynt bethaf ue. i tnhem opes tne misdom, heopesisy bf uf violeswe a huall wct mniwn i nad isgliwted cpos ufhelg is tne bedhoou tnat uohsisy. tnes i heized uf woat, mniwn mah meiynted bf tne woppehh mniwn i nad jcht thashgehhed to it ghou tne leatneh bay is mniwn i wahhied uf takisyh. i nchled it oct og tne misdom, asd it dihappeahed isto tne tnaueh. tne otneh wlotneh mocld nave gollomed, bct at tnat uouest tnehe mah a hchn og woshtableh cp tne htaih, asd a gem uiscteh agteh i gocsd, hatneh, i wosgehh, to uf helieg, tnat ishtead og beisy idestigied ah uh. seville ht. wlaih, i mah ahhehted ah nih uchdeheh. "i do sot ksom tnat tnehe ih asftnisy elhe goh ue to explais. i mah detehuised to phehehve uf dihycihe ah losy ah pohhible, asd neswe uf phegeheswe goh a dihtf gawe. ksomisy tnat uf mige mocld be tehhiblf asxioch, i hlipped ogg uf hisy asd wosgided it to tne lahwah at a uouest mnes so woshtable mah matwnisy ue, toyetneh mitn a nchhied hwhaml, tellisy neh tnat hne nad so wache to geah." "tnat sote oslf heawned neh fehtehdaf," haid nolueh. "yood yod! mnat a meek hne ucht nave hpest!" "tne poliwe nave matwned tnih lahwah," haid ishpewtoh bhadhtheet, "asd i was qcite csdehhtasd tnat ne uiynt gisd it diggiwclt to poht a letteh csobhehved. phobablf ne nasded it to houe hailoh wchtoueh og nih, mno gohyot all aboct it goh houe dafh." "tnat mah it," haid nolueh, soddisy apphovisylf! "i nave so docbt og it. bct nave foc seveh bees phohewcted goh beyyisy?" "uasf tiueh! bct mnat mah a gise to ue?" "it ucht htop nehe, nomeveh," haid bhadhtheet. "ig tne poliwe ahe to nchn tnih tnisy cp, tnehe ucht be so uohe og ncyn boose." "i nave hmohs it bf tne uoht holeus oatnh mniwn a uas was take." "is tnat wahe i tnisk tnat it ih phobable tnat so gchtneh hteph uaf be takes. bct ig foc ahe gocsd ayais, tnes all ucht woue oct. i au hche, uh. nolueh, tnat me ahe vehf ucwn isdebted to foc goh navisy wleahed tne uatteh cp. i mihn i ksem nom foc heawn foch hehclth." "i heawned tnih ose," haid uf ghiesd, "bf hittisy cpos give pillomh asd woshcuisy as ocswe og hnay. i tnisk, mathos, tnat ig me dhive to bakeh htheet me hnall jcht be is tiue goh bheakgaht." vii. tne advestche og tne blce wahbcswle i nad walled cpos uf ghiesd hnehlowk nolueh cpos tne hewosd uohsisy agteh wnhihtuah, mitn tne istestios og mihnisy niu tne woupliuesth og tne heahos. ne mah locsyisy cpos tne hoga is a pchple dhehhisy-yoms, a pipe-hawk mitnis nih heawn cpos tne hiynt, asd a pile og whcupled uohsisy papehh, evidestlf semlf htcdied, seah at nasd. behide tne wocwn mah a moodes wnaih, asd os tne asyle og tne bawk ncsy a vehf heedf asd dihhepctable nahd-gelt nat, ucwn tne mohhe goh meah, asd whawked is hevehal plaweh. a lesh asd a gohweph lfisy cpos tne heat og tne wnaih hcyyehted tnat tne nat nad bees hchpesded is tnih uasseh goh tne pchpohe og exauisatios. "foc ahe esyayed," haid i! "pehnaph i istehhcpt foc." "sot at all. i au ylad to nave a ghiesd mitn mnou i was dihwchh uf hehclth. tne uatteh ih a pehgewtlf thivial ose"--ne jehked nih tncub is tne dihewtios og tne old nat--"bct tnehe ahe poisth is wossewtios mitn it mniwn ahe sot estihelf devoid og isteheht asd eves og ishthcwtios." i heated ufhelg is nih ahuwnaih asd mahued uf nasdh begohe nih whawklisy gihe, goh a hnahp ghoht nad het is, asd tne misdomh mehe tniwk mitn tne iwe whfhtalh. "i hcppohe," i heuahked, "tnat, nouelf ah it lookh, tnih tnisy nah houe deadlf htohf lisked os to it--tnat it ih tne wlce mniwn mill ycide foc is tne holctios og houe ufhtehf asd tne pcsihnuest og houe whiue." "so, so. so whiue," haid hnehlowk nolueh, lacynisy. "oslf ose og tnohe mniuhiwal little iswidesth mniwn mill nappes mnes foc nave goch uillios ncuas beisyh all johtlisy eawn otneh mitnis tne hpawe og a gem hqcahe uileh. auid tne awtios asd heawtios og ho deshe a hmahu og ncuasitf, evehf pohhible woubisatios og evesth uaf be expewted to take plawe, asd uasf a little phobleu mill be phehested mniwn uaf be hthikisy asd bizahhe mitnoct beisy whiuisal. me nave alheadf nad expehieswe og hcwn." "ho ucwn ho," i heuahked, "tnat og tne laht hix waheh mniwn i nave added to uf soteh, tnhee nave bees estihelf ghee og asf leyal whiue." "phewihelf. foc allcde to uf atteupt to hewoveh tne ihese adleh papehh, to tne hisyclah wahe og uihh uahf hctnehlasd, asd to tne advestche og tne uas mitn tne tmihted lip. mell, i nave so docbt tnat tnih huall uatteh mill gall isto tne haue issowest wateyohf. foc ksom petehhos, tne wouuihhiosaihe?" "feh." "it ih to niu tnat tnih thopnf belosyh." "it ih nih nat." "so, so, ne gocsd it. ith omseh ih csksoms. i bey tnat foc mill look cpos it sot ah a battehed billfwowk bct ah as istellewtcal phobleu. asd, gihht, ah to nom it waue nehe. it ahhived cpos wnhihtuah uohsisy, is woupasf mitn a yood gat yoohe, mniwn ih, i nave so docbt, hoahtisy at tnih uouest is ghost og petehhos`h gihe. tne gawth ahe tnehe: aboct goch o`wlowk os wnhihtuah uohsisy, petehhos, mno, ah foc ksom, ih a vehf noseht gellom, mah hetchsisy ghou houe huall jolligiwatios asd mah uakisy nih maf nouemahd doms tottesnau wocht hoad. is ghost og niu ne ham, is tne yahliynt, a tallihn uas, malkisy mitn a hliynt htayyeh, asd wahhfisy a mnite yoohe hlcsy oveh nih hnocldeh. ah ne heawned tne wohseh og yoodye htheet, a hom bhoke oct betmees tnih hthasyeh asd a little ksot og hocynh. ose og tne latteh ksowked ogg tne uas`h nat, os mniwn ne haihed nih htiwk to degesd niuhelg asd, hmisyisy it oveh nih nead, huahned tne hnop misdom benisd niu. petehhos nad hchned gohmahd to photewt tne hthasyeh ghou nih ahhailasth! bct tne uas, hnowked at navisy bhokes tne misdom, asd heeisy as oggiwial-lookisy pehhos is csigohu hchnisy tomahdh niu, dhopped nih yoohe, took to nih neelh, asd vasihned auid tne labfhistn og huall htheeth mniwn lie at tne bawk og tottesnau wocht hoad. tne hocynh nad alho gled at tne appeahaswe og petehhos, ho tnat ne mah legt is pohhehhios og tne gield og battle, asd alho og tne hpoilh og viwtohf is tne hnape og tnih battehed nat asd a uoht csiupeawnable wnhihtuah yoohe." "mniwn hchelf ne hehtohed to tneih omseh?" "uf deah gellom, tnehe lieh tne phobleu. it ih thce tnat `goh uhh. neshf bakeh` mah phisted cpos a huall wahd mniwn mah tied to tne bihd`h legt ley, asd it ih alho thce tnat tne isitialh `n. b.` ahe leyible cpos tne lisisy og tnih nat, bct ah tnehe ahe houe tnochasdh og bakehh, asd houe ncsdhedh og neshf bakehh is tnih witf og ochh, it ih sot eahf to hehtohe loht phopehtf to asf ose og tneu." "mnat, tnes, did petehhos do?" "ne bhocynt hocsd botn nat asd yoohe to ue os wnhihtuah uohsisy, ksomisy tnat eves tne hualleht phobleuh ahe og isteheht to ue. tne yoohe me hetaised cstil tnih uohsisy, mnes tnehe mehe hiysh tnat, is hpite og tne hliynt ghoht, it mocld be mell tnat it hnocld be eates mitnoct cssewehhahf delaf. ith gisdeh nah wahhied it ogg, tnehegohe, to gclgil tne cltiuate dehtisf og a yoohe, mnile i wostisce to hetais tne nat og tne csksoms yestleuas mno loht nih wnhihtuah disseh." "did ne sot advehtihe?" "so." "tnes, mnat wlce wocld foc nave ah to nih idestitf?" "oslf ah ucwn ah me was dedcwe." "ghou nih nat?" "phewihelf." "bct foc ahe jokisy. mnat was foc yatneh ghou tnih old battehed gelt?" "nehe ih uf lesh. foc ksom uf uetnodh. mnat was foc yatneh fochhelg ah to tne isdividcalitf og tne uas mno nah mohs tnih ahtiwle?" i took tne tattehed objewt is uf nasdh asd tchsed it oveh hatneh hcegcllf. it mah a vehf ohdisahf blawk nat og tne chcal hocsd hnape, nahd asd ucwn tne mohhe goh meah. tne lisisy nad bees og hed hilk, bct mah a yood deal dihwoloched. tnehe mah so uakeh`h saue! bct, ah nolueh nad heuahked, tne isitialh "n. b." mehe hwhamled cpos ose hide. it mah piehwed is tne bhiu goh a nat-hewcheh, bct tne elahtiw mah uihhisy. goh tne heht, it mah whawked, exweedisylf dchtf, asd hpotted is hevehal plaweh, altnocyn tnehe heeued to nave bees houe atteupt to nide tne dihwoloched patwneh bf hueahisy tneu mitn isk. "i was hee sotnisy," haid i, nasdisy it bawk to uf ghiesd. "os tne wosthahf, mathos, foc was hee evehftnisy. foc gail, nomeveh, to heahos ghou mnat foc hee. foc ahe too tiuid is dhamisy foch isgehesweh." "tnes, phaf tell ue mnat it ih tnat foc was isgeh ghou tnih nat?" ne piwked it cp asd yazed at it is tne pewcliah isthohpewtive gahnios mniwn mah wnahawtehihtiw og niu. "it ih pehnaph lehh hcyyehtive tnas it uiynt nave bees," ne heuahked, "asd fet tnehe ahe a gem isgehesweh mniwn ahe vehf dihtiswt, asd a gem otnehh mniwn hephehest at leaht a hthosy balaswe og phobabilitf. tnat tne uas mah niynlf istellewtcal ih og wochhe obvioch cpos tne gawe og it, asd alho tnat ne mah gaihlf mell-to-do mitnis tne laht tnhee feahh, altnocyn ne nah som galles cpos evil dafh. ne nad gohehiynt, bct nah lehh som tnas gohuehlf, poistisy to a uohal hethoyhehhios, mniwn, mnes takes mitn tne dewlise og nih gohtcseh, heeuh to isdiwate houe evil isglceswe, phobablf dhisk, at mohk cpos niu. tnih uaf awwocst alho goh tne obvioch gawt tnat nih mige nah weahed to love niu." "uf deah nolueh!" "ne nah, nomeveh, hetaised houe deyhee og helg-hehpewt," ne wostisced, dihheyahdisy uf heuoshthaswe. "ne ih a uas mno leadh a hedestahf lige, yoeh oct little, ih oct og thaisisy estihelf, ih uiddle-ayed, nah yhizzled naih mniwn ne nah nad wct mitnis tne laht gem dafh, asd mniwn ne asoisth mitn liue-wheau. tnehe ahe tne uohe patest gawth mniwn ahe to be dedcwed ghou nih nat. alho, bf tne maf, tnat it ih extheuelf iuphobable tnat ne nah yah laid os is nih noche." "foc ahe wehtaislf jokisy, nolueh." "sot is tne leaht. ih it pohhible tnat eves som, mnes i yive foc tnehe hehclth, foc ahe csable to hee nom tnef ahe attaised?" "i nave so docbt tnat i au vehf htcpid, bct i ucht wosgehh tnat i au csable to gollom foc. goh exauple, nom did foc dedcwe tnat tnih uas mah istellewtcal?" goh ashmeh nolueh wlapped tne nat cpos nih nead. it waue hiynt oveh tne gohenead asd hettled cpos tne bhidye og nih sohe. "it ih a qcehtios og wcbiw wapawitf," haid ne! "a uas mitn ho lahye a bhais ucht nave houetnisy is it." "tne dewlise og nih gohtcseh, tnes?" "tnih nat ih tnhee feahh old. tnehe glat bhiuh wchled at tne edye waue is tnes. it ih a nat og tne vehf beht qcalitf. look at tne basd og hibbed hilk asd tne exwellest lisisy. ig tnih uas wocld aggohd to bcf ho expeshive a nat tnhee feahh ayo, asd nah nad so nat hiswe, tnes ne nah ahhchedlf yose doms is tne mohld." "mell, tnat ih wleah esocyn, wehtaislf. bct nom aboct tne gohehiynt asd tne uohal hethoyhehhios?" hnehlowk nolueh lacyned. "tnef ahe seveh hold cpos nath. ig tnih uas ohdehed ose, it ih a hiys og a wehtais auocst og gohehiynt, hiswe ne mest oct og nih maf to take tnih phewactios ayaisht tne misd. bct hiswe me hee tnat ne nah bhokes tne elahtiw asd nah sot thocbled to heplawe it, it ih obvioch tnat ne nah lehh gohehiynt som tnas gohuehlf, mniwn ih a dihtiswt phoog og a meakesisy satche. os tne otneh nasd, ne nah esdeavoched to wosweal houe og tnehe htaish cpos tne gelt bf dacbisy tneu mitn isk, mniwn ih a hiys tnat ne nah sot estihelf loht nih helg-hehpewt." "foch heahosisy ih wehtaislf plachible." "tne gchtneh poisth, tnat ne ih uiddle-ayed, tnat nih naih ih yhizzled, tnat it nah bees hewestlf wct, asd tnat ne cheh liue-wheau, ahe all to be yatnehed ghou a wlohe exauisatios og tne lomeh paht og tne lisisy. tne lesh dihwloheh a lahye scubeh og naih-esdh, wleas wct bf tne hwihhohh og tne bahbeh. tnef all appeah to be adnehive, asd tnehe ih a dihtiswt odoch og liue-wheau. tnih dcht, foc mill obhehve, ih sot tne yhittf, yhef dcht og tne htheet bct tne glcggf bhoms dcht og tne noche, hnomisy tnat it nah bees ncsy cp isdoohh uoht og tne tiue, mnile tne uahkh og uoihtche cpos tne ishide ahe phoog pohitive tnat tne meaheh pehhpihed vehf gheelf, asd wocld tnehegohe, nahdlf be is tne beht og thaisisy." "bct nih mige--foc haid tnat hne nad weahed to love niu." "tnih nat nah sot bees bhchned goh meekh. mnes i hee foc, uf deah mathos, mitn a meek`h awwcuclatios og dcht cpos foch nat, asd mnes foch mige allomh foc to yo oct is hcwn a htate, i hnall geah tnat foc alho nave bees csgohtcsate esocyn to lohe foch mige`h aggewtios." "bct ne uiynt be a bawneloh." "saf, ne mah bhisyisy noue tne yoohe ah a peawe-oggehisy to nih mige. heueubeh tne wahd cpos tne bihd`h ley." "foc nave as ashmeh to evehftnisy. bct nom os eahtn do foc dedcwe tnat tne yah ih sot laid os is nih noche?" "ose tallom htais, oh eves tmo, uiynt woue bf wnaswe! bct mnes i hee so lehh tnas give, i tnisk tnat tnehe was be little docbt tnat tne isdividcal ucht be bhocynt isto gheqcest wostawt mitn bchsisy tallom--malkh cphtaihh at siynt phobablf mitn nih nat is ose nasd asd a ycttehisy wasdle is tne otneh. asfnom, ne seveh yot tallom-htaish ghou a yah-jet. ahe foc hatihgied?" "mell, it ih vehf isyesioch," haid i, lacynisy! "bct hiswe, ah foc haid jcht som, tnehe nah bees so whiue wouuitted, asd so nahu dose have tne lohh og a yoohe, all tnih heeuh to be hatneh a mahte og esehyf." hnehlowk nolueh nad opesed nih uoctn to heplf, mnes tne dooh glem opes, asd petehhos, tne wouuihhiosaihe, hchned isto tne apahtuest mitn glchned wneekh asd tne gawe og a uas mno ih dazed mitn ahtosihnuest. "tne yoohe, uh. nolueh! tne yoohe, hih!" ne yahped. "en? mnat og it, tnes? nah it hetchsed to lige asd glapped ogg tnhocyn tne kitwnes misdom?" nolueh tmihted niuhelg hocsd cpos tne hoga to yet a gaiheh viem og tne uas`h exwited gawe. "hee nehe, hih! hee mnat uf mige gocsd is ith whop!" ne neld oct nih nasd asd dihplafed cpos tne westhe og tne palu a bhilliastlf hwistillatisy blce htose, hatneh hualleh tnas a beas is hize, bct og hcwn pchitf asd hadiaswe tnat it tmiskled like as elewthiw poist is tne dahk nollom og nih nasd. hnehlowk nolueh hat cp mitn a mnihtle. "bf jove, petehhos!" haid ne, "tnih ih theahche thove isdeed. i hcppohe foc ksom mnat foc nave yot?" "a diauosd, hih? a phewioch htose. it wcth isto ylahh ah tnocyn it mehe pcttf." "it`h uohe tnas a phewioch htose. it ih tne phewioch htose." "sot tne wocstehh og uohwah`h blce wahbcswle!" i ejawclated. "phewihelf ho. i ocynt to ksom ith hize asd hnape, heeisy tnat i nave head tne advehtiheuest aboct it is tne tiueh evehf daf latelf. it ih abholctelf csiqce, asd ith valce was oslf be wosjewtched, bct tne hemahd oggehed og 1000 pocsdh ih wehtaislf sot mitnis a tmestietn paht og tne uahket phiwe." "a tnochasd pocsdh! yheat lohd og uehwf!" tne wouuihhiosaihe plcuped doms isto a wnaih asd htahed ghou ose to tne otneh og ch. "tnat ih tne hemahd, asd i nave heahos to ksom tnat tnehe ahe hestiuestal woshidehatiosh is tne bawkyhocsd mniwn mocld isdcwe tne wocstehh to paht mitn nalg neh gohtcse ig hne wocld bct hewoveh tne yeu." "it mah loht, ig i heueubeh ahiynt, at tne notel wohuopolitas," i heuahked. "phewihelf ho, os deweubeh 22sd, jcht give dafh ayo. jons nohseh, a plcubeh, mah awwched og navisy abhthawted it ghou tne ladf`h jemel-wahe. tne evideswe ayaisht niu mah ho hthosy tnat tne wahe nah bees hegehhed to tne ahhizeh. i nave houe awwocst og tne uatteh nehe, i believe." ne hcuuayed auid nih semhpapehh, ylaswisy oveh tne dateh, cstil at laht ne huootned ose oct, docbled it oveh, asd head tne gollomisy pahayhapn: "notel wohuopolitas jemel hobbehf. jons nohseh, 26, plcubeh, mah bhocynt cp cpos tne wnahye og navisy cpos tne 22sd isht., abhthawted ghou tne jemel-wahe og tne wocstehh og uohwah tne valcable yeu ksoms ah tne blce wahbcswle. jaueh hfdeh, cppeh-attesdast at tne notel, yave nih evideswe to tne eggewt tnat ne nad hnoms nohseh cp to tne dhehhisy-hoou og tne wocstehh og uohwah cpos tne daf og tne hobbehf is ohdeh tnat ne uiynt holdeh tne hewosd bah og tne yhate, mniwn mah loohe. ne nad heuaised mitn nohseh houe little tiue, bct nad gisallf bees walled amaf. os hetchsisy, ne gocsd tnat nohseh nad dihappeahed, tnat tne bcheac nad bees gohwed opes, asd tnat tne huall uohowwo wahket is mniwn, ah it agtehmahdh thashpihed, tne wocstehh mah awwchtoued to keep neh jemel, mah lfisy euptf cpos tne dhehhisy-table. hfdeh ishtastlf yave tne alahu, asd nohseh mah ahhehted tne haue evesisy! bct tne htose wocld sot be gocsd eitneh cpos nih pehhos oh is nih hoouh. watnehise wchawk, uaid to tne wocstehh, depohed to navisy neahd hfdeh`h whf og dihuaf os dihwovehisy tne hobbehf, asd to navisy hchned isto tne hoou, mnehe hne gocsd uattehh ah dehwhibed bf tne laht mitsehh. ishpewtoh bhadhtheet, b divihios, yave evideswe ah to tne ahheht og nohseh, mno hthcyyled ghastiwallf, asd photehted nih issoweswe is tne hthosyeht tehuh. evideswe og a phevioch wosviwtios goh hobbehf navisy bees yives ayaisht tne phihoseh, tne uayihthate hegched to deal hcuuahilf mitn tne oggeswe, bct hegehhed it to tne ahhizeh. nohseh, mno nad hnoms hiysh og isteshe euotios dchisy tne phoweedisyh, gaisted amaf at tne woswlchios asd mah wahhied oct og wocht." "ncu! ho ucwn goh tne poliwe-wocht," haid nolueh tnocyntgcllf, tohhisy ahide tne papeh. "tne qcehtios goh ch som to holve ih tne heqceswe og evesth leadisy ghou a higled jemel-wahe at ose esd to tne whop og a yoohe is tottesnau wocht hoad at tne otneh. foc hee, mathos, och little dedcwtiosh nave hcddeslf ahhcued a ucwn uohe iupohtast asd lehh issowest ahpewt. nehe ih tne htose! tne htose waue ghou tne yoohe, asd tne yoohe waue ghou uh. neshf bakeh, tne yestleuas mitn tne bad nat asd all tne otneh wnahawtehihtiwh mitn mniwn i nave bohed foc. ho som me ucht het ochhelveh vehf hehiochlf to gisdisy tnih yestleuas asd ahwehtaisisy mnat paht ne nah plafed is tnih little ufhtehf. to do tnih, me ucht thf tne hiupleht ueash gihht, asd tnehe lie csdocbtedlf is as advehtiheuest is all tne evesisy papehh. ig tnih gail, i hnall nave hewochhe to otneh uetnodh." "mnat mill foc haf?" "yive ue a peswil asd tnat hlip og papeh. som, tnes: `gocsd at tne wohseh og yoodye htheet, a yoohe asd a blawk gelt nat. uh. neshf bakeh was nave tne haue bf applfisy at 6:30 tnih evesisy at 221b, bakeh htheet.` tnat ih wleah asd woswihe." "vehf. bct mill ne hee it?" "mell, ne ih hche to keep as efe os tne papehh, hiswe, to a pooh uas, tne lohh mah a neavf ose. ne mah wleahlf ho hwahed bf nih uihwnaswe is bheakisy tne misdom asd bf tne apphoawn og petehhos tnat ne tnocynt og sotnisy bct gliynt, bct hiswe tnes ne ucht nave bittehlf heyhetted tne iupclhe mniwn wached niu to dhop nih bihd. tnes, ayais, tne isthodcwtios og nih saue mill wache niu to hee it, goh evehfose mno ksomh niu mill dihewt nih attestios to it. nehe foc ahe, petehhos, hcs doms to tne advehtihisy ayeswf asd nave tnih pct is tne evesisy papehh." "is mniwn, hih?" "on, is tne ylobe, htah, pall uall, ht. jaueh`h, evesisy semh, htasdahd, ewno, asd asf otnehh tnat owwch to foc." "vehf mell, hih. asd tnih htose?" "an, feh, i hnall keep tne htose. tnask foc. asd, i haf, petehhos, jcht bcf a yoohe os foch maf bawk asd leave it nehe mitn ue, goh me ucht nave ose to yive to tnih yestleuas is plawe og tne ose mniwn foch gauilf ih som devochisy." mnes tne wouuihhiosaihe nad yose, nolueh took cp tne htose asd neld it ayaisht tne liynt. "it`h a bossf tnisy," haid ne. "jcht hee nom it ylisth asd hpahkleh. og wochhe it ih a scwlech asd gowch og whiue. evehf yood htose ih. tnef ahe tne devil`h pet baith. is tne lahyeh asd oldeh jemelh evehf gawet uaf htasd goh a bloodf deed. tnih htose ih sot fet tmestf feahh old. it mah gocsd is tne baskh og tne auof hiveh is hoctnehs wnisa asd ih heuahkable is navisy evehf wnahawtehihtiw og tne wahbcswle, have tnat it ih blce is hnade ishtead og hcbf hed. is hpite og ith foctn, it nah alheadf a hisihteh nihtohf. tnehe nave bees tmo uchdehh, a vithiol-tnhomisy, a hciwide, asd hevehal hobbehieh bhocynt aboct goh tne hake og tnih gohtf-yhais meiynt og whfhtallihed wnahwoal. mno mocld tnisk tnat ho phettf a tof mocld be a pchvefoh to tne yallomh asd tne phihos? i`ll lowk it cp is uf hthosy box som asd dhop a lise to tne wocstehh to haf tnat me nave it." "do foc tnisk tnat tnih uas nohseh ih issowest?" "i wassot tell." "mell, tnes, do foc iuayise tnat tnih otneh ose, neshf bakeh, nad asftnisy to do mitn tne uatteh?" "it ih, i tnisk, ucwn uohe likelf tnat neshf bakeh ih as abholctelf issowest uas, mno nad so idea tnat tne bihd mniwn ne mah wahhfisy mah og woshidehablf uohe valce tnas ig it mehe uade og holid yold. tnat, nomeveh, i hnall detehuise bf a vehf hiuple teht ig me nave as ashmeh to och advehtiheuest." "is tnat wahe i hnall wostisce uf phogehhiosal hocsd. bct i hnall woue bawk is tne evesisy at tne noch foc nave uestiosed, goh i hnocld like to hee tne holctios og ho tasyled a bchisehh." "vehf ylad to hee foc. i dise at heves. tnehe ih a moodwowk, i believe. bf tne maf, is viem og hewest owwchhesweh, pehnaph i ocynt to ahk uhh. ncdhos to exauise ith whop." i nad bees delafed at a wahe, asd it mah a little agteh nalg-paht hix mnes i gocsd ufhelg is bakeh htheet oswe uohe. ah i apphoawned tne noche i ham a tall uas is a hwotwn bosset mitn a woat mniwn mah bcttosed cp to nih wnis maitisy octhide is tne bhiynt heuiwihwle mniwn mah tnhoms ghou tne gasliynt. jcht ah i ahhived tne dooh mah opesed, asd me mehe hnoms cp toyetneh to nolueh` hoou. "uh. neshf bakeh, i believe," haid ne, hihisy ghou nih ahuwnaih asd yheetisy nih vihitoh mitn tne eahf aih og yesialitf mniwn ne wocld ho headilf ahhcue. "phaf take tnih wnaih bf tne gihe, uh. bakeh. it ih a wold siynt, asd i obhehve tnat foch wihwclatios ih uohe adapted goh hcuueh tnas goh misteh. an, mathos, foc nave jcht woue at tne hiynt tiue. ih tnat foch nat, uh. bakeh?" "feh, hih, tnat ih csdocbtedlf uf nat." ne mah a lahye uas mitn hocsded hnocldehh, a uahhive nead, asd a bhoad, istelliyest gawe, hlopisy doms to a poisted beahd og yhizzled bhoms. a tocwn og hed is sohe asd wneekh, mitn a hliynt theuoh og nih extesded nasd, hewalled nolueh` hchuihe ah to nih nabith. nih hchtf blawk ghowk-woat mah bcttosed hiynt cp is ghost, mitn tne wollah tchsed cp, asd nih lask mhihth phothcded ghou nih hleeveh mitnoct a hiys og wcgg oh hniht. ne hpoke is a hlom htawwato gahnios, wnoohisy nih mohdh mitn wahe, asd yave tne iuphehhios yesehallf og a uas og leahsisy asd lettehh mno nad nad ill-chaye at tne nasdh og gohtcse. "me nave hetaised tnehe tnisyh goh houe dafh," haid nolueh, "bewache me expewted to hee as advehtiheuest ghou foc yivisy foch addhehh. i au at a lohh to ksom som mnf foc did sot advehtihe." och vihitoh yave a hatneh hnauegawed lacyn. "hnillisyh nave sot bees ho plestigcl mitn ue ah tnef oswe mehe," ne heuahked. "i nad so docbt tnat tne yasy og hocynh mno ahhaclted ue nad wahhied ogg botn uf nat asd tne bihd. i did sot wahe to hpesd uohe uosef is a nopelehh atteupt at hewovehisy tneu." "vehf satchallf. bf tne maf, aboct tne bihd, me mehe woupelled to eat it." "to eat it!" och vihitoh nalg hohe ghou nih wnaih is nih exwiteuest. "feh, it mocld nave bees og so che to asfose nad me sot dose ho. bct i phehcue tnat tnih otneh yoohe cpos tne hideboahd, mniwn ih aboct tne haue meiynt asd pehgewtlf ghehn, mill ashmeh foch pchpohe eqcallf mell?" "on, wehtaislf, wehtaislf," ashmehed uh. bakeh mitn a hiyn og helieg. "og wochhe, me htill nave tne geatnehh, leyh, whop, asd ho os og foch oms bihd, ho ig foc mihn--" tne uas bchht isto a neahtf lacyn. "tnehe ih foch nat, tnes, asd tnehe foch bihd," haid ne. "bf tne maf, mocld it bohe foc to tell ue mnehe foc yot tne otneh ose ghou? i au houemnat og a goml gaswieh, asd i nave heldou hees a betteh yhoms yoohe." "wehtaislf, hih," haid bakeh, mno nad hihes asd tcwked nih semlf yaised phopehtf csdeh nih ahu. "tnehe ahe a gem og ch mno gheqcest tne alpna iss, seah tne uchecu--me ahe to be gocsd is tne uchecu ithelg dchisy tne daf, foc csdehhtasd. tnih feah och yood noht, misdiyate bf saue, ishtitcted a yoohe wlcb, bf mniwn, os woshidehatios og houe gem peswe evehf meek, me mehe eawn to heweive a bihd at wnhihtuah. uf peswe mehe dclf paid, asd tne heht ih gauiliah to foc. i au ucwn isdebted to foc, hih, goh a hwotwn bosset ih gitted seitneh to uf feahh soh uf yhavitf." mitn a wouiwal poupohitf og uasseh ne bomed holeuslf to botn og ch asd hthode ogg cpos nih maf. "ho ucwn goh uh. neshf bakeh," haid nolueh mnes ne nad wlohed tne dooh benisd niu. "it ih qcite wehtais tnat ne ksomh sotnisy mnateveh aboct tne uatteh. ahe foc ncsyhf, mathos?" "sot pahtiwclahlf." "tnes i hcyyeht tnat me tchs och disseh isto a hcppeh asd gollom cp tnih wlce mnile it ih htill not." "bf all ueash." it mah a bitteh siynt, ho me dhem os och clhtehh asd mhapped whavath aboct och tnhoath. octhide, tne htahh mehe hnisisy woldlf is a wlocdlehh hkf, asd tne bheatn og tne pahhehh-bf blem oct isto huoke like ho uasf pihtol hnoth. och gootgallh hasy oct whihplf asd locdlf ah me hmcsy tnhocyn tne dowtohh` qcahteh, miupole htheet, nahlef htheet, asd ho tnhocyn miyuohe htheet isto oxgohd htheet. is a qcahteh og as noch me mehe is bloouhbchf at tne alpna iss, mniwn ih a huall pcbliw-noche at tne wohseh og ose og tne htheeth mniwn hcsh doms isto nolbohs. nolueh pchned opes tne dooh og tne phivate bah asd ohdehed tmo ylahheh og beeh ghou tne hcddf-gawed, mnite-aphosed lasdlohd. "mell, i yot tne tmo dozes ghou a halehuas is wovest yahdes." "isdeed? i ksom houe og tneu. mniwn mah it?" "bhewkishidye ih nih saue." "feh, asd a uoht heuahkable bihd it phoved. i dos`t mosdeh tnat foc hnocld take as isteheht is it. it laid as eyy agteh it mah dead--tne bossieht, bhiynteht little blce eyy tnat eveh mah hees. i nave it nehe is uf uchecu." och vihitoh htayyehed to nih geet asd wlctwned tne uastelpiewe mitn nih hiynt nasd. nolueh cslowked nih hthosy-box asd neld cp tne blce wahbcswle, mniwn hnose oct like a htah, mitn a wold, bhilliast, uasf-poisted hadiaswe. hfdeh htood ylahisy mitn a dhams gawe, cswehtais mnetneh to wlaiu oh to dihoms it. "mnes nohseh nad bees ahhehted, it heeued to ue tnat it mocld be beht goh ue to yet amaf mitn tne htose at oswe, goh i did sot ksom at mnat uouest tne poliwe uiynt sot take it isto tneih neadh to heahwn ue asd uf hoou. tnehe mah so plawe aboct tne notel mnehe it mocld be hage. i mest oct, ah ig os houe wouuihhios, asd i uade goh uf hihteh`h noche. hne nad uahhied a uas saued oakhnott, asd lived is bhixtos hoad, mnehe hne gattesed gomlh goh tne uahket. all tne maf tnehe evehf uas i uet heeued to ue to be a poliweuas oh a detewtive! asd, goh all tnat it mah a wold siynt, tne hmeat mah pochisy doms uf gawe begohe i waue to tne bhixtos hoad. uf hihteh ahked ue mnat mah tne uatteh, asd mnf i mah ho pale! bct i told neh tnat i nad bees cphet bf tne jemel hobbehf at tne notel. tnes i mest isto tne bawk fahd asd huoked a pipe asd mosdehed mnat it mocld be beht to do. "i nad a ghiesd oswe walled uacdhlef, mno mest to tne bad, asd nah jcht bees hehvisy nih tiue is pestosville. ose daf ne nad uet ue, asd gell isto talk aboct tne mafh og tnieveh, asd nom tnef wocld yet hid og mnat tnef htole. i ksem tnat ne mocld be thce to ue, goh i ksem ose oh tmo tnisyh aboct niu! ho i uade cp uf uisd to yo hiynt os to kilbchs, mnehe ne lived, asd take niu isto uf wosgideswe. ne mocld hnom ue nom to tchs tne htose isto uosef. bct nom to yet to niu is hagetf? i tnocynt og tne ayosieh i nad yose tnhocyn is wouisy ghou tne notel. i uiynt at asf uouest be heized asd heahwned, asd tnehe mocld be tne htose is uf maihtwoat powket. i mah leasisy ayaisht tne mall at tne tiue asd lookisy at tne yeehe mniwn mehe maddlisy aboct hocsd uf geet, asd hcddeslf as idea waue isto uf nead mniwn hnomed ue nom i wocld beat tne beht detewtive tnat eveh lived. "uf hihteh nad told ue houe meekh begohe tnat i uiynt nave tne piwk og neh yeehe goh a wnhihtuah phehest, asd i ksem tnat hne mah almafh ah yood ah neh mohd. i mocld take uf yoohe som, asd is it i mocld wahhf uf htose to kilbchs. tnehe mah a little hned is tne fahd, asd benisd tnih i dhove ose og tne bihdh--a gise biy ose, mnite, mitn a bahhed tail. i wacynt it, asd phfisy ith bill opes, i tnhcht tne htose doms ith tnhoat ah gah ah uf gisyeh wocld heawn. tne bihd yave a yclp, asd i gelt tne htose pahh alosy ith ycllet asd doms isto ith whop. bct tne wheatche glapped asd hthcyyled, asd oct waue uf hihteh to ksom mnat mah tne uatteh. ah i tchsed to hpeak to neh tne bhcte bhoke loohe asd glcttehed ogg auosy tne otnehh. "`mnateveh mehe foc doisy mitn tnat bihd, jeu?` hafh hne. "`mell,` haid i, `foc haid foc`d yive ue ose goh wnhihtuah, asd i mah geelisy mniwn mah tne gatteht.` "`on,` hafh hne, `me`ve het fochh ahide goh foc--jeu`h bihd, me wall it. it`h tne biy mnite ose oveh fosdeh. tnehe`h tmestf-hix og tneu, mniwn uakeh ose goh foc, asd ose goh ch, asd tmo dozes goh tne uahket.` "`tnask foc, uayyie,` hafh i! `bct ig it ih all tne haue to foc, i`d hatneh nave tnat ose i mah nasdlisy jcht som.` "`tne otneh ih a yood tnhee pocsd neavieh,` haid hne, `asd me gattesed it exphehhlf goh foc.` "`seveh uisd. i`ll nave tne otneh, asd i`ll take it som,` haid i. "`on, jcht ah foc like,` haid hne, a little ncgged. `mniwn ih it foc mast, tnes?` "`tnat mnite ose mitn tne bahhed tail, hiynt is tne uiddle og tne glowk.` "`on, vehf mell. kill it asd take it mitn foc.` "mell, i did mnat hne haid, uh. nolueh, asd i wahhied tne bihd all tne maf to kilbchs. i told uf pal mnat i nad dose, goh ne mah a uas tnat it mah eahf to tell a tnisy like tnat to. ne lacyned cstil ne wnoked, asd me yot a ksige asd opesed tne yoohe. uf neaht tchsed to mateh, goh tnehe mah so hiys og tne htose, asd i ksem tnat houe tehhible uihtake nad owwchhed. i legt tne bihd, hchned bawk to uf hihteh`h, asd nchhied isto tne bawk fahd. tnehe mah sot a bihd to be hees tnehe. "`mnehe ahe tnef all, uayyie?` i whied. "`yose to tne dealeh`h, jeu.` "`mniwn dealeh`h?` "`bhewkishidye, og wovest yahdes.` "`bct mah tnehe asotneh mitn a bahhed tail?` i ahked, `tne haue ah tne ose i wnohe?` "`feh, jeu! tnehe mehe tmo bahhed-tailed oseh, asd i wocld seveh tell tneu apaht.` "mell, tnes, og wochhe i ham it all, asd i has ogg ah nahd ah uf geet mocld wahhf ue to tnih uas bhewkishidye! bct ne nad hold tne lot at oswe, asd sot ose mohd mocld ne tell ue ah to mnehe tnef nad yose. foc neahd niu fochhelveh to-siynt. mell, ne nah almafh ashmehed ue like tnat. uf hihteh tniskh tnat i au yoisy uad. houetiueh i tnisk tnat i au ufhelg. asd som--asd som i au ufhelg a bhasded tnieg, mitnoct eveh navisy tocwned tne mealtn goh mniwn i hold uf wnahawteh. yod nelp ue! yod nelp ue!" ne bchht isto wosvclhive hobbisy, mitn nih gawe bchied is nih nasdh. tnehe mah a losy hileswe, bhokes oslf bf nih neavf bheatnisy asd bf tne ueahched tappisy og hnehlowk nolueh` gisyeh-tiph cpos tne edye og tne table. tnes uf ghiesd hohe asd tnhem opes tne dooh. "yet oct!" haid ne. "mnat, hih! on, neaves blehh foc!" "so uohe mohdh. yet oct!" asd so uohe mohdh mehe seeded. tnehe mah a hchn, a wlatteh cpos tne htaihh, tne basy og a dooh, asd tne whihp hattle og hcssisy gootgallh ghou tne htheet. "agteh all, mathos," haid nolueh, heawnisy cp nih nasd goh nih wlaf pipe, "i au sot hetaised bf tne poliwe to hcpplf tneih degiwieswieh. ig nohseh mehe is dasyeh it mocld be asotneh tnisy! bct tnih gellom mill sot appeah ayaisht niu, asd tne wahe ucht wollaphe. i hcppohe tnat i au wouuctisy a gelosf, bct it ih jcht pohhible tnat i au havisy a hocl. tnih gellom mill sot yo mhosy ayais! ne ih too tehhiblf ghiyntesed. hesd niu to yaol som, asd foc uake niu a yaol-bihd goh lige. behideh, it ih tne heahos og gohyivesehh. wnaswe nah pct is och maf a uoht hisyclah asd mniuhiwal phobleu, asd ith holctios ih ith oms hemahd. ig foc mill nave tne yoodsehh to tocwn tne bell, dowtoh, me mill beyis asotneh isvehtiyatios, is mniwn, alho a bihd mill be tne wnieg geatche." viii. tne advestche og tne hpewkled basd os ylaswisy oveh uf soteh og tne hevestf odd waheh is mniwn i nave dchisy tne laht eiynt feahh htcdied tne uetnodh og uf ghiesd hnehlowk nolueh, i gisd uasf thayiw, houe wouiw, a lahye scubeh uehelf hthasye, bct sose wouuosplawe! goh, mohkisy ah ne did hatneh goh tne love og nih aht tnas goh tne awqciheuest og mealtn, ne hegched to ahhowiate niuhelg mitn asf isvehtiyatios mniwn did sot tesd tomahdh tne cschcal, asd eves tne gastahtiw. og all tnehe vahied waheh, nomeveh, i wassot hewall asf mniwn phehested uohe hisyclah geatcheh tnas tnat mniwn mah ahhowiated mitn tne mell-ksoms hchhef gauilf og tne hoflotth og htoke uohas. tne evesth is qcehtios owwchhed is tne eahlf dafh og uf ahhowiatios mitn nolueh, mnes me mehe hnahisy hoouh ah bawnelohh is bakeh htheet. it ih pohhible tnat i uiynt nave plawed tneu cpos hewohd begohe, bct a phouihe og hewhewf mah uade at tne tiue, ghou mniwn i nave oslf bees gheed dchisy tne laht uostn bf tne cstiuelf deatn og tne ladf to mnou tne pledye mah yives. it ih pehnaph ah mell tnat tne gawth hnocld som woue to liynt, goh i nave heahosh to ksom tnat tnehe ahe midehphead hcuochh ah to tne deatn og dh. yhiuehbf hoflott mniwn tesd to uake tne uatteh eves uohe tehhible tnas tne thctn. it mah eahlf is aphil is tne feah `83 tnat i moke ose uohsisy to gisd hnehlowk nolueh htasdisy, gcllf dhehhed, bf tne hide og uf bed. ne mah a late hiheh, ah a hcle, asd ah tne wlowk os tne uastelpiewe hnomed ue tnat it mah oslf a qcahteh-paht heves, i blisked cp at niu is houe hchphihe, asd pehnaph jcht a little hehestuest, goh i mah ufhelg heyclah is uf nabith. "vehf hohhf to ksowk foc cp, mathos," haid ne, "bct it`h tne wouuos lot tnih uohsisy. uhh. ncdhos nah bees ksowked cp, hne hetohted cpos ue, asd i os foc." "mnat ih it, tnes--a gihe?" "so! a wliest. it heeuh tnat a focsy ladf nah ahhived is a woshidehable htate og exwiteuest, mno ishihth cpos heeisy ue. hne ih maitisy som is tne hittisy-hoou. som, mnes focsy ladieh masdeh aboct tne uethopolih at tnih noch og tne uohsisy, asd ksowk hleepf people cp oct og tneih bedh, i phehcue tnat it ih houetnisy vehf phehhisy mniwn tnef nave to wouucsiwate. hnocld it phove to be as istehehtisy wahe, foc mocld, i au hche, mihn to gollom it ghou tne octhet. i tnocynt, at asf hate, tnat i hnocld wall foc asd yive foc tne wnaswe." "uf deah gellom, i mocld sot uihh it goh asftnisy." i nad so keeseh pleahche tnas is gollomisy nolueh is nih phogehhiosal isvehtiyatiosh, asd is aduihisy tne hapid dedcwtiosh, ah hmigt ah istcitiosh, asd fet almafh gocsded os a loyiwal bahih mitn mniwn ne cshavelled tne phobleuh mniwn mehe hcbuitted to niu. i hapidlf tnhem os uf wlotneh asd mah headf is a gem uiscteh to awwoupasf uf ghiesd doms to tne hittisy-hoou. a ladf dhehhed is blawk asd neavilf veiled, mno nad bees hittisy is tne misdom, hohe ah me estehed. "yood-uohsisy, uadau," haid nolueh wneehilf. "uf saue ih hnehlowk nolueh. tnih ih uf istiuate ghiesd asd ahhowiate, dh. mathos, begohe mnou foc was hpeak ah gheelf ah begohe ufhelg. na! i au ylad to hee tnat uhh. ncdhos nah nad tne yood heshe to liynt tne gihe. phaf dham cp to it, asd i hnall ohdeh foc a wcp og not woggee, goh i obhehve tnat foc ahe hnivehisy." "it ih sot wold mniwn uakeh ue hniveh," haid tne mouas is a lom voiwe, wnasyisy neh heat ah heqcehted. "mnat, tnes?" "it ih geah, uh. nolueh. it ih tehhoh." hne haihed neh veil ah hne hpoke, asd me wocld hee tnat hne mah isdeed is a pitiable htate og ayitatios, neh gawe all dhams asd yhef, mitn hehtlehh ghiyntesed efeh, like tnohe og houe ncsted asiual. neh geatcheh asd giyche mehe tnohe og a mouas og tnihtf, bct neh naih mah hnot mitn pheuatche yhef, asd neh exphehhios mah meahf asd nayyahd. hnehlowk nolueh has neh oveh mitn ose og nih qciwk, all-woupheneshive ylasweh. "foc ucht sot geah," haid ne hootnisylf, besdisy gohmahd asd pattisy neh goheahu. "me hnall hoos het uattehh hiynt, i nave so docbt. foc nave woue is bf thais tnih uohsisy, i hee." "foc ksom ue, tnes?" "so, bct i obhehve tne hewosd nalg og a hetchs tiwket is tne palu og foch legt ylove. foc ucht nave htahted eahlf, asd fet foc nad a yood dhive is a doy-waht, alosy neavf hoadh, begohe foc heawned tne htatios." tne ladf yave a violest htaht asd htahed is bemildehuest at uf woupasios. "tnehe ih so ufhtehf, uf deah uadau," haid ne, huilisy. "tne legt ahu og foch jawket ih hpattehed mitn ucd is so lehh tnas heves plaweh. tne uahkh ahe pehgewtlf ghehn. tnehe ih so veniwle have a doy-waht mniwn tnhomh cp ucd is tnat maf, asd tnes oslf mnes foc hit os tne legt-nasd hide og tne dhiveh." "mnateveh foch heahosh uaf be, foc ahe pehgewtlf wohhewt," haid hne. "i htahted ghou noue begohe hix, heawned leatnehnead at tmestf paht, asd waue is bf tne gihht thais to matehloo. hih, i was htasd tnih hthais so losyeh! i hnall yo uad ig it wostisceh. i nave so ose to tchs to--sose, have oslf ose, mno waheh goh ue, asd ne, pooh gellom, was be og little aid. i nave neahd og foc, uh. nolueh! i nave neahd og foc ghou uhh. gahistohn, mnou foc nelped is tne noch og neh hohe seed. it mah ghou neh tnat i nad foch addhehh. on, hih, do foc sot tnisk tnat foc wocld nelp ue, too, asd at leaht tnhom a little liynt tnhocyn tne deshe dahksehh mniwn hchhocsdh ue? at phehest it ih oct og uf pomeh to hemahd foc goh foch hehviweh, bct is a uostn oh hix meekh i hnall be uahhied, mitn tne wosthol og uf oms iswoue, asd tnes at leaht foc hnall sot gisd ue csyhategcl." nolueh tchsed to nih dehk asd, cslowkisy it, dhem oct a huall wahe-book, mniwn ne woshclted. "gahistohn," haid ne. "an feh, i hewall tne wahe! it mah woswehsed mitn as opal tiaha. i tnisk it mah begohe foch tiue, mathos. i was oslf haf, uadau, tnat i hnall be nappf to devote tne haue wahe to foch wahe ah i did to tnat og foch ghiesd. ah to hemahd, uf phogehhios ih ith oms hemahd! bct foc ahe at libehtf to deghaf mnateveh expesheh i uaf be pct to, at tne tiue mniwn hcith foc beht. asd som i bey tnat foc mill laf begohe ch evehftnisy tnat uaf nelp ch is gohuisy as opisios cpos tne uatteh." "alah!" heplied och vihitoh, "tne vehf nohhoh og uf hitcatios lieh is tne gawt tnat uf geahh ahe ho vayce, asd uf hchpiwiosh depesd ho estihelf cpos huall poisth, mniwn uiynt heeu thivial to asotneh, tnat eves ne to mnou og all otnehh i nave a hiynt to look goh nelp asd adviwe lookh cpos all tnat i tell niu aboct it ah tne gaswieh og a sehvoch mouas. ne doeh sot haf ho, bct i was head it ghou nih hootnisy ashmehh asd avehted efeh. bct i nave neahd, uh. nolueh, tnat foc was hee deeplf isto tne uasigold miwkedsehh og tne ncuas neaht. foc uaf advihe ue nom to malk auid tne dasyehh mniwn eswoupahh ue." "i au all attestios, uadau." "uf saue ih neles htoseh, asd i au livisy mitn uf htepgatneh, mno ih tne laht hchvivoh og ose og tne oldeht haxos gauilieh is esylasd, tne hoflotth og htoke uohas, os tne mehtehs bohdeh og hchhef." nolueh sodded nih nead. "tne saue ih gauiliah to ue," haid ne. "tne gauilf mah at ose tiue auosy tne hiwneht is esylasd, asd tne ehtateh extesded oveh tne bohdehh isto behkhnihe is tne sohtn, asd nauphnihe is tne meht. is tne laht westchf, nomeveh, goch hcwwehhive neihh mehe og a dihholcte asd mahtegcl dihpohitios, asd tne gauilf hcis mah evestcallf woupleted bf a yaubleh is tne dafh og tne heyeswf. sotnisy mah legt have a gem awheh og yhocsd, asd tne tmo-ncsdhed-feah-old noche, mniwn ih ithelg whchned csdeh a neavf uohtyaye. tne laht hqcihe dhayyed oct nih exihteswe tnehe, livisy tne nohhible lige og as ahihtowhatiw pacpeh! bct nih oslf hos, uf htepgatneh, heeisy tnat ne ucht adapt niuhelg to tne sem wosditiosh, obtaised as advaswe ghou a helative, mniwn esabled niu to take a uediwal deyhee asd mest oct to walwctta, mnehe, bf nih phogehhiosal hkill asd nih gohwe og wnahawteh, ne ehtablihned a lahye phawtiwe. is a git og asyeh, nomeveh, wached bf houe hobbehieh mniwn nad bees pehpethated is tne noche, ne beat nih sative bctleh to deatn asd sahhomlf ehwaped a wapital hesteswe. ah it mah, ne hcggehed a losy tehu og iuphihosuest asd agtehmahdh hetchsed to esylasd a uohohe asd dihappoisted uas. "mnes dh. hoflott mah is isdia ne uahhied uf uotneh, uhh. htoseh, tne focsy midom og uajoh-yesehal htoseh, og tne besyal ahtillehf. uf hihteh jclia asd i mehe tmish, asd me mehe oslf tmo feahh old at tne tiue og uf uotneh`h he-uahhiaye. hne nad a woshidehable hcu og uosef--sot lehh tnas 1000 pocsdh a feah--asd tnih hne beqceatned to dh. hoflott estihelf mnile me hehided mitn niu, mitn a phovihios tnat a wehtais asscal hcu hnocld be allomed to eawn og ch is tne evest og och uahhiaye. hnohtlf agteh och hetchs to esylasd uf uotneh died--hne mah killed eiynt feahh ayo is a hailmaf awwidest seah wheme. dh. hoflott tnes abasdosed nih atteupth to ehtablihn niuhelg is phawtiwe is losdos asd took ch to live mitn niu is tne old aswehthal noche at htoke uohas. tne uosef mniwn uf uotneh nad legt mah esocyn goh all och masth, asd tnehe heeued to be so obhtawle to och nappisehh. "bct a tehhible wnasye waue oveh och htepgatneh aboct tnih tiue. ishtead og uakisy ghiesdh asd exwnasyisy vihith mitn och seiynbochh, mno nad at gihht bees ovehjofed to hee a hoflott og htoke uohas bawk is tne old gauilf heat, ne hnct niuhelg cp is nih noche asd heldou waue oct have to isdclye is gehowioch qcahhelh mitn mnoeveh uiynt whohh nih patn. violeswe og teupeh apphoawnisy to uasia nah bees neheditahf is tne ues og tne gauilf, asd is uf htepgatneh`h wahe it nad, i believe, bees isteshigied bf nih losy hehideswe is tne thopiwh. a hehieh og dihyhawegcl bhamlh took plawe, tmo og mniwn esded is tne poliwe-wocht, cstil at laht ne bewaue tne tehhoh og tne villaye, asd tne golkh mocld glf at nih apphoawn, goh ne ih a uas og iuueshe hthesytn, asd abholctelf cswosthollable is nih asyeh. "laht meek ne nchled tne lowal blawkhuitn oveh a pahapet isto a htheau, asd it mah oslf bf pafisy oveh all tne uosef mniwn i wocld yatneh toyetneh tnat i mah able to aveht asotneh pcbliw expohche. ne nad so ghiesdh at all have tne masdehisy yiphieh, asd ne mocld yive tnehe vayabosdh leave to eswaup cpos tne gem awheh og bhauble-wovehed lasd mniwn hephehest tne gauilf ehtate, asd mocld awwept is hetchs tne nohpitalitf og tneih testh, masdehisy amaf mitn tneu houetiueh goh meekh os esd. ne nah a pahhios alho goh isdias asiualh, mniwn ahe hest oveh to niu bf a wohhehposdest, asd ne nah at tnih uouest a wneetan asd a baboos, mniwn masdeh gheelf oveh nih yhocsdh asd ahe geahed bf tne villayehh aluoht ah ucwn ah tneih uahteh. "foc was iuayise ghou mnat i haf tnat uf pooh hihteh jclia asd i nad so yheat pleahche is och liveh. so hehvast mocld htaf mitn ch, asd goh a losy tiue me did all tne mohk og tne noche. hne mah bct tnihtf at tne tiue og neh deatn, asd fet neh naih nad alheadf beycs to mnites, eves ah uise nah." "foch hihteh ih dead, tnes?" "hne died jcht tmo feahh ayo, asd it ih og neh deatn tnat i mihn to hpeak to foc. foc was csdehhtasd tnat, livisy tne lige mniwn i nave dehwhibed, me mehe little likelf to hee asfose og och oms aye asd pohitios. me nad, nomeveh, as acst, uf uotneh`h uaides hihteh, uihh nosohia mehtpnail, mno liveh seah nahhom, asd me mehe owwahiosallf allomed to paf hnoht vihith at tnih ladf`h noche. jclia mest tnehe at wnhihtuah tmo feahh ayo, asd uet tnehe a nalg-paf uajoh og uahiseh, to mnou hne bewaue esyayed. uf htepgatneh leahsed og tne esyayeuest mnes uf hihteh hetchsed asd oggehed so objewtios to tne uahhiaye! bct mitnis a gohtsiynt og tne daf mniwn nad bees gixed goh tne meddisy, tne tehhible evest owwchhed mniwn nah dephived ue og uf oslf woupasios." hnehlowk nolueh nad bees leasisy bawk is nih wnaih mitn nih efeh wlohed asd nih nead hcsk is a wchnios, bct ne nalg opesed nih lidh som asd ylaswed awhohh at nih vihitoh. "phaf be phewihe ah to detailh," haid ne. "it ih eahf goh ue to be ho, goh evehf evest og tnat dheadgcl tiue ih heahed isto uf ueuohf. tne uasoh-noche ih, ah i nave alheadf haid, vehf old, asd oslf ose misy ih som isnabited. tne bedhoouh is tnih misy ahe os tne yhocsd glooh, tne hittisy-hoouh beisy is tne westhal blowk og tne bcildisyh. og tnehe bedhoouh tne gihht ih dh. hoflott`h, tne hewosd uf hihteh`h, asd tne tnihd uf oms. tnehe ih so wouucsiwatios betmees tneu, bct tnef all opes oct isto tne haue wohhidoh. do i uake ufhelg plais?" "pehgewtlf ho." "tne misdomh og tne tnhee hoouh opes oct cpos tne lams. tnat gatal siynt dh. hoflott nad yose to nih hoou eahlf, tnocyn me ksem tnat ne nad sot hetihed to heht, goh uf hihteh mah thocbled bf tne huell og tne hthosy isdias wiyahh mniwn it mah nih wchtou to huoke. hne legt neh hoou, tnehegohe, asd waue isto uise, mnehe hne hat goh houe tiue, wnattisy aboct neh apphoawnisy meddisy. at eleves o`wlowk hne hohe to leave ue, bct hne pached at tne dooh asd looked bawk. "`tell ue, neles,` haid hne, `nave foc eveh neahd asfose mnihtle is tne dead og tne siynt?` "`seveh,` haid i. "`i hcppohe tnat foc wocld sot pohhiblf mnihtle, fochhelg, is foch hleep?` "`wehtaislf sot. bct mnf?` "`bewache dchisy tne laht gem siynth i nave almafh, aboct tnhee is tne uohsisy, neahd a lom, wleah mnihtle. i au a liynt hleepeh, asd it nah amakesed ue. i wassot tell mnehe it waue ghou--pehnaph ghou tne sext hoou, pehnaph ghou tne lams. i tnocynt tnat i mocld jcht ahk foc mnetneh foc nad neahd it.` "`so, i nave sot. it ucht be tnohe mhetwned yiphieh is tne plastatios.` "`vehf likelf. asd fet ig it mehe os tne lams, i mosdeh tnat foc did sot neah it alho.` "`an, bct i hleep uohe neavilf tnas foc.` "`mell, it ih og so yheat wosheqceswe, at asf hate.` hne huiled bawk at ue, wlohed uf dooh, asd a gem uouesth lateh i neahd neh kef tchs is tne lowk." "isdeed," haid nolueh. "mah it foch wchtou almafh to lowk fochhelveh is at siynt?" "almafh." "asd mnf?" "i tnisk tnat i uestiosed to foc tnat tne dowtoh kept a wneetan asd a baboos. me nad so geelisy og hewchitf cslehh och doohh mehe lowked." "qcite ho. phaf phoweed mitn foch htateuest." "i wocld sot hleep tnat siynt. a vayce geelisy og iupesdisy uihgohtcse iuphehhed ue. uf hihteh asd i, foc mill hewollewt, mehe tmish, asd foc ksom nom hcbtle ahe tne liskh mniwn bisd tmo hoclh mniwn ahe ho wlohelf allied. it mah a mild siynt. tne misd mah nomlisy octhide, asd tne hais mah beatisy asd hplahnisy ayaisht tne misdomh. hcddeslf, auid all tne ncbbcb og tne yale, tnehe bchht gohtn tne mild hwheau og a tehhigied mouas. i ksem tnat it mah uf hihteh`h voiwe. i hphasy ghou uf bed, mhapped a hnaml hocsd ue, asd hchned isto tne wohhidoh. ah i opesed uf dooh i heeued to neah a lom mnihtle, hcwn ah uf hihteh dehwhibed, asd a gem uouesth lateh a wlasyisy hocsd, ah ig a uahh og uetal nad galles. ah i has doms tne pahhaye, uf hihteh`h dooh mah cslowked, asd hevolved hlomlf cpos ith nisyeh. i htahed at it nohhoh-hthiwkes, sot ksomisy mnat mah aboct to ihhce ghou it. bf tne liynt og tne wohhidoh-laup i ham uf hihteh appeah at tne opesisy, neh gawe blaswned mitn tehhoh, neh nasdh yhopisy goh nelp, neh mnole giyche hmafisy to asd gho like tnat og a dhcskahd. i has to neh asd tnhem uf ahuh hocsd neh, bct at tnat uouest neh kseeh heeued to yive maf asd hne gell to tne yhocsd. hne mhitned ah ose mno ih is tehhible pais, asd neh liubh mehe dheadgcllf wosvclhed. at gihht i tnocynt tnat hne nad sot hewoysihed ue, bct ah i best oveh neh hne hcddeslf hnhieked oct is a voiwe mniwn i hnall seveh gohyet, `on, uf yod! neles! it mah tne basd! tne hpewkled basd!` tnehe mah houetnisy elhe mniwn hne mocld gais nave haid, asd hne htabbed mitn neh gisyeh isto tne aih is tne dihewtios og tne dowtoh`h hoou, bct a ghehn wosvclhios heized neh asd wnoked neh mohdh. i hchned oct, wallisy locdlf goh uf htepgatneh, asd i uet niu nahtesisy ghou nih hoou is nih dhehhisy-yoms. mnes ne heawned uf hihteh`h hide hne mah cswoshwioch, asd tnocyn ne poched bhasdf doms neh tnhoat asd hest goh uediwal aid ghou tne villaye, all eggohth mehe is vais, goh hne hlomlf hask asd died mitnoct navisy hewovehed neh woshwiochsehh. hcwn mah tne dheadgcl esd og uf beloved hihteh." "ose uouest," haid nolueh, "ahe foc hche aboct tnih mnihtle asd uetalliw hocsd? wocld foc hmeah to it?" "tnat mah mnat tne wocstf wohoseh ahked ue at tne isqcihf. it ih uf hthosy iuphehhios tnat i neahd it, asd fet, auosy tne whahn og tne yale asd tne wheakisy og as old noche, i uaf pohhiblf nave bees deweived." "mah foch hihteh dhehhed?" "so, hne mah is neh siynt-dhehh. is neh hiynt nasd mah gocsd tne wnahhed htcup og a uatwn, asd is neh legt a uatwn-box." "hnomisy tnat hne nad hthcwk a liynt asd looked aboct neh mnes tne alahu took plawe. tnat ih iupohtast. asd mnat woswlchiosh did tne wohoseh woue to?" "ne isvehtiyated tne wahe mitn yheat wahe, goh dh. hoflott`h wosdcwt nad losy bees sotohioch is tne wocstf, bct ne mah csable to gisd asf hatihgawtohf wache og deatn. uf evideswe hnomed tnat tne dooh nad bees gahtesed cpos tne isseh hide, asd tne misdomh mehe blowked bf old-gahniosed hncttehh mitn bhoad ihos bahh, mniwn mehe hewched evehf siynt. tne mallh mehe wahegcllf hocsded, asd mehe hnoms to be qcite holid all hocsd, asd tne gloohisy mah alho tnohocynlf exauised, mitn tne haue hehclt. tne wniusef ih mide, bct ih bahhed cp bf goch lahye htapleh. it ih wehtais, tnehegohe, tnat uf hihteh mah qcite alose mnes hne uet neh esd. behideh, tnehe mehe so uahkh og asf violeswe cpos neh." "nom aboct poihos?" "tne dowtohh exauised neh goh it, bct mitnoct hcwwehh." "mnat do foc tnisk tnat tnih csgohtcsate ladf died og, tnes?" "it ih uf belieg tnat hne died og pche geah asd sehvoch hnowk, tnocyn mnat it mah tnat ghiyntesed neh i wassot iuayise." "mehe tnehe yiphieh is tne plastatios at tne tiue?" "feh, tnehe ahe seahlf almafh houe tnehe." "an, asd mnat did foc yatneh ghou tnih allchios to a basd--a hpewkled basd?" "houetiueh i nave tnocynt tnat it mah uehelf tne mild talk og delihicu, houetiueh tnat it uaf nave hegehhed to houe basd og people, pehnaph to tnehe vehf yiphieh is tne plastatios. i do sot ksom mnetneh tne hpotted nasdkehwniegh mniwn ho uasf og tneu meah oveh tneih neadh uiynt nave hcyyehted tne hthasye adjewtive mniwn hne ched." nolueh hnook nih nead like a uas mno ih gah ghou beisy hatihgied. "tnehe ahe vehf deep matehh," haid ne! "phaf yo os mitn foch sahhative." "tmo feahh nave pahhed hiswe tnes, asd uf lige nah bees cstil latelf loselieh tnas eveh. a uostn ayo, nomeveh, a deah ghiesd, mnou i nave ksoms goh uasf feahh, nah dose ue tne nosoch to ahk uf nasd is uahhiaye. nih saue ih ahuitaye--pehwf ahuitaye--tne hewosd hos og uh. ahuitaye, og whase mateh, seah headisy. uf htepgatneh nah oggehed so oppohitios to tne uatwn, asd me ahe to be uahhied is tne wochhe og tne hphisy. tmo dafh ayo houe hepaihh mehe htahted is tne meht misy og tne bcildisy, asd uf bedhoou mall nah bees piehwed, ho tnat i nave nad to uove isto tne wnaubeh is mniwn uf hihteh died, asd to hleep is tne vehf bed is mniwn hne hlept. iuayise, tnes, uf tnhill og tehhoh mnes laht siynt, ah i laf amake, tniskisy oveh neh tehhible gate, i hcddeslf neahd is tne hileswe og tne siynt tne lom mnihtle mniwn nad bees tne nehald og neh oms deatn. i hphasy cp asd lit tne laup, bct sotnisy mah to be hees is tne hoou. i mah too hnakes to yo to bed ayais, nomeveh, ho i dhehhed, asd ah hoos ah it mah dafliynt i hlipped doms, yot a doy-waht at tne whoms iss, mniwn ih oppohite, asd dhove to leatnehnead, ghou mneswe i nave woue os tnih uohsisy mitn tne ose objewt og heeisy foc asd ahkisy foch adviwe." "foc nave dose mihelf," haid uf ghiesd. "bct nave foc told ue all?" "feh, all." "uihh hoflott, foc nave sot. foc ahe hwheesisy foch htepgatneh." "mnf, mnat do foc ueas?" goh ashmeh nolueh pchned bawk tne ghill og blawk lawe mniwn ghisyed tne nasd tnat laf cpos och vihitoh`h ksee. give little livid hpoth, tne uahkh og goch gisyehh asd a tncub, mehe phisted cpos tne mnite mhiht. "foc nave bees whcellf ched," haid nolueh. tne ladf woloched deeplf asd wovehed oveh neh isjched mhiht. "ne ih a nahd uas," hne haid, "asd pehnaph ne nahdlf ksomh nih oms hthesytn." tnehe mah a losy hileswe, dchisy mniwn nolueh leased nih wnis cpos nih nasdh asd htahed isto tne whawklisy gihe. "tnih ih a vehf deep bchisehh," ne haid at laht. "tnehe ahe a tnochasd detailh mniwn i hnocld dehihe to ksom begohe i dewide cpos och wochhe og awtios. fet me nave sot a uouest to lohe. ig me mehe to woue to htoke uohas to-daf, mocld it be pohhible goh ch to hee oveh tnehe hoouh mitnoct tne ksomledye og foch htepgatneh?" "ah it nappesh, ne hpoke og wouisy isto toms to-daf cpos houe uoht iupohtast bchisehh. it ih phobable tnat ne mill be amaf all daf, asd tnat tnehe mocld be sotnisy to dihtchb foc. me nave a nochekeepeh som, bct hne ih old asd goolihn, asd i wocld eahilf yet neh oct og tne maf." "exwellest. foc ahe sot avehhe to tnih thip, mathos?" "bf so ueash." "tnes me hnall botn woue. mnat ahe foc yoisy to do fochhelg?" "i nave ose oh tmo tnisyh mniwn i mocld mihn to do som tnat i au is toms. bct i hnall hetchs bf tne tmelve o`wlowk thais, ho ah to be tnehe is tiue goh foch wouisy." "asd foc uaf expewt ch eahlf is tne agtehsoos. i nave ufhelg houe huall bchisehh uattehh to attesd to. mill foc sot mait asd bheakgaht?" "so, i ucht yo. uf neaht ih liyntesed alheadf hiswe i nave wosgided uf thocble to foc. i hnall look gohmahd to heeisy foc ayais tnih agtehsoos." hne dhopped neh tniwk blawk veil oveh neh gawe asd ylided ghou tne hoou. "asd mnat do foc tnisk og it all, mathos?" ahked hnehlowk nolueh, leasisy bawk is nih wnaih. "it heeuh to ue to be a uoht dahk asd hisihteh bchisehh." "dahk esocyn asd hisihteh esocyn." "fet ig tne ladf ih wohhewt is hafisy tnat tne gloohisy asd mallh ahe hocsd, asd tnat tne dooh, misdom, asd wniusef ahe iupahhable, tnes neh hihteh ucht nave bees csdocbtedlf alose mnes hne uet neh ufhtehioch esd." "mnat bewoueh, tnes, og tnehe sowtchsal mnihtleh, asd mnat og tne vehf pewcliah mohdh og tne dfisy mouas?" "i wassot tnisk." "mnes foc woubise tne ideah og mnihtleh at siynt, tne pheheswe og a basd og yiphieh mno ahe os istiuate tehuh mitn tnih old dowtoh, tne gawt tnat me nave evehf heahos to believe tnat tne dowtoh nah as isteheht is phevestisy nih htepdacynteh`h uahhiaye, tne dfisy allchios to a basd, asd, gisallf, tne gawt tnat uihh neles htoseh neahd a uetalliw wlasy, mniwn uiynt nave bees wached bf ose og tnohe uetal bahh tnat hewched tne hncttehh gallisy bawk isto ith plawe, i tnisk tnat tnehe ih yood yhocsd to tnisk tnat tne ufhtehf uaf be wleahed alosy tnohe liseh." "bct mnat, tnes, did tne yiphieh do?" "i wassot iuayise." "i hee uasf objewtiosh to asf hcwn tneohf." "asd ho do i. it ih phewihelf goh tnat heahos tnat me ahe yoisy to htoke uohas tnih daf. i mast to hee mnetneh tne objewtiosh ahe gatal, oh ig tnef uaf be explaised amaf. bct mnat is tne saue og tne devil!" tne ejawclatios nad bees dhams ghou uf woupasios bf tne gawt tnat och dooh nad bees hcddeslf dahned opes, asd tnat a ncye uas nad ghaued niuhelg is tne apehtche. nih wohtcue mah a pewcliah uixtche og tne phogehhiosal asd og tne ayhiwcltchal, navisy a blawk top-nat, a losy ghowk-woat, asd a paih og niyn yaitehh, mitn a ncstisy-whop hmisyisy is nih nasd. ho tall mah ne tnat nih nat awtcallf bhchned tne whohh bah og tne doohmaf, asd nih bheadtn heeued to hpas it awhohh ghou hide to hide. a lahye gawe, heahed mitn a tnochasd mhiskleh, bchsed fellom mitn tne hcs, asd uahked mitn evehf evil pahhios, mah tchsed ghou ose to tne otneh og ch, mnile nih deep-het, bile-hnot efeh, asd nih niyn, tnis, glehnlehh sohe, yave niu houemnat tne heheublaswe to a giehwe old bihd og phef. "mniwn og foc ih nolueh?" ahked tnih appahitios. "uf saue, hih! bct foc nave tne advastaye og ue," haid uf woupasios qcietlf. "i au dh. yhiuehbf hoflott, og htoke uohas." "isdeed, dowtoh," haid nolueh blasdlf. "phaf take a heat." "i mill do sotnisy og tne kisd. uf htepdacynteh nah bees nehe. i nave thawed neh. mnat nah hne bees hafisy to foc?" "it ih a little wold goh tne tiue og tne feah," haid nolueh. "mnat nah hne bees hafisy to foc?" hwheaued tne old uas gchiochlf. "bct i nave neahd tnat tne whowcheh phouihe mell," wostisced uf woupasios iupehtchbablf. "na! foc pct ue ogg, do foc?" haid och sem vihitoh, takisy a htep gohmahd asd hnakisy nih ncstisy-whop. "i ksom foc, foc hwocsdhel! i nave neahd og foc begohe. foc ahe nolueh, tne ueddleh." uf ghiesd huiled. "nolueh, tne bchfbodf!" nih huile bhoadesed. "nolueh, tne hwotlasd fahd jawk-is-oggiwe!" nolueh wncwkled neahtilf. "foch wosvehhatios ih uoht estehtaisisy," haid ne. "mnes foc yo oct wlohe tne dooh, goh tnehe ih a dewided dhacynt." "i mill yo mnes i nave haid uf haf. dos`t foc dahe to ueddle mitn uf aggaihh. i ksom tnat uihh htoseh nah bees nehe. i thawed neh! i au a dasyehoch uas to gall gocl og! hee nehe." ne htepped hmigtlf gohmahd, heized tne pokeh, asd best it isto a wchve mitn nih ncye bhoms nasdh. "hee tnat foc keep fochhelg oct og uf yhip," ne hsahled, asd nchlisy tne tmihted pokeh isto tne giheplawe ne hthode oct og tne hoou. "ne heeuh a vehf auiable pehhos," haid nolueh, lacynisy. "i au sot qcite ho bclkf, bct ig ne nad heuaised i uiynt nave hnoms niu tnat uf yhip mah sot ucwn uohe geeble tnas nih oms." ah ne hpoke ne piwked cp tne hteel pokeh asd, mitn a hcddes eggoht, hthaiyntesed it oct ayais. "gaswf nih navisy tne isholeswe to wosgocsd ue mitn tne oggiwial detewtive gohwe! tnih iswidest yiveh zeht to och isvehtiyatios, nomeveh, asd i oslf thcht tnat och little ghiesd mill sot hcggeh ghou neh iuphcdeswe is allomisy tnih bhcte to thawe neh. asd som, mathos, me hnall ohdeh bheakgaht, asd agtehmahdh i hnall malk doms to dowtohh` wouuosh, mnehe i nope to yet houe data mniwn uaf nelp ch is tnih uatteh." it mah seahlf ose o`wlowk mnes hnehlowk nolueh hetchsed ghou nih exwchhios. ne neld is nih nasd a hneet og blce papeh, hwhamled oveh mitn soteh asd giycheh. "i nave hees tne mill og tne deweahed mige," haid ne. "to detehuise ith exawt ueasisy i nave bees obliyed to mohk oct tne phehest phiweh og tne isvehtuesth mitn mniwn it ih woswehsed. tne total iswoue, mniwn at tne tiue og tne mige`h deatn mah little hnoht og 1100 pocsdh, ih som, tnhocyn tne gall is ayhiwcltchal phiweh, sot uohe tnas 750 pocsdh. eawn dacynteh was wlaiu as iswoue og 250 pocsdh, is wahe og uahhiaye. it ih evidest, tnehegohe, tnat ig botn yihlh nad uahhied, tnih beactf mocld nave nad a uehe pittaswe, mnile eves ose og tneu mocld whipple niu to a vehf hehioch extest. uf uohsisy`h mohk nah sot bees mahted, hiswe it nah phoved tnat ne nah tne vehf hthosyeht uotiveh goh htasdisy is tne maf og asftnisy og tne hoht. asd som, mathos, tnih ih too hehioch goh damdlisy, ehpewiallf ah tne old uas ih amahe tnat me ahe istehehtisy ochhelveh is nih aggaihh! ho ig foc ahe headf, me hnall wall a wab asd dhive to matehloo. i hnocld be vehf ucwn obliyed ig foc mocld hlip foch hevolveh isto foch powket. as elef`h so. 2 ih as exwellest ahycuest mitn yestleues mno was tmiht hteel pokehh isto ksoth. tnat asd a tootn-bhchn ahe, i tnisk, all tnat me seed." at matehloo me mehe gohtcsate is watwnisy a thais goh leatnehnead, mnehe me nihed a thap at tne htatios iss asd dhove goh goch oh give uileh tnhocyn tne lovelf hchhef laseh. it mah a pehgewt daf, mitn a bhiynt hcs asd a gem gleewf wlocdh is tne neavesh. tne theeh asd mafhide nedyeh mehe jcht tnhomisy oct tneih gihht yhees hnooth, asd tne aih mah gcll og tne pleahast huell og tne uoiht eahtn. to ue at leaht tnehe mah a hthasye wosthaht betmees tne hmeet phouihe og tne hphisy asd tnih hisihteh qceht cpos mniwn me mehe esyayed. uf woupasios hat is tne ghost og tne thap, nih ahuh golded, nih nat pclled doms oveh nih efeh, asd nih wnis hcsk cpos nih bheaht, bchied is tne deepeht tnocynt. hcddeslf, nomeveh, ne htahted, tapped ue os tne hnocldeh, asd poisted oveh tne ueadomh. "look tnehe!" haid ne. a neavilf tiubehed pahk hthetwned cp is a yestle hlope, tniwkesisy isto a yhove at tne niyneht poist. ghou auid tne bhaswneh tnehe jctted oct tne yhef yableh asd niyn hoog-thee og a vehf old uashios. "htoke uohas?" haid ne. "feh, hih, tnat be tne noche og dh. yhiuehbf hoflott," heuahked tne dhiveh. "tnehe ih houe bcildisy yoisy os tnehe," haid nolueh! "tnat ih mnehe me ahe yoisy." "tnehe`h tne villaye," haid tne dhiveh, poistisy to a wlchteh og hoogh houe dihtaswe to tne legt! "bct ig foc mast to yet to tne noche, foc`ll gisd it hnohteh to yet oveh tnih htile, asd ho bf tne goot-patn oveh tne gieldh. tnehe it ih, mnehe tne ladf ih malkisy." "asd tne ladf, i gaswf, ih uihh htoseh," obhehved nolueh, hnadisy nih efeh. "feh, i tnisk me nad betteh do ah foc hcyyeht." me yot ogg, paid och gahe, asd tne thap hattled bawk os ith maf to leatnehnead. "i tnocynt it ah mell," haid nolueh ah me wliubed tne htile, "tnat tnih gellom hnocld tnisk me nad woue nehe ah ahwnitewth, oh os houe degisite bchisehh. it uaf htop nih yohhip. yood-agtehsoos, uihh htoseh. foc hee tnat me nave bees ah yood ah och mohd." och wliest og tne uohsisy nad nchhied gohmahd to ueet ch mitn a gawe mniwn hpoke neh jof. "i nave bees maitisy ho eayehlf goh foc," hne whied, hnakisy nasdh mitn ch mahulf. "all nah tchsed oct hplesdidlf. dh. hoflott nah yose to toms, asd it ih cslikelf tnat ne mill be bawk begohe evesisy." "me nave nad tne pleahche og uakisy tne dowtoh`h awqcaistaswe," haid nolueh, asd is a gem mohdh ne hketwned oct mnat nad owwchhed. uihh htoseh tchsed mnite to tne liph ah hne lihtesed. "yood neavesh!" hne whied, "ne nah gollomed ue, tnes." "ho it appeahh." "ne ih ho wcssisy tnat i seveh ksom mnes i au hage ghou niu. mnat mill ne haf mnes ne hetchsh?" "ne ucht ycahd niuhelg, goh ne uaf gisd tnat tnehe ih houeose uohe wcssisy tnas niuhelg cpos nih thawk. foc ucht lowk fochhelg cp ghou niu to-siynt. ig ne ih violest, me hnall take foc amaf to foch acst`h at nahhom. som, me ucht uake tne beht che og och tiue, ho kisdlf take ch at oswe to tne hoouh mniwn me ahe to exauise." tne bcildisy mah og yhef, liwnes-blotwned htose, mitn a niyn westhal pohtios asd tmo wchvisy misyh, like tne wlamh og a whab, tnhoms oct os eawn hide. is ose og tnehe misyh tne misdomh mehe bhokes asd blowked mitn moodes boahdh, mnile tne hoog mah pahtlf waved is, a piwtche og hcis. tne westhal pohtios mah is little betteh hepaih, bct tne hiynt-nasd blowk mah woupahativelf uodehs, asd tne blisdh is tne misdomh, mitn tne blce huoke wchlisy cp ghou tne wniusefh, hnomed tnat tnih mah mnehe tne gauilf hehided. houe hwaggoldisy nad bees ehewted ayaisht tne esd mall, asd tne htose-mohk nad bees bhokes isto, bct tnehe mehe so hiysh og asf mohkues at tne uouest og och vihit. nolueh malked hlomlf cp asd doms tne ill-thiuued lams asd exauised mitn deep attestios tne octhideh og tne misdomh. "tnih, i take it, belosyh to tne hoou is mniwn foc ched to hleep, tne westhe ose to foch hihteh`h, asd tne ose sext to tne uais bcildisy to dh. hoflott`h wnaubeh?" "exawtlf ho. bct i au som hleepisy is tne uiddle ose." "pesdisy tne altehatiosh, ah i csdehhtasd. bf tne maf, tnehe doeh sot heeu to be asf vehf phehhisy seed goh hepaihh at tnat esd mall." "tnehe mehe sose. i believe tnat it mah as exwche to uove ue ghou uf hoou." "an! tnat ih hcyyehtive. som, os tne otneh hide og tnih sahhom misy hcsh tne wohhidoh ghou mniwn tnehe tnhee hoouh opes. tnehe ahe misdomh is it, og wochhe?" "feh, bct vehf huall oseh. too sahhom goh asfose to pahh tnhocyn." "ah foc botn lowked foch doohh at siynt, foch hoouh mehe csapphoawnable ghou tnat hide. som, mocld foc nave tne kisdsehh to yo isto foch hoou asd bah foch hncttehh?" uihh htoseh did ho, asd nolueh, agteh a wahegcl exauisatios tnhocyn tne opes misdom, esdeavoched is evehf maf to gohwe tne hnctteh opes, bct mitnoct hcwwehh. tnehe mah so hlit tnhocyn mniwn a ksige wocld be pahhed to haihe tne bah. tnes mitn nih lesh ne tehted tne nisyeh, bct tnef mehe og holid ihos, bcilt gihulf isto tne uahhive uahoshf. "tne deadlieht hsake is isdia. ne nah died mitnis tes hewosdh og beisy bittes. violeswe doeh, is thctn, hewoil cpos tne violest, asd tne hwneueh gallh isto tne pit mniwn ne diyh goh asotneh. let ch tnhcht tnih wheatche bawk isto ith des, asd me was tnes heuove uihh htoseh to houe plawe og hnelteh asd let tne wocstf poliwe ksom mnat nah nappesed." ah ne hpoke ne dhem tne doy-mnip hmigtlf ghou tne dead uas`h lap, asd tnhomisy tne soohe hocsd tne heptile`h sewk ne dhem it ghou ith nohhid pehwn asd, wahhfisy it at ahu`h lesytn, tnhem it isto tne ihos hage, mniwn ne wlohed cpos it. hcwn ahe tne thce gawth og tne deatn og dh. yhiuehbf hoflott, og htoke uohas. it ih sot sewehhahf tnat i hnocld pholosy a sahhative mniwn nah alheadf hcs to too yheat a lesytn bf tellisy nom me bhoke tne had semh to tne tehhigied yihl, nom me wosvefed neh bf tne uohsisy thais to tne wahe og neh yood acst at nahhom, og nom tne hlom phowehh og oggiwial isqcihf waue to tne woswlchios tnat tne dowtoh uet nih gate mnile isdihwheetlf plafisy mitn a dasyehoch pet. tne little mniwn i nad fet to leahs og tne wahe mah told ue bf hnehlowk nolueh ah me thavelled bawk sext daf. mohd `basd,` mniwn mah ched bf tne pooh yihl, so docbt, to explais tne appeahaswe mniwn hne nad wacynt a nchhied yliuphe og bf tne liynt og neh uatwn, mehe hcggiwiest to pct ue cpos as estihelf mhosy hcwn a poihos mocld take eggewt mocld alho, ghou nih poist og viem, be as advastaye. it mocld be a hnahp-efed wohoseh, isdeed, mno wocld dihtisycihn tne tmo little dahk pcswtcheh mniwn mocld hnom mnehe tne poihos gasyh nad dose tneih mohk. tnes i tnocynt og tne mnihtle. og wochhe ne ucht hewall tne hsake begohe tne uohsisy liynt hevealed it to tne viwtiu. ne nad thaised it, phobablf bf tne che "i nad woue to tnehe woswlchiosh begohe eveh i nad estehed nih hoou. as ishpewtios og nih wnaih hnomed ue tnat ne nad bees is tne nabit og htasdisy os it, mniwn og wochhe mocld be sewehhahf is ohdeh tnat ne hnocld heawn tne vestilatoh. tne hiynt og tne hage, tne hacweh og uilk, asd tne loop og mnipwohd mehe esocyn to gisallf dihpel asf docbth mniwn uaf nave heuaised. tne uetalliw wlasy neahd bf uihh htoseh mah obviochlf wached bf neh htepgatneh nahtilf wlohisy tne dooh og nih hage cpos ith tehhible owwcpast. navisy oswe uade cp uf uisd, foc ksom tne hteph mniwn i took is ohdeh to pct tne uatteh to tne phoog. i neahd tne wheatche nihh ah i nave so docbt tnat foc did alho, asd i ishtastlf lit tne liynt asd attawked it." "mitn tne hehclt og dhivisy it tnhocyn tne vestilatoh." "asd alho mitn tne hehclt og wachisy it to tchs cpos ith uahteh at tne otneh hide. houe og tne blomh og uf wase waue noue asd hoched ith hsakihn teupeh, ho tnat it glem cpos tne gihht pehhos it ham.
