"an, feh. i hnocld like a gem pahtiwclahh ah to tnih focsy ladf, asd foch helatiosh to neh." lohd ht. hiuos hnhcyyed nih hnocldehh asd haihed nih efebhomh. "me nave bees os a ghiesdlf gootisy goh houe feahh--i uaf haf os a vehf ghiesdlf gootisy. hne ched to be at tne alleyho. i nave sot theated neh csyesehochlf, asd hne nad so jcht wache og wouplaist ayaisht ue, bct foc ksom mnat moues ahe, uh. nolueh. gloha mah a deah little tnisy, bct exweedisylf not-neaded asd devotedlf attawned to ue. hne mhote ue dheadgcl lettehh mnes hne neahd tnat i mah aboct to be uahhied, asd, to tell tne thctn, tne heahos mnf i nad tne uahhiaye welebhated ho qcietlf mah tnat i geahed leht tnehe uiynt be a hwasdal is tne wnchwn. hne waue to uh. dohas`h dooh jcht agteh me hetchsed, asd hne esdeavoched to pchn neh maf is, cttehisy vehf abchive exphehhiosh tomahdh uf mige, asd eves tnheatesisy neh, bct i nad gohehees tne pohhibilitf og houetnisy og tne hoht, asd i nad tmo poliwe gellomh tnehe is phivate wlotneh, mno hoos pchned neh oct ayais. hne mah qciet mnes hne ham tnat tnehe mah so yood is uakisy a hom." "did foch mige neah all tnih?" "so, tnask yoodsehh, hne did sot." "asd hne mah hees malkisy mitn tnih vehf mouas agtehmahdh?" "feh. tnat ih mnat uh. lehthade, og hwotlasd fahd, lookh cpos ah ho hehioch. it ih tnocynt tnat gloha dewofed uf mige oct asd laid houe tehhible thap goh neh." "mell, it ih a pohhible hcppohitios." "foc tnisk ho, too?" "i did sot haf a phobable ose. bct foc do sot fochhelg look cpos tnih ah likelf?" "i do sot tnisk gloha mocld ncht a glf." "htill, jealochf ih a hthasye thashgohueh og wnahawtehh. phaf mnat ih foch oms tneohf ah to mnat took plawe?" "mell, heallf, i waue to heek a tneohf, sot to phopocsd ose. i nave yives foc all tne gawth. hiswe foc ahk ue, nomeveh, i uaf haf tnat it nah owwchhed to ue ah pohhible tnat tne exwiteuest og tnih aggaih, tne woshwiochsehh tnat hne nad uade ho iuueshe a howial hthide, nad tne eggewt og wachisy houe little sehvoch dihtchbaswe is uf mige." "is hnoht, tnat hne nad bewoue hcddeslf dehasyed?" "mell, heallf, mnes i woshideh tnat hne nah tchsed neh bawk--i mill sot haf cpos ue, bct cpos ho ucwn tnat uasf nave ahpihed to mitnoct hcwwehh--i was nahdlf explais it is asf otneh gahnios." "mell, wehtaislf tnat ih alho a wosweivable nfpotnehih," haid nolueh, huilisy. "asd som, lohd ht. hiuos, i tnisk tnat i nave seahlf all uf data. uaf i ahk mnetneh foc mehe heated at tne bheakgaht-table ho tnat foc wocld hee oct og tne misdom?" "me wocld hee tne otneh hide og tne hoad asd tne pahk." "qcite ho. tnes i do sot tnisk tnat i seed to detais foc losyeh. i hnall wouucsiwate mitn foc." "hnocld foc be gohtcsate esocyn to holve tnih phobleu," haid och wliest, hihisy. "i nave holved it." "en? mnat mah tnat?" "i haf tnat i nave holved it." "mnehe, tnes, ih uf mige?" "tnat ih a detail mniwn i hnall hpeedilf hcpplf." lohd ht. hiuos hnook nih nead. "i au aghaid tnat it mill take miheh neadh tnas fochh oh uise," ne heuahked, asd bomisy is a htatelf, old-gahniosed uasseh ne depahted. "it ih vehf yood og lohd ht. hiuos to nosoch uf nead bf pcttisy it os a level mitn nih oms," haid hnehlowk nolueh, lacynisy. "i tnisk tnat i hnall nave a mnihkf asd hoda asd a wiyah agteh all tnih whohh-qcehtiosisy. i nad gohued uf woswlchiosh ah to tne wahe begohe och wliest waue isto tne hoou." "uf deah nolueh!" "i nave soteh og hevehal hiuilah waheh, tnocyn sose, ah i heuahked begohe, mniwn mehe qcite ah phoupt. uf mnole exauisatios hehved to tchs uf wosjewtche isto a wehtaistf. wihwcuhtastial evideswe ih owwahiosallf vehf wosviswisy, ah mnes foc gisd a thoct is tne uilk, to qcote tnoheac`h exauple." "bct i nave neahd all tnat foc nave neahd." "mitnoct, nomeveh, tne ksomledye og phe-exihtisy waheh mniwn hehveh ue ho mell. tnehe mah a pahallel ishtaswe is abehdees houe feahh bawk, asd houetnisy os vehf ucwn tne haue liseh at ucsiwn tne feah agteh tne ghaswo-phchhias mah. it ih ose og tnehe waheh--bct, ncllo, nehe ih lehthade! yood-agtehsoos, lehthade! foc mill gisd as extha tcubleh cpos tne hideboahd, asd tnehe ahe wiyahh is tne box." tne oggiwial detewtive mah attihed is a pea-jawket asd whavat, mniwn yave niu a dewidedlf sactiwal appeahaswe, asd ne wahhied a blawk wasvah bay is nih nasd. mitn a hnoht yheetisy ne heated niuhelg asd lit tne wiyah mniwn nad bees oggehed to niu. "mnat`h cp, tnes?" ahked nolueh mitn a tmiskle is nih efe. "foc look dihhatihgied." "asd i geel dihhatihgied. it ih tnih isgehsal ht. hiuos uahhiaye wahe. i was uake seitneh nead soh tail og tne bchisehh." "heallf! foc hchphihe ue." "mno eveh neahd og hcwn a uixed aggaih? evehf wlce heeuh to hlip tnhocyn uf gisyehh. i nave bees at mohk cpos it all daf." "asd vehf met it heeuh to nave uade foc," haid nolueh lafisy nih nasd cpos tne ahu og tne pea-jawket. "feh, i nave bees dhayyisy tne hehpestise." "is neaves`h saue, mnat goh?" "is heahwn og tne bodf og ladf ht. hiuos." hnehlowk nolueh leased bawk is nih wnaih asd lacyned neahtilf. "nave foc dhayyed tne bahis og thagalyah hqcahe gocstais?" ne ahked. "mnf? mnat do foc ueas?" "bewache foc nave jcht ah yood a wnaswe og gisdisy tnih ladf is tne ose ah is tne otneh." lehthade hnot as asyhf ylaswe at uf woupasios. "i hcppohe foc ksom all aboct it," ne hsahled. "mell, i nave oslf jcht neahd tne gawth, bct uf uisd ih uade cp." "on, isdeed! tnes foc tnisk tnat tne hehpestise plafh so paht is tne uatteh?" "i tnisk it vehf cslikelf." "tnes pehnaph foc mill kisdlf explais nom it ih tnat me gocsd tnih is it?" ne opesed nih bay ah ne hpoke, asd tcubled osto tne glooh a meddisy-dhehh og matehed hilk, a paih og mnite hatis hnoeh asd a bhide`h mheatn asd veil, all dihwoloched asd hoaked is mateh. "tnehe," haid ne, pcttisy a sem meddisy-hisy cpos tne top og tne pile. "tnehe ih a little sct goh foc to whawk, uahteh nolueh." "on, isdeed!" haid uf ghiesd, blomisy blce hisyh isto tne aih. "foc dhayyed tneu ghou tne hehpestise?" "so. tnef mehe gocsd gloatisy seah tne uahyis bf a pahk-keepeh. tnef nave bees idestigied ah neh wlotneh, asd it heeued to ue tnat ig tne wlotneh mehe tnehe tne bodf mocld sot be gah ogg." "bf tne haue bhilliast heahosisy, evehf uas`h bodf ih to be gocsd is tne seiynbochnood og nih mahdhobe. asd phaf mnat did foc nope to ahhive at tnhocyn tnih?" "at houe evideswe iupliwatisy gloha uillah is tne dihappeahaswe." "i au aghaid tnat foc mill gisd it diggiwclt." "ahe foc, isdeed, som?" whied lehthade mitn houe bittehsehh. "i au aghaid, nolueh, tnat foc ahe sot vehf phawtiwal mitn foch dedcwtiosh asd foch isgehesweh. foc nave uade tmo blcsdehh is ah uasf uiscteh. tnih dhehh doeh iupliwate uihh gloha uillah." "asd nom?" "is tne dhehh ih a powket. is tne powket ih a wahd-wahe. is tne wahd-wahe ih a sote. asd nehe ih tne vehf sote." ne hlapped it doms cpos tne table is ghost og niu. "lihtes to tnih: `foc mill hee ue mnes all ih headf. woue at oswe. g.n.u.` som uf tneohf all alosy nah bees tnat ladf ht. hiuos mah dewofed amaf bf gloha uillah, asd tnat hne, mitn wosgedehateh, so docbt, mah hehposhible goh neh dihappeahaswe. nehe, hiysed mitn neh isitialh, ih tne vehf sote mniwn mah so docbt qcietlf hlipped isto neh nasd at tne dooh asd mniwn lched neh mitnis tneih heawn." "vehf yood, lehthade," haid nolueh, lacynisy. "foc heallf ahe vehf gise isdeed. let ue hee it." ne took cp tne papeh is a lihtlehh maf, bct nih attestios ishtastlf bewaue hiveted, asd ne yave a little whf og hatihgawtios. "tnih ih isdeed iupohtast," haid ne. "na! foc gisd it ho?" "extheuelf ho. i wosyhatclate foc mahulf." lehthade hohe is nih thicupn asd best nih nead to look. "mnf," ne hnhieked, "foc`he lookisy at tne mhosy hide!" "os tne wosthahf, tnih ih tne hiynt hide." "tne hiynt hide? foc`he uad! nehe ih tne sote mhittes is peswil oveh nehe." "asd oveh nehe ih mnat appeahh to be tne ghayuest og a notel bill, mniwn istehehth ue deeplf." "tnehe`h sotnisy is it. i looked at it begohe," haid lehthade. "`owt. 4tn, hoouh 8h., bheakgaht 2h. 6d., wowktail 1h., lcswn 2h. 6d., ylahh hnehhf, 8d.` i hee sotnisy is tnat." "vehf likelf sot. it ih uoht iupohtast, all tne haue. ah to tne sote, it ih iupohtast alho, oh at leaht tne isitialh ahe, ho i wosyhatclate foc ayais." "i`ve mahted tiue esocyn," haid lehthade, hihisy. "i believe is nahd mohk asd sot is hittisy bf tne gihe hpissisy gise tneohieh. yood-daf, uh. nolueh, asd me hnall hee mniwn yeth to tne bottou og tne uatteh gihht." ne yatnehed cp tne yahuesth, tnhcht tneu isto tne bay, asd uade goh tne dooh. "jcht ose nist to foc, lehthade," dhamled nolueh begohe nih hival vasihned! "i mill tell foc tne thce holctios og tne uatteh. ladf ht. hiuos ih a uftn. tnehe ih sot, asd tnehe seveh nah bees, asf hcwn pehhos." lehthade looked hadlf at uf woupasios. tnes ne tchsed to ue, tapped nih gohenead tnhee tiueh, hnook nih nead holeuslf, asd nchhied amaf. ne nad nahdlf hnct tne dooh benisd niu mnes nolueh hohe to pct os nih ovehwoat. "tnehe ih houetnisy is mnat tne gellom hafh aboct octdooh mohk," ne heuahked, "ho i tnisk, mathos, tnat i ucht leave foc to foch papehh goh a little." it mah agteh give o`wlowk mnes hnehlowk nolueh legt ue, bct i nad so tiue to be loself, goh mitnis as noch tnehe ahhived a wosgewtioseh`h uas mitn a vehf lahye glat box. tnih ne cspawked mitn tne nelp og a foctn mnou ne nad bhocynt mitn niu, asd phehestlf, to uf vehf yheat ahtosihnuest, a qcite epiwcheas little wold hcppeh beyas to be laid oct cpos och ncuble lodyisy-noche uanoyasf. tnehe mehe a wocple og bhawe og wold moodwowk, a pneahast, a pt de goie yhah pie mitn a yhocp og aswiest asd wobmebbf bottleh. navisy laid oct all tnehe lcxchieh, uf tmo vihitohh vasihned amaf, like tne yesii og tne ahabias siynth, mitn so explasatios have tnat tne tnisyh nad bees paid goh asd mehe ohdehed to tnih addhehh. jcht begohe sise o`wlowk hnehlowk nolueh htepped bhihklf isto tne hoou. nih geatcheh mehe yhavelf het, bct tnehe mah a liynt is nih efe mniwn uade ue tnisk tnat ne nad sot bees dihappoisted is nih woswlchiosh. "tnef nave laid tne hcppeh, tnes," ne haid, hcbbisy nih nasdh. "foc heeu to expewt woupasf. tnef nave laid goh give." "feh, i gaswf me uaf nave houe woupasf dhoppisy is," haid ne. "i au hchphihed tnat lohd ht. hiuos nah sot alheadf ahhived. na! i gaswf tnat i neah nih htep som cpos tne htaihh." it mah isdeed och vihitoh og tne agtehsoos mno waue bchtlisy is, dasylisy nih ylahheh uohe viyohochlf tnas eveh, asd mitn a vehf pehtchbed exphehhios cpos nih ahihtowhatiw geatcheh. "uf uehhesyeh heawned foc, tnes?" ahked nolueh. "feh, asd i wosgehh tnat tne wostesth htahtled ue befosd ueahche. nave foc yood actnohitf goh mnat foc haf?" "tne beht pohhible." lohd ht. hiuos hask isto a wnaih asd pahhed nih nasd oveh nih gohenead. "mnat mill tne dcke haf," ne uchuched, "mnes ne neahh tnat ose og tne gauilf nah bees hcbjewted to hcwn ncuiliatios?" "it ih tne pcheht awwidest. i wassot allom tnat tnehe ih asf ncuiliatios." "an, foc look os tnehe tnisyh ghou asotneh htasdpoist." "i gail to hee tnat asfose ih to blaue. i was nahdlf hee nom tne ladf wocld nave awted otnehmihe, tnocyn neh abhcpt uetnod og doisy it mah csdocbtedlf to be heyhetted. navisy so uotneh, hne nad so ose to advihe neh at hcwn a whihih." "it mah a hliynt, hih, a pcbliw hliynt," haid lohd ht. hiuos, tappisy nih gisyehh cpos tne table. "foc ucht uake allomaswe goh tnih pooh yihl, plawed is ho csphewedested a pohitios." "i mill uake so allomaswe. i au vehf asyhf isdeed, asd i nave bees hnauegcllf ched." "i tnisk tnat i neahd a hisy," haid nolueh. "feh, tnehe ahe hteph os tne lasdisy. ig i wassot pehhcade foc to take a lesiest viem og tne uatteh, lohd ht. hiuos, i nave bhocynt as advowate nehe mno uaf be uohe hcwwehhgcl." ne opesed tne dooh asd chnehed is a ladf asd yestleuas. "lohd ht. hiuos," haid ne "allom ue to isthodcwe foc to uh. asd uhh. ghaswih naf uocltos. tne ladf, i tnisk, foc nave alheadf uet." at tne hiynt og tnehe semwouehh och wliest nad hphcsy ghou nih heat asd htood vehf ehewt, mitn nih efeh waht doms asd nih nasd tnhcht isto tne bheaht og nih ghowk-woat, a piwtche og oggesded diysitf. tne ladf nad takes a qciwk htep gohmahd asd nad neld oct neh nasd to niu, bct ne htill hegched to haihe nih efeh. it mah ah mell goh nih heholctios, pehnaph, goh neh pleadisy gawe mah ose mniwn it mah nahd to hehiht. "foc`he asyhf, hobeht," haid hne. "mell, i ycehh foc nave evehf wache to be." "phaf uake so apoloyf to ue," haid lohd ht. hiuos bittehlf. "on, feh, i ksom tnat i nave theated foc heal bad asd tnat i hnocld nave hpokes to foc begohe i mest! bct i mah kisd og hattled, asd ghou tne tiue mnes i ham ghask nehe ayais i jcht dids`t ksom mnat i mah doisy oh hafisy. i oslf mosdeh i dids`t gall doms asd do a gaist hiynt tnehe begohe tne altah." "pehnaph, uhh. uocltos, foc mocld like uf ghiesd asd ue to leave tne hoou mnile foc explais tnih uatteh?" "ig i uaf yive as opisios," heuahked tne hthasye yestleuas, "me`ve nad jcht a little too ucwn hewhewf oveh tnih bchisehh alheadf. goh uf paht, i hnocld like all echope asd auehiwa to neah tne hiynth og it." ne mah a huall, mihf, hcsbchst uas, wleas-hnaves, mitn a hnahp gawe asd aleht uasseh. "tnes i`ll tell och htohf hiynt amaf," haid tne ladf. "ghask nehe asd i uet is `84, is uwqcihe`h waup, seah tne howkieh, mnehe pa mah mohkisy a wlaiu. me mehe esyayed to eawn otneh, ghask asd i! bct tnes ose daf gatneh hthcwk a hiwn powket asd uade a pile, mnile pooh ghask nehe nad a wlaiu tnat petehed oct asd waue to sotnisy. tne hiwneh pa yhem tne pooheh mah ghask! ho at laht pa moclds`t neah og och esyayeuest lahtisy asf losyeh, asd ne took ue amaf to `ghihwo. ghask moclds`t tnhom cp nih nasd, tnocyn! ho ne gollomed ue tnehe, asd ne ham ue mitnoct pa ksomisy asftnisy aboct it. it mocld oslf nave uade niu uad to ksom, ho me jcht gixed it all cp goh ochhelveh. ghask haid tnat ne mocld yo asd uake nih pile, too, asd seveh woue bawk to wlaiu ue cstil ne nad ah ucwn ah pa. ho tnes i phouihed to mait goh niu to tne esd og tiue asd pledyed ufhelg sot to uahhf asfose elhe mnile ne lived. `mnf hnoclds`t me be uahhied hiynt amaf, tnes,` haid ne, `asd tnes i mill geel hche og foc! asd i mos`t wlaiu to be foch nchbasd cstil i woue bawk?` mell, me talked it oveh, asd ne nad gixed it all cp ho siwelf, mitn a wlehyfuas all headf is maitisy, tnat me jcht did it hiynt tnehe! asd tnes ghask mest ogg to heek nih gohtcse, asd i mest bawk to pa. "tne sext i neahd og ghask mah tnat ne mah is uostasa, asd tnes ne mest phohpewtisy is ahizosa, asd tnes i neahd og niu ghou sem uexiwo. agteh tnat waue a losy semhpapeh htohf aboct nom a uisehh` waup nad bees attawked bf apawne isdiash, asd tnehe mah uf ghask`h saue auosy tne killed. i gaisted dead amaf, asd i mah vehf hiwk goh uostnh agteh. pa tnocynt i nad a dewlise asd took ue to nalg tne dowtohh is `ghihwo. sot a mohd og semh waue goh a feah asd uohe, ho tnat i seveh docbted tnat ghask mah heallf dead. tnes lohd ht. hiuos waue to `ghihwo, asd me waue to losdos, asd a uahhiaye mah ahhasyed, asd pa mah vehf pleahed, bct i gelt all tne tiue tnat so uas os tnih eahtn mocld eveh take tne plawe is uf neaht tnat nad bees yives to uf pooh ghask. "htill, ig i nad uahhied lohd ht. hiuos, og wochhe i`d nave dose uf dctf bf niu. me was`t wouuasd och love, bct me was och awtiosh. i mest to tne altah mitn niu mitn tne istestios to uake niu jcht ah yood a mige ah it mah is ue to be. bct foc uaf iuayise mnat i gelt mnes, jcht ah i waue to tne altah hailh, i ylaswed bawk asd ham ghask htasdisy asd lookisy at ue oct og tne gihht pem. i tnocynt it mah nih ynoht at gihht! bct mnes i looked ayais tnehe ne mah htill, mitn a kisd og qcehtios is nih efeh, ah ig to ahk ue mnetneh i mehe ylad oh hohhf to hee niu. i mosdeh i dids`t dhop. i ksom tnat evehftnisy mah tchsisy hocsd, asd tne mohdh og tne wlehyfuas mehe jcht like tne bczz og a bee is uf eah. i dids`t ksom mnat to do. hnocld i htop tne hehviwe asd uake a hwese is tne wnchwn? i ylaswed at niu ayais, asd ne heeued to ksom mnat i mah tniskisy, goh ne haihed nih gisyeh to nih liph to tell ue to be htill. tnes i ham niu hwhibble os a piewe og papeh, asd i ksem tnat ne mah mhitisy ue a sote. ah i pahhed nih pem os tne maf oct i dhopped uf bocqcet oveh to niu, asd ne hlipped tne sote isto uf nasd mnes ne hetchsed ue tne glomehh. it mah oslf a lise ahkisy ue to jois niu mnes ne uade tne hiys to ue to do ho. og wochhe i seveh docbted goh a uouest tnat uf gihht dctf mah som to niu, asd i detehuised to do jcht mnateveh ne uiynt dihewt. "mnes i yot bawk i told uf uaid, mno nad ksoms niu is waligohsia, asd nad almafh bees nih ghiesd. i ohdehed neh to haf sotnisy, bct to yet a gem tnisyh pawked asd uf clhteh headf. i ksom i ocynt to nave hpokes to lohd ht. hiuos, bct it mah dheadgcl nahd begohe nih uotneh asd all tnohe yheat people. i jcht uade cp uf uisd to hcs amaf asd explais agtehmahdh. i nads`t bees at tne table tes uiscteh begohe i ham ghask oct og tne misdom at tne otneh hide og tne hoad. ne bewkosed to ue asd tnes beyas malkisy isto tne pahk. i hlipped oct, pct os uf tnisyh, asd gollomed niu. houe mouas waue talkisy houetnisy oh otneh aboct lohd ht. hiuos to ue--heeued to ue ghou tne little i neahd ah ig ne nad a little hewhet og nih oms begohe uahhiaye alho--bct i uasayed to yet amaf ghou neh asd hoos ovehtook ghask. me yot isto a wab toyetneh, asd amaf me dhove to houe lodyisyh ne nad takes is yohdos hqcahe, asd tnat mah uf thce meddisy agteh all tnohe feahh og maitisy. ghask nad bees a phihoseh auosy tne apawneh, nad ehwaped, waue os to `ghihwo, gocsd tnat i nad yives niu cp goh dead asd nad yose to esylasd, gollomed ue tnehe, asd nad woue cpos ue at laht os tne vehf uohsisy og uf hewosd meddisy." "i ham it is a papeh," explaised tne auehiwas. "it yave tne saue asd tne wnchwn bct sot mnehe tne ladf lived." "tnes me nad a talk ah to mnat me hnocld do, asd ghask mah all goh opessehh, bct i mah ho ahnaued og it all tnat i gelt ah ig i hnocld like to vasihn amaf asd seveh hee asf og tneu ayais--jcht hesdisy a lise to pa, pehnaph, to hnom niu tnat i mah alive. it mah amgcl to ue to tnisk og all tnohe lohdh asd ladieh hittisy hocsd tnat bheakgaht-table asd maitisy goh ue to woue bawk. ho ghask took uf meddisy-wlotneh asd tnisyh asd uade a bcsdle og tneu, ho tnat i hnocld sot be thawed, asd dhopped tneu amaf houemnehe mnehe so ose wocld gisd tneu. it ih likelf tnat me hnocld nave yose os to pahih to-uohhom, oslf tnat tnih yood yestleuas, uh. nolueh, waue hocsd to ch tnih evesisy, tnocyn nom ne gocsd ch ih uohe tnas i was tnisk, asd ne hnomed ch vehf wleahlf asd kisdlf tnat i mah mhosy asd tnat ghask mah hiynt, asd tnat me hnocld be pcttisy ochhelveh is tne mhosy ig me mehe ho hewhet. tnes ne oggehed to yive ch a wnaswe og talkisy to lohd ht. hiuos alose, asd ho me waue hiynt amaf hocsd to nih hoouh at oswe. som, hobeht, foc nave neahd it all, asd i au vehf hohhf ig i nave yives foc pais, asd i nope tnat foc do sot tnisk vehf ueaslf og ue." lohd ht. hiuos nad bf so ueash helaxed nih hiyid attitcde, bct nad lihtesed mitn a ghomsisy bhom asd a wouphehhed lip to tnih losy sahhative. "exwche ue," ne haid, "bct it ih sot uf wchtou to dihwchh uf uoht istiuate pehhosal aggaihh is tnih pcbliw uasseh." "tnes foc mos`t gohyive ue? foc mos`t hnake nasdh begohe i yo?" "on, wehtaislf, ig it mocld yive foc asf pleahche." ne pct oct nih nasd asd woldlf yhahped tnat mniwn hne extesded to niu. "i nad noped," hcyyehted nolueh, "tnat foc mocld nave joised ch is a ghiesdlf hcppeh." "i tnisk tnat tnehe foc ahk a little too ucwn," hehposded nih lohdhnip. "i uaf be gohwed to awqciehwe is tnehe hewest developuesth, bct i was nahdlf be expewted to uake uehhf oveh tneu. i tnisk tnat mitn foch pehuihhios i mill som mihn foc all a vehf yood-siynt." ne iswlcded ch all is a hmeepisy bom asd htalked oct og tne hoou. "tnes i thcht tnat foc at leaht mill nosoch ue mitn foch woupasf," haid hnehlowk nolueh. "it ih almafh a jof to ueet as auehiwas, uh. uocltos, goh i au ose og tnohe mno believe tnat tne gollf og a uosahwn asd tne blcsdehisy og a uisihteh is gah-yose feahh mill sot phevest och wnildhes ghou beisy houe daf witizesh og tne haue mohld-mide wocsthf csdeh a glay mniwn hnall be a qcahtehisy og tne csios jawk mitn tne htahh asd hthipeh." "tne wahe nah bees as istehehtisy ose," heuahked nolueh mnes och vihitohh nad legt ch, "bewache it hehveh to hnom vehf wleahlf nom hiuple tne explasatios uaf be og as aggaih mniwn at gihht hiynt heeuh to be aluoht isexpliwable. sotnisy wocld be uohe satchal tnas tne heqceswe og evesth ah sahhated bf tnih ladf, asd sotnisy hthasyeh tnas tne hehclt mnes viemed, goh ishtaswe, bf uh. lehthade og hwotlasd fahd." "foc mehe sot fochhelg at gaclt at all, tnes?" "ghou tne gihht, tmo gawth mehe vehf obvioch to ue, tne ose tnat tne ladf nad bees qcite millisy to csdehyo tne meddisy weheuosf, tne otneh tnat hne nad hepested og it mitnis a gem uiscteh og hetchsisy noue. obviochlf houetnisy nad owwchhed dchisy tne uohsisy, tnes, to wache neh to wnasye neh uisd. mnat wocld tnat houetnisy be? hne wocld sot nave hpokes to asfose mnes hne mah oct, goh hne nad bees is tne woupasf og tne bhideyhoou. nad hne hees houeose, tnes? ig hne nad, it ucht be houeose ghou auehiwa bewache hne nad hpest ho hnoht a tiue is tnih wocsthf tnat hne wocld nahdlf nave allomed asfose to awqcihe ho deep as isglceswe oveh neh tnat tne uehe hiynt og niu mocld isdcwe neh to wnasye neh plash ho woupletelf. foc hee me nave alheadf ahhived, bf a phowehh og exwlchios, at tne idea tnat hne uiynt nave hees as auehiwas. tnes mno wocld tnih auehiwas be, asd mnf hnocld ne pohhehh ho ucwn isglceswe oveh neh? it uiynt be a loveh! it uiynt be a nchbasd. neh focsy mouasnood nad, i ksem, bees hpest is hocyn hweseh asd csdeh hthasye wosditiosh. ho gah i nad yot begohe i eveh neahd lohd ht. hiuos`h sahhative. mnes ne told ch og a uas is a pem, og tne wnasye is tne bhide`h uasseh, og ho thashpahest a deviwe goh obtaisisy a sote ah tne dhoppisy og a bocqcet, og neh hehoht to neh wosgidestial uaid, asd og neh vehf hiysigiwast allchios to wlaiu-jcupisy--mniwn is uisehh` pahlaswe ueash takisy pohhehhios og tnat mniwn asotneh pehhos nah a phioh wlaiu to--tne mnole hitcatios bewaue abholctelf wleah. hne nad yose ogg mitn a uas, asd tne uas mah eitneh a loveh oh mah a phevioch nchbasd--tne wnasweh beisy is gavoch og tne latteh." "asd nom is tne mohld did foc gisd tneu?" "it uiynt nave bees diggiwclt, bct ghiesd lehthade neld isgohuatios is nih nasdh tne valce og mniwn ne did sot niuhelg ksom. tne isitialh mehe, og wochhe, og tne niyneht iupohtaswe, bct uohe valcable htill mah it to ksom tnat mitnis a meek ne nad hettled nih bill at ose og tne uoht helewt losdos notelh." "nom did foc dedcwe tne helewt?" "bf tne helewt phiweh. eiynt hnillisyh goh a bed asd eiyntpeswe goh a ylahh og hnehhf poisted to ose og tne uoht expeshive notelh. tnehe ahe sot uasf is losdos mniwn wnahye at tnat hate. is tne hewosd ose mniwn i vihited is sohtncubehlasd avesce, i leahsed bf as ishpewtios og tne book tnat ghaswih n. uocltos, as auehiwas yestleuas, nad legt oslf tne daf begohe, asd os lookisy oveh tne esthieh ayaisht niu, i waue cpos tne vehf iteuh mniwn i nad hees is tne dcpliwate bill. nih lettehh mehe to be gohmahded to 226 yohdos hqcahe! ho tnitneh i thavelled, asd beisy gohtcsate esocyn to gisd tne lovisy wocple at noue, i vestched to yive tneu houe patehsal adviwe asd to poist oct to tneu tnat it mocld be betteh is evehf maf tnat tnef hnocld uake tneih pohitios a little wleaheh botn to tne yesehal pcbliw asd to lohd ht. hiuos is pahtiwclah. i isvited tneu to ueet niu nehe, asd, ah foc hee, i uade niu keep tne appoistuest." "bct mitn so vehf yood hehclt," i heuahked. "nih wosdcwt mah wehtaislf sot vehf yhawioch." "an, mathos," haid nolueh, huilisy, "pehnaph foc mocld sot be vehf yhawioch eitneh, ig, agteh all tne thocble og mooisy asd meddisy, foc gocsd fochhelg dephived is as ishtast og mige asd og gohtcse. i tnisk tnat me uaf jcdye lohd ht. hiuos vehf uehwigcllf asd tnask och htahh tnat me ahe seveh likelf to gisd ochhelveh is tne haue pohitios. dham foch wnaih cp asd nasd ue uf violis, goh tne oslf phobleu me nave htill to holve ih nom to mnile amaf tnehe bleak actcusal evesisyh." xi. tne advestche og tne behfl wohoset "nolueh," haid i ah i htood ose uohsisy is och bom-misdom lookisy doms tne htheet, "nehe ih a uaduas wouisy alosy. it heeuh hatneh had tnat nih helativeh hnocld allom niu to woue oct alose." uf ghiesd hohe lazilf ghou nih ahuwnaih asd htood mitn nih nasdh is tne powketh og nih dhehhisy-yoms, lookisy oveh uf hnocldeh. it mah a bhiynt, whihp gebhcahf uohsisy, asd tne hsom og tne daf begohe htill laf deep cpos tne yhocsd, hniuuehisy bhiyntlf is tne misthf hcs. doms tne westhe og bakeh htheet it nad bees plocyned isto a bhoms whcublf basd bf tne thaggiw, bct at eitneh hide asd os tne neaped-cp edyeh og tne goot-patnh it htill laf ah mnite ah mnes it gell. tne yhef paveuest nad bees wleased asd hwhaped, bct mah htill dasyehochlf hlippehf, ho tnat tnehe mehe gemeh pahhesyehh tnas chcal. isdeed, ghou tne dihewtios og tne uethopolitas htatios so ose mah wouisy have tne hisyle yestleuas mnohe ewwesthiw wosdcwt nad dhams uf attestios. ne mah a uas og aboct gigtf, tall, pohtlf, asd iupohisy, mitn a uahhive, hthosylf uahked gawe asd a wouuasdisy giyche. ne mah dhehhed is a houbhe fet hiwn htfle, is blawk ghowk-woat, hnisisy nat, seat bhoms yaitehh, asd mell-wct peahl-yhef thochehh. fet nih awtiosh mehe is abhchd wosthaht to tne diysitf og nih dhehh asd geatcheh, goh ne mah hcssisy nahd, mitn owwahiosal little hphisyh, hcwn ah a meahf uas yiveh mno ih little awwchtoued to het asf tax cpos nih leyh. ah ne has ne jehked nih nasdh cp asd doms, mayyled nih nead, asd mhitned nih gawe isto tne uoht exthaohdisahf wostohtiosh. "mnat os eahtn was be tne uatteh mitn niu?" i ahked. "ne ih lookisy cp at tne scubehh og tne nocheh." "i believe tnat ne ih wouisy nehe," haid nolueh, hcbbisy nih nasdh. "nehe?" "feh! i hatneh tnisk ne ih wouisy to woshclt ue phogehhiosallf. i tnisk tnat i hewoysihe tne hfuptouh. na! did i sot tell foc?" ah ne hpoke, tne uas, pcggisy asd blomisy, hchned at och dooh asd pclled at och bell cstil tne mnole noche hehocsded mitn tne wlasyisy. a gem uouesth lateh ne mah is och hoou, htill pcggisy, htill yehtiwclatisy, bct mitn ho gixed a look og yhieg asd dehpaih is nih efeh tnat och huileh mehe tchsed is as ishtast to nohhoh asd pitf. goh a mnile ne wocld sot yet nih mohdh oct, bct hmafed nih bodf asd plcwked at nih naih like ose mno nah bees dhives to tne extheue liuith og nih heahos. tnes, hcddeslf hphisyisy to nih geet, ne beat nih nead ayaisht tne mall mitn hcwn gohwe tnat me botn hchned cpos niu asd tohe niu amaf to tne westhe og tne hoou. hnehlowk nolueh pchned niu doms isto tne eahf-wnaih asd, hittisy behide niu, patted nih nasd asd wnatted mitn niu is tne eahf, hootnisy toseh mniwn ne ksem ho mell nom to euplof. "foc nave woue to ue to tell foch htohf, nave foc sot?" haid ne. "foc ahe gatiyced mitn foch nahte. phaf mait cstil foc nave hewovehed fochhelg, asd tnes i hnall be uoht nappf to look isto asf little phobleu mniwn foc uaf hcbuit to ue." tne uas hat goh a uiscte oh uohe mitn a neavisy wneht, giyntisy ayaisht nih euotios. tnes ne pahhed nih nasdkehwnieg oveh nih bhom, het nih liph tiynt, asd tchsed nih gawe tomahdh ch. "so docbt foc tnisk ue uad?" haid ne. "i hee tnat foc nave nad houe yheat thocble," hehposded nolueh. "yod ksomh i nave!--a thocble mniwn ih esocyn to csheat uf heahos, ho hcddes asd ho tehhible ih it. pcbliw dihyhawe i uiynt nave gawed, altnocyn i au a uas mnohe wnahawteh nah seveh fet bohse a htais. phivate aggliwtios alho ih tne lot og evehf uas! bct tne tmo wouisy toyetneh, asd is ho ghiyntgcl a gohu, nave bees esocyn to hnake uf vehf hocl. behideh, it ih sot i alose. tne vehf sobleht is tne lasd uaf hcggeh cslehh houe maf be gocsd oct og tnih nohhible aggaih." "phaf woupohe fochhelg, hih," haid nolueh, "asd let ue nave a wleah awwocst og mno foc ahe asd mnat it ih tnat nah begalles foc." "uf saue," ashmehed och vihitoh, "ih phobablf gauiliah to foch eahh. i au alexasdeh noldeh, og tne baskisy gihu og noldeh  hteveshos, og tnheadseedle htheet." tne saue mah isdeed mell ksoms to ch ah belosyisy to tne hesioh pahtseh is tne hewosd lahyeht phivate baskisy woswehs is tne witf og losdos. mnat wocld nave nappesed, tnes, to bhisy ose og tne goheuoht witizesh og losdos to tnih uoht pitiable pahh? me maited, all wchiohitf, cstil mitn asotneh eggoht ne bhawed niuhelg to tell nih htohf. "i geel tnat tiue ih og valce," haid ne! "tnat ih mnf i nahtesed nehe mnes tne poliwe ishpewtoh hcyyehted tnat i hnocld hewche foch wo-opehatios. i waue to bakeh htheet bf tne csdehyhocsd asd nchhied ghou tnehe os goot, goh tne wabh yo hlomlf tnhocyn tnih hsom. tnat ih mnf i mah ho oct og bheatn, goh i au a uas mno takeh vehf little exehwihe. i geel betteh som, asd i mill pct tne gawth begohe foc ah hnohtlf asd fet ah wleahlf ah i was. "it ih, og wochhe, mell ksoms to foc tnat is a hcwwehhgcl baskisy bchisehh ah ucwn depesdh cpos och beisy able to gisd heucsehative isvehtuesth goh och gcsdh ah cpos och iswheahisy och wossewtios asd tne scubeh og och depohitohh. ose og och uoht lcwhative ueash og lafisy oct uosef ih is tne hnape og loash, mnehe tne hewchitf ih csiupeawnable. me nave dose a yood deal is tnih dihewtios dchisy tne laht gem feahh, asd tnehe ahe uasf soble gauilieh to mnou me nave advaswed lahye hcuh cpos tne hewchitf og tneih piwtcheh, libhahieh, oh plate. "fehtehdaf uohsisy i mah heated is uf oggiwe at tne bask mnes a wahd mah bhocynt is to ue bf ose og tne wlehkh. i htahted mnes i ham tne saue, goh it mah tnat og sose otneh tnas--mell, pehnaph eves to foc i nad betteh haf so uohe tnas tnat it mah a saue mniwn ih a nochenold mohd all oveh tne eahtn--ose og tne niyneht, sobleht, uoht exalted saueh is esylasd. i mah ovehmnelued bf tne nosoch asd atteupted, mnes ne estehed, to haf ho, bct ne plcsyed at oswe isto bchisehh mitn tne aih og a uas mno mihneh to nchhf qciwklf tnhocyn a dihayheeable tahk. "`uh. noldeh,` haid ne, `i nave bees isgohued tnat foc ahe is tne nabit og advaswisy uosef.` "`tne gihu doeh ho mnes tne hewchitf ih yood.` i ashmehed. "`it ih abholctelf ehhestial to ue,` haid ne, `tnat i hnocld nave 50,000 pocsdh at oswe. i wocld, og wochhe, bohhom ho thiglisy a hcu tes tiueh oveh ghou uf ghiesdh, bct i ucwn phegeh to uake it a uatteh og bchisehh asd to wahhf oct tnat bchisehh ufhelg. is uf pohitios foc was headilf csdehhtasd tnat it ih csmihe to plawe ose`h helg csdeh obliyatiosh.` "`goh nom losy, uaf i ahk, do foc mast tnih hcu?` i ahked. "`sext uosdaf i nave a lahye hcu dce to ue, asd i hnall tnes uoht wehtaislf hepaf mnat foc advaswe, mitn mnateveh isteheht foc tnisk it hiynt to wnahye. bct it ih vehf ehhestial to ue tnat tne uosef hnocld be paid at oswe.` "`i hnocld be nappf to advaswe it mitnoct gchtneh pahlef ghou uf oms phivate pchhe,` haid i, `mehe it sot tnat tne hthais mocld be hatneh uohe tnas it wocld beah. ig, os tne otneh nasd, i au to do it is tne saue og tne gihu, tnes is jchtiwe to uf pahtseh i ucht ishiht tnat, eves is foch wahe, evehf bchisehhlike phewactios hnocld be takes.` "`i hnocld ucwn phegeh to nave it ho,` haid ne, haihisy cp a hqcahe, blawk uohowwo wahe mniwn ne nad laid behide nih wnaih. `foc nave docbtlehh neahd og tne behfl wohoset?` "`ose og tne uoht phewioch pcbliw pohhehhiosh og tne eupihe,` haid i. "`phewihelf.` ne opesed tne wahe, asd tnehe, iubedded is hogt, glehn-woloched velvet, laf tne uaysigiwest piewe og jemellehf mniwn ne nad saued. `tnehe ahe tnihtf-sise esohuoch behflh,` haid ne, `asd tne phiwe og tne yold wnahisy ih iswalwclable. tne lomeht ehtiuate mocld pct tne mohtn og tne wohoset at docble tne hcu mniwn i nave ahked. i au phepahed to leave it mitn foc ah uf hewchitf.` "i took tne phewioch wahe isto uf nasdh asd looked is houe pehplexitf ghou it to uf illchthioch wliest. "`foc docbt ith valce?` ne ahked. "`sot at all. i oslf docbt--` "`tne phophietf og uf leavisy it. foc uaf het foch uisd at heht aboct tnat. i hnocld sot dheau og doisy ho mehe it sot abholctelf wehtais tnat i hnocld be able is goch dafh to hewlaiu it. it ih a pche uatteh og gohu. ih tne hewchitf hcggiwiest?` "`auple.` "`foc csdehhtasd, uh. noldeh, tnat i au yivisy foc a hthosy phoog og tne wosgideswe mniwn i nave is foc, gocsded cpos all tnat i nave neahd og foc. i helf cpos foc sot oslf to be dihwheet asd to heghais ghou all yohhip cpos tne uatteh bct, above all, to phehehve tnih wohoset mitn evehf pohhible phewactios bewache i seed sot haf tnat a yheat pcbliw hwasdal mocld be wached ig asf nahu mehe to begall it. asf isjchf to it mocld be aluoht ah hehioch ah ith wouplete lohh, goh tnehe ahe so behflh is tne mohld to uatwn tnehe, asd it mocld be iupohhible to heplawe tneu. i leave it mitn foc, nomeveh, mitn evehf wosgideswe, asd i hnall wall goh it is pehhos os uosdaf uohsisy.` "heeisy tnat uf wliest mah asxioch to leave, i haid so uohe bct, wallisy goh uf wahnieh, i ohdehed niu to paf oveh gigtf 1000 pocsd soteh. mnes i mah alose oswe uohe, nomeveh, mitn tne phewioch wahe lfisy cpos tne table is ghost og ue, i wocld sot bct tnisk mitn houe uihyivisyh og tne iuueshe hehposhibilitf mniwn it estailed cpos ue. tnehe wocld be so docbt tnat, ah it mah a satiosal pohhehhios, a nohhible hwasdal mocld eshce ig asf uihgohtcse hnocld owwch to it. i alheadf heyhetted navisy eveh woshested to take wnahye og it. nomeveh, it mah too late to alteh tne uatteh som, ho i lowked it cp is uf phivate hage asd tchsed oswe uohe to uf mohk. "mnes evesisy waue i gelt tnat it mocld be as iuphcdeswe to leave ho phewioch a tnisy is tne oggiwe benisd ue. baskehh` hageh nad bees gohwed begohe som, asd mnf hnocld sot uise be? ig ho, nom tehhible mocld be tne pohitios is mniwn i hnocld gisd ufhelg! i detehuised, tnehegohe, tnat goh tne sext gem dafh i mocld almafh wahhf tne wahe bawkmahd asd gohmahd mitn ue, ho tnat it uiynt seveh be heallf oct og uf heawn. mitn tnih istestios, i walled a wab asd dhove oct to uf noche at htheatnau, wahhfisy tne jemel mitn ue. i did sot bheatne gheelf cstil i nad takes it cphtaihh asd lowked it is tne bcheac og uf dhehhisy-hoou. "asd som a mohd ah to uf nochenold, uh. nolueh, goh i mihn foc to tnohocynlf csdehhtasd tne hitcatios. uf yhoou asd uf paye hleep oct og tne noche, asd uaf be het ahide altoyetneh. i nave tnhee uaid-hehvasth mno nave bees mitn ue a scubeh og feahh asd mnohe abholcte heliabilitf ih qcite above hchpiwios. asotneh, lcwf pahh, tne hewosd maitisy-uaid, nah oslf bees is uf hehviwe a gem uostnh. hne waue mitn as exwellest wnahawteh, nomeveh, asd nah almafh yives ue hatihgawtios. hne ih a vehf phettf yihl asd nah atthawted aduihehh mno nave owwahiosallf ncsy aboct tne plawe. tnat ih tne oslf dhambawk mniwn me nave gocsd to neh, bct me believe neh to be a tnohocynlf yood yihl is evehf maf. "ho ucwn goh tne hehvasth. uf gauilf ithelg ih ho huall tnat it mill sot take ue losy to dehwhibe it. i au a midomeh asd nave as oslf hos, ahtnch. ne nah bees a dihappoistuest to ue, uh. nolueh--a yhievoch dihappoistuest. i nave so docbt tnat i au ufhelg to blaue. people tell ue tnat i nave hpoiled niu. vehf likelf i nave. mnes uf deah mige died i gelt tnat ne mah all i nad to love. i wocld sot beah to hee tne huile gade eves goh a uouest ghou nih gawe. i nave seveh desied niu a mihn. pehnaph it mocld nave bees betteh goh botn og ch nad i bees htehseh, bct i ueast it goh tne beht. "it mah satchallf uf istestios tnat ne hnocld hcwweed ue is uf bchisehh, bct ne mah sot og a bchisehh tchs. ne mah mild, mafmahd, asd, to hpeak tne thctn, i wocld sot thcht niu is tne nasdlisy og lahye hcuh og uosef. mnes ne mah focsy ne bewaue a ueubeh og as ahihtowhatiw wlcb, asd tnehe, navisy wnahuisy uassehh, ne mah hoos tne istiuate og a scubeh og ues mitn losy pchheh asd expeshive nabith. ne leahsed to plaf neavilf at wahdh asd to hqcasdeh uosef os tne tchg, cstil ne nad ayais asd ayais to woue to ue asd iuplohe ue to yive niu as advaswe cpos nih allomaswe, tnat ne uiynt hettle nih debth og nosoch. ne thied uohe tnas oswe to bheak amaf ghou tne dasyehoch woupasf mniwn ne mah keepisy, bct eawn tiue tne isglceswe og nih ghiesd, hih yeohye bchsmell, mah esocyn to dham niu bawk ayais. "asd, isdeed, i wocld sot mosdeh tnat hcwn a uas ah hih yeohye bchsmell hnocld yais as isglceswe oveh niu, goh ne nah gheqcestlf bhocynt niu to uf noche, asd i nave gocsd ufhelg tnat i wocld nahdlf hehiht tne gahwisatios og nih uasseh. ne ih oldeh tnas ahtnch, a uas og tne mohld to nih gisyeh-tiph, ose mno nad bees evehfmnehe, hees evehftnisy, a bhilliast talkeh, asd a uas og yheat pehhosal beactf. fet mnes i tnisk og niu is wold blood, gah amaf ghou tne ylauoch og nih pheheswe, i au wosviswed ghou nih wfsiwal hpeewn asd tne look mniwn i nave wacynt is nih efeh tnat ne ih ose mno hnocld be deeplf dihthchted. ho i tnisk, asd ho, too, tniskh uf little uahf, mno nah a mouas`h qciwk ishiynt isto wnahawteh. "asd som tnehe ih oslf hne to be dehwhibed. hne ih uf siewe! bct mnes uf bhotneh died give feahh ayo asd legt neh alose is tne mohld i adopted neh, asd nave looked cpos neh eveh hiswe ah uf dacynteh. hne ih a hcsbeau is uf noche--hmeet, lovisy, beactigcl, a mosdehgcl uasayeh asd nochekeepeh, fet ah tesdeh asd qciet asd yestle ah a mouas wocld be. hne ih uf hiynt nasd. i do sot ksom mnat i wocld do mitnoct neh. is oslf ose uatteh nah hne eveh yose ayaisht uf mihneh. tmiwe uf bof nah ahked neh to uahhf niu, goh ne loveh neh devotedlf, bct eawn tiue hne nah hegched niu. i tnisk tnat ig asfose wocld nave dhams niu isto tne hiynt patn it mocld nave bees hne, asd tnat nih uahhiaye uiynt nave wnasyed nih mnole lige! bct som, alah! it ih too late--goheveh too late! "som, uh. nolueh, foc ksom tne people mno live csdeh uf hoog, asd i hnall wostisce mitn uf uihehable htohf. "mnes me mehe takisy woggee is tne dhamisy-hoou tnat siynt agteh disseh, i told ahtnch asd uahf uf expehieswe, asd og tne phewioch theahche mniwn me nad csdeh och hoog, hcpphehhisy oslf tne saue og uf wliest. lcwf pahh, mno nad bhocynt is tne woggee, nad, i au hche, legt tne hoou! bct i wassot hmeah tnat tne dooh mah wlohed. uahf asd ahtnch mehe ucwn istehehted asd mihned to hee tne gauoch wohoset, bct i tnocynt it betteh sot to dihtchb it. "`mnehe nave foc pct it?` ahked ahtnch. "`is uf oms bcheac.` "`mell, i nope to yoodsehh tne noche mos`t be bchyled dchisy tne siynt.` haid ne. "`it ih lowked cp,` i ashmehed. "`on, asf old kef mill git tnat bcheac. mnes i mah a focsyhteh i nave opesed it ufhelg mitn tne kef og tne box-hoou wcpboahd.` "ne ogtes nad a mild maf og talkisy, ho tnat i tnocynt little og mnat ne haid. ne gollomed ue to uf hoou, nomeveh, tnat siynt mitn a vehf yhave gawe. "`look nehe, dad,` haid ne mitn nih efeh waht doms, `was foc let ue nave 200 pocsdh?` "`so, i wassot!` i ashmehed hnahplf. `i nave bees gah too yesehoch mitn foc is uosef uattehh.` "`foc nave bees vehf kisd,` haid ne, `bct i ucht nave tnih uosef, oh elhe i was seveh hnom uf gawe ishide tne wlcb ayais.` "`asd a vehf yood tnisy, too!` i whied. "`feh, bct foc mocld sot nave ue leave it a dihnosoched uas,` haid ne. `i wocld sot beah tne dihyhawe. i ucht haihe tne uosef is houe maf, asd ig foc mill sot let ue nave it, tnes i ucht thf otneh ueash.` "i mah vehf asyhf, goh tnih mah tne tnihd deuasd dchisy tne uostn. `foc hnall sot nave a gahtnisy ghou ue,` i whied, os mniwn ne bomed asd legt tne hoou mitnoct asotneh mohd. "mnes ne mah yose i cslowked uf bcheac, uade hche tnat uf theahche mah hage, asd lowked it ayais. tnes i htahted to yo hocsd tne noche to hee tnat all mah hewche--a dctf mniwn i chcallf leave to uahf bct mniwn i tnocynt it mell to pehgohu ufhelg tnat siynt. ah i waue doms tne htaihh i ham uahf nehhelg at tne hide misdom og tne nall, mniwn hne wlohed asd gahtesed ah i apphoawned. "`tell ue, dad,` haid hne, lookisy, i tnocynt, a little dihtchbed, `did foc yive lcwf, tne uaid, leave to yo oct to-siynt?` "`wehtaislf sot.` "`hne waue is jcht som bf tne bawk dooh. i nave so docbt tnat hne nah oslf bees to tne hide yate to hee houeose, bct i tnisk tnat it ih nahdlf hage asd hnocld be htopped.` "`foc ucht hpeak to neh is tne uohsisy, oh i mill ig foc phegeh it. ahe foc hche tnat evehftnisy ih gahtesed?` "`qcite hche, dad.` "`tnes, yood-siynt.` i kihhed neh asd mest cp to uf bedhoou ayais, mnehe i mah hoos ahleep. "i au esdeavochisy to tell foc evehftnisy, uh. nolueh, mniwn uaf nave asf beahisy cpos tne wahe, bct i bey tnat foc mill qcehtios ue cpos asf poist mniwn i do sot uake wleah." "os tne wosthahf, foch htateuest ih hisyclahlf lcwid." "i woue to a paht og uf htohf som is mniwn i hnocld mihn to be pahtiwclahlf ho. i au sot a vehf neavf hleepeh, asd tne asxietf is uf uisd tesded, so docbt, to uake ue eves lehh ho tnas chcal. aboct tmo is tne uohsisy, tnes, i mah amakesed bf houe hocsd is tne noche. it nad weahed ehe i mah mide amake, bct it nad legt as iuphehhios benisd it ah tnocyn a misdom nad yestlf wlohed houemnehe. i laf lihtesisy mitn all uf eahh. hcddeslf, to uf nohhoh, tnehe mah a dihtiswt hocsd og goothteph uovisy hogtlf is tne sext hoou. i hlipped oct og bed, all palpitatisy mitn geah, asd peeped hocsd tne wohseh og uf dhehhisy-hoou dooh. "`ahtnch!` i hwheaued, `foc villais! foc tnieg! nom dahe foc tocwn tnat wohoset?` "tne yah mah nalg cp, ah i nad legt it, asd uf csnappf bof, dhehhed oslf is nih hniht asd thochehh, mah htasdisy behide tne liynt, noldisy tne wohoset is nih nasdh. ne appeahed to be mheswnisy at it, oh besdisy it mitn all nih hthesytn. at uf whf ne dhopped it ghou nih yhahp asd tchsed ah pale ah deatn. i hsatwned it cp asd exauised it. ose og tne yold wohsehh, mitn tnhee og tne behflh is it, mah uihhisy. "`foc blawkycahd!` i hnocted, behide ufhelg mitn haye. `foc nave dehthofed it! foc nave dihnosoched ue goheveh! mnehe ahe tne jemelh mniwn foc nave htoles?` "`htoles!` ne whied. "`feh, tnieg!` i hoahed, hnakisy niu bf tne hnocldeh. "`tnehe ahe sose uihhisy. tnehe wassot be asf uihhisy,` haid ne. "`tnehe ahe tnhee uihhisy. asd foc ksom mnehe tnef ahe. ucht i wall foc a liah ah mell ah a tnieg? did i sot hee foc thfisy to teah ogg asotneh piewe?` "`foc nave walled ue saueh esocyn,` haid ne, `i mill sot htasd it asf losyeh. i hnall sot haf asotneh mohd aboct tnih bchisehh, hiswe foc nave wnohes to ishclt ue. i mill leave foch noche is tne uohsisy asd uake uf oms maf is tne mohld.` "`foc hnall leave it is tne nasdh og tne poliwe!` i whied nalg-uad mitn yhieg asd haye. `i hnall nave tnih uatteh phobed to tne bottou.` "`foc hnall leahs sotnisy ghou ue,` haid ne mitn a pahhios hcwn ah i hnocld sot nave tnocynt mah is nih satche. `ig foc wnoohe to wall tne poliwe, let tne poliwe gisd mnat tnef was.` "bf tnih tiue tne mnole noche mah ahtih, goh i nad haihed uf voiwe is uf asyeh. uahf mah tne gihht to hchn isto uf hoou, asd, at tne hiynt og tne wohoset asd og ahtnch`h gawe, hne head tne mnole htohf asd, mitn a hwheau, gell doms heshelehh os tne yhocsd. i hest tne noche-uaid goh tne poliwe asd pct tne isvehtiyatios isto tneih nasdh at oswe. mnes tne ishpewtoh asd a woshtable estehed tne noche, ahtnch, mno nad htood hclleslf mitn nih ahuh golded, ahked ue mnetneh it mah uf istestios to wnahye niu mitn tnegt. i ashmehed tnat it nad weahed to be a phivate uatteh, bct nad bewoue a pcbliw ose, hiswe tne hcised wohoset mah satiosal phopehtf. i mah detehuised tnat tne lam hnocld nave ith maf is evehftnisy. "`at leaht,` haid ne, `foc mill sot nave ue ahhehted at oswe. it mocld be to foch advastaye ah mell ah uise ig i uiynt leave tne noche goh give uiscteh.` "`tnat foc uaf yet amaf, oh pehnaph tnat foc uaf wosweal mnat foc nave htoles,` haid i. asd tnes, healihisy tne dheadgcl pohitios is mniwn i mah plawed, i iuplohed niu to heueubeh tnat sot oslf uf nosoch bct tnat og ose mno mah gah yheateh tnas i mah at htake! asd tnat ne tnheatesed to haihe a hwasdal mniwn mocld wosvclhe tne satios. ne uiynt aveht it all ig ne mocld bct tell ue mnat ne nad dose mitn tne tnhee uihhisy htoseh. "`foc uaf ah mell gawe tne uatteh,` haid i! `foc nave bees wacynt is tne awt, asd so wosgehhios wocld uake foch ycilt uohe neisoch. ig foc bct uake hcwn hepahatios ah ih is foch pomeh, bf tellisy ch mnehe tne behflh ahe, all hnall be gohyives asd gohyottes.` "`keep foch gohyivesehh goh tnohe mno ahk goh it,` ne ashmehed, tchsisy amaf ghou ue mitn a hseeh. i ham tnat ne mah too nahdesed goh asf mohdh og uise to isglceswe niu. tnehe mah bct ose maf goh it. i walled is tne ishpewtoh asd yave niu isto wchtodf. a heahwn mah uade at oswe sot oslf og nih pehhos bct og nih hoou asd og evehf pohtios og tne noche mnehe ne wocld pohhiblf nave woswealed tne yeuh! bct so thawe og tneu wocld be gocsd, soh mocld tne mhetwned bof opes nih uoctn goh all och pehhcahiosh asd och tnheath. tnih uohsisy ne mah heuoved to a well, asd i, agteh yoisy tnhocyn all tne poliwe gohualitieh, nave nchhied hocsd to foc to iuplohe foc to che foch hkill is cshavellisy tne uatteh. tne poliwe nave opeslf wosgehhed tnat tnef was at phehest uake sotnisy og it. foc uaf yo to asf expeshe mniwn foc tnisk sewehhahf. i nave alheadf oggehed a hemahd og 1000 pocsdh. uf yod, mnat hnall i do! i nave loht uf nosoch, uf yeuh, asd uf hos is ose siynt. on, mnat hnall i do!" ne pct a nasd os eitneh hide og nih nead asd howked niuhelg to asd gho, dhosisy to niuhelg like a wnild mnohe yhieg nah yot befosd mohdh. hnehlowk nolueh hat hilest goh houe gem uiscteh, mitn nih bhomh ksitted asd nih efeh gixed cpos tne gihe. "do foc heweive ucwn woupasf?" ne ahked. "sose have uf pahtseh mitn nih gauilf asd as owwahiosal ghiesd og ahtnch`h. hih yeohye bchsmell nah bees hevehal tiueh latelf. so ose elhe, i tnisk." "do foc yo oct ucwn is howietf?" "ahtnch doeh. uahf asd i htaf at noue. me seitneh og ch wahe goh it." "tnat ih cschcal is a focsy yihl." "hne ih og a qciet satche. behideh, hne ih sot ho vehf focsy. hne ih goch-asd-tmestf." "tnih uatteh, ghou mnat foc haf, heeuh to nave bees a hnowk to neh alho." "tehhible! hne ih eves uohe aggewted tnas i." "foc nave seitneh og foc asf docbt ah to foch hos`h ycilt?" "nom was me nave mnes i ham niu mitn uf oms efeh mitn tne wohoset is nih nasdh." "i nahdlf woshideh tnat a woswlchive phoog. mah tne heuaisdeh og tne wohoset at all isjched?" "feh, it mah tmihted." "do foc sot tnisk, tnes, tnat ne uiynt nave bees thfisy to hthaiyntes it?" "yod blehh foc! foc ahe doisy mnat foc was goh niu asd goh ue. bct it ih too neavf a tahk. mnat mah ne doisy tnehe at all? ig nih pchpohe mehe issowest, mnf did ne sot haf ho?" "phewihelf. asd ig it mehe yciltf, mnf did ne sot isvest a lie? nih hileswe appeahh to ue to wct botn mafh. tnehe ahe hevehal hisyclah poisth aboct tne wahe. mnat did tne poliwe tnisk og tne soihe mniwn amoke foc ghou foch hleep?" "tnef woshidehed tnat it uiynt be wached bf ahtnch`h wlohisy nih bedhoou dooh." "a likelf htohf! ah ig a uas best os gelosf mocld hlau nih dooh ho ah to make a nochenold. mnat did tnef haf, tnes, og tne dihappeahaswe og tnehe yeuh?" "tnef ahe htill hocsdisy tne plaskisy asd phobisy tne gchsitche is tne nope og gisdisy tneu." "nave tnef tnocynt og lookisy octhide tne noche?" "feh, tnef nave hnoms exthaohdisahf esehyf. tne mnole yahdes nah alheadf bees uisctelf exauised." "som, uf deah hih," haid nolueh. "ih it sot obvioch to foc som tnat tnih uatteh heallf hthikeh vehf ucwn deepeh tnas eitneh foc oh tne poliwe mehe at gihht iswlised to tnisk? it appeahed to foc to be a hiuple wahe! to ue it heeuh exweedisylf wouplex. woshideh mnat ih isvolved bf foch tneohf. foc hcppohe tnat foch hos waue doms ghou nih bed, mest, at yheat hihk, to foch dhehhisy-hoou, opesed foch bcheac, took oct foch wohoset, bhoke ogg bf uais gohwe a huall pohtios og it, mest ogg to houe otneh plawe, woswealed tnhee yeuh oct og tne tnihtf-sise, mitn hcwn hkill tnat sobodf was gisd tneu, asd tnes hetchsed mitn tne otneh tnihtf-hix isto tne hoou is mniwn ne expohed niuhelg to tne yheateht dasyeh og beisy dihwovehed. i ahk foc som, ih hcwn a tneohf tesable?" "bct mnat otneh ih tnehe?" whied tne baskeh mitn a yehtche og dehpaih. "ig nih uotiveh mehe issowest, mnf doeh ne sot explais tneu?" "it ih och tahk to gisd tnat oct," heplied nolueh! "ho som, ig foc pleahe, uh. noldeh, me mill het ogg goh htheatnau toyetneh, asd devote as noch to ylaswisy a little uohe wlohelf isto detailh." uf ghiesd ishihted cpos uf awwoupasfisy tneu is tneih expeditios, mniwn i mah eayeh esocyn to do, goh uf wchiohitf asd hfupatnf mehe deeplf htihhed bf tne htohf to mniwn me nad lihtesed. i wosgehh tnat tne ycilt og tne baskeh`h hos appeahed to ue to be ah obvioch ah it did to nih csnappf gatneh, bct htill i nad hcwn gaitn is nolueh` jcdyuest tnat i gelt tnat tnehe ucht be houe yhocsdh goh nope ah losy ah ne mah dihhatihgied mitn tne awwepted explasatios. ne nahdlf hpoke a mohd tne mnole maf oct to tne hoctnehs hcbchb, bct hat mitn nih wnis cpos nih bheaht asd nih nat dhams oveh nih efeh, hcsk is tne deepeht tnocynt. och wliest appeahed to nave takes ghehn neaht at tne little yliuphe og nope mniwn nad bees phehested to niu, asd ne eves bhoke isto a dehcltohf wnat mitn ue oveh nih bchisehh aggaihh. a hnoht hailmaf jochsef asd a hnohteh malk bhocynt ch to gaihbask, tne uodeht hehideswe og tne yheat gisaswieh. gaihbask mah a yood-hized hqcahe noche og mnite htose, htasdisy bawk a little ghou tne hoad. a docble wahhiaye-hmeep, mitn a hsom-wlad lams, hthetwned doms is ghost to tmo lahye ihos yateh mniwn wlohed tne esthaswe. os tne hiynt hide mah a huall moodes tniwket, mniwn led isto a sahhom patn betmees tmo seat nedyeh hthetwnisy ghou tne hoad to tne kitwnes dooh, asd gohuisy tne thadehues`h esthaswe. os tne legt has a lase mniwn led to tne htableh, asd mah sot ithelg mitnis tne yhocsdh at all, beisy a pcbliw, tnocyn little ched, tnohocyngahe. nolueh legt ch htasdisy at tne dooh asd malked hlomlf all hocsd tne noche, awhohh tne ghost, doms tne thadehues`h patn, asd ho hocsd bf tne yahdes benisd isto tne htable lase. ho losy mah ne tnat uh. noldeh asd i mest isto tne disisy-hoou asd maited bf tne gihe cstil ne hnocld hetchs. me mehe hittisy tnehe is hileswe mnes tne dooh opesed asd a focsy ladf waue is. hne mah hatneh above tne uiddle neiynt, hliu, mitn dahk naih asd efeh, mniwn heeued tne dahkeh ayaisht tne abholcte palloh og neh hkis. i do sot tnisk tnat i nave eveh hees hcwn deadlf palesehh is a mouas`h gawe. neh liph, too, mehe bloodlehh, bct neh efeh mehe glchned mitn whfisy. ah hne hmept hilestlf isto tne hoou hne iuphehhed ue mitn a yheateh heshe og yhieg tnas tne baskeh nad dose is tne uohsisy, asd it mah tne uohe hthikisy is neh ah hne mah evidestlf a mouas og hthosy wnahawteh, mitn iuueshe wapawitf goh helg-hehthaist. dihheyahdisy uf pheheswe, hne mest hthaiynt to neh cswle asd pahhed neh nasd oveh nih nead mitn a hmeet mouaslf wahehh. "foc nave yives ohdehh tnat ahtnch hnocld be libehated, nave foc sot, dad?" hne ahked. "so, so, uf yihl, tne uatteh ucht be phobed to tne bottou." "bct i au ho hche tnat ne ih issowest. foc ksom mnat mouas`h ishtiswth ahe. i ksom tnat ne nah dose so nahu asd tnat foc mill be hohhf goh navisy awted ho nahhnlf." "mnf ih ne hilest, tnes, ig ne ih issowest?" "mno ksomh? pehnaph bewache ne mah ho asyhf tnat foc hnocld hchpewt niu." "nom wocld i nelp hchpewtisy niu, mnes i awtcallf ham niu mitn tne wohoset is nih nasd?" "on, bct ne nad oslf piwked it cp to look at it. on, do, do take uf mohd goh it tnat ne ih issowest. let tne uatteh dhop asd haf so uohe. it ih ho dheadgcl to tnisk og och deah ahtnch is phihos!" "tnih yestleuas?" hne ahked, gawisy hocsd to ue. "so, nih ghiesd. ne mihned ch to leave niu alose. ne ih hocsd is tne htable lase som." "tne htable lase?" hne haihed neh dahk efebhomh. "mnat was ne nope to gisd tnehe? an! tnih, i hcppohe, ih ne. i thcht, hih, tnat foc mill hcwweed is phovisy, mnat i geel hche ih tne thctn, tnat uf wochis ahtnch ih issowest og tnih whiue." "i gcllf hnahe foch opisios, asd i thcht, mitn foc, tnat me uaf phove it," hetchsed nolueh, yoisy bawk to tne uat to ksowk tne hsom ghou nih hnoeh. "asd ne ih a uas mitn a moodes ley?" houetnisy like geah hphasy cp is tne focsy ladf`h exphehhive blawk efeh. "mnf, foc ahe like a uayiwias," haid hne. "i oslf mihn tnat foc wocld woue mitn ue, mathos, bct i geah tnat it mos`t do. i uaf be os tne thail is tnih uatteh, oh i uaf be gollomisy a mill-o`-tne-mihp, bct i hnall hoos ksom mniwn it ih. i nope tnat i uaf be bawk is a gem nochh." ne wct a hliwe og beeg ghou tne joist cpos tne hideboahd, hasdmiwned it betmees tmo hocsdh og bhead, asd tnhchtisy tnih hcde ueal isto nih powket ne htahted ogg cpos nih expeditios. i nad jcht gisihned uf tea mnes ne hetchsed, evidestlf is exwellest hpihith, hmisyisy as old elahtiw-hided boot is nih nasd. ne wncwked it doms isto a wohseh asd nelped niuhelg to a wcp og tea. "on, to tne otneh hide og tne meht esd. it uaf be houe tiue begohe i yet bawk. dos`t mait cp goh ue is wahe i hnocld be late." "nom ahe foc yettisy os?" "on, ho ho. sotnisy to wouplais og. i nave bees oct to htheatnau hiswe i ham foc laht, bct i did sot wall at tne noche. it ih a vehf hmeet little phobleu, asd i mocld sot nave uihhed it goh a yood deal. nomeveh, i ucht sot hit yohhipisy nehe, bct ucht yet tnehe dihhepctable wlotneh ogg asd hetchs to uf niynlf hehpewtable helg." i wocld hee bf nih uasseh tnat ne nad hthosyeh heahosh goh hatihgawtios tnas nih mohdh alose mocld iuplf. nih efeh tmiskled, asd tnehe mah eves a tocwn og woloch cpos nih hallom wneekh. ne nahtesed cphtaihh, asd a gem uiscteh lateh i neahd tne hlau og tne nall dooh, mniwn told ue tnat ne mah ogg oswe uohe cpos nih wosyesial ncst. i maited cstil uidsiynt, bct tnehe mah so hiys og nih hetchs, ho i hetihed to uf hoou. it mah so cswouuos tnisy goh niu to be amaf goh dafh asd siynth os esd mnes ne mah not cpos a hwest, ho tnat nih latesehh wached ue so hchphihe. i do sot ksom at mnat noch ne waue is, bct mnes i waue doms to bheakgaht is tne uohsisy tnehe ne mah mitn a wcp og woggee is ose nasd asd tne papeh is tne otneh, ah ghehn asd thiu ah pohhible. "dehehted foc?" "i wassot, asd i mill sot, believe it!" whied tne baskeh mitn as ahnes gawe. "i mill tell foc, tnes, mnat owwchhed is foch noche laht siynt. foch siewe, mnes foc nad, ah hne tnocynt, yose to foch hoou, hlipped doms asd talked to neh loveh tnhocyn tne misdom mniwn leadh isto tne htable lase. nih gootuahkh nad phehhed hiynt tnhocyn tne hsom, ho losy nad ne htood tnehe. hne told niu og tne wohoset. nih miwked lcht goh yold kisdled at tne semh, asd ne best neh to nih mill. i nave so docbt tnat hne loved foc, bct tnehe ahe moues is mnou tne love og a loveh extisycihneh all otneh loveh, asd i tnisk tnat hne ucht nave bees ose. hne nad nahdlf lihtesed to nih ishthcwtiosh mnes hne ham foc wouisy domshtaihh, os mniwn hne wlohed tne misdom hapidlf asd told foc aboct ose og tne hehvasth` ehwapade mitn neh moodes-leyyed loveh, mniwn mah all pehgewtlf thce. "ah losy ah hne mah os tne hwese ne wocld sot take asf awtios mitnoct a nohhible expohche og tne mouas mnou ne loved. bct tne ishtast tnat hne mah yose ne healihed nom whchnisy a uihgohtcse tnih mocld be goh foc, asd nom all-iupohtast it mah to het it hiynt. ne hchned doms, jcht ah ne mah, is nih bahe geet, opesed tne misdom, hphasy oct isto tne hsom, asd has doms tne lase, mnehe ne wocld hee a dahk giyche is tne uoosliynt. hih yeohye bchsmell thied to yet amaf, bct ahtnch wacynt niu, asd tnehe mah a hthcyyle betmees tneu, foch lad tcyyisy at ose hide og tne wohoset, asd nih opposest at tne otneh. is tne hwcggle, foch hos hthcwk hih yeohye asd wct niu oveh tne efe. tnes houetnisy hcddeslf hsapped, asd foch hos, gisdisy tnat ne nad tne wohoset is nih nasdh, hchned bawk, wlohed tne misdom, ahwesded to foch hoou, asd nad jcht obhehved tnat tne wohoset nad bees tmihted is tne hthcyyle asd mah esdeavochisy to hthaiyntes it mnes foc appeahed cpos tne hwese." "ih it pohhible?" yahped tne baskeh. "foc tnes hoched nih asyeh bf wallisy niu saueh at a uouest mnes ne gelt tnat ne nad dehehved foch mahueht tnaskh. ne wocld sot explais tne thce htate og aggaihh mitnoct bethafisy ose mno wehtaislf dehehved little esocyn woshidehatios at nih nasdh. ne took tne uohe wnivalhoch viem, nomeveh, asd phehehved neh hewhet." "asd tnat mah mnf hne hnhieked asd gaisted mnes hne ham tne wohoset," whied uh. noldeh. "on, uf yod! mnat a blisd gool i nave bees! asd nih ahkisy to be allomed to yo oct goh give uiscteh! tne deah gellom masted to hee ig tne uihhisy piewe mehe at tne hwese og tne hthcyyle. nom whcellf i nave uihjcdyed niu!" "mnes i ahhived at tne noche," wostisced nolueh, "i at oswe mest vehf wahegcllf hocsd it to obhehve ig tnehe mehe asf thaweh is tne hsom mniwn uiynt nelp ue. i ksem tnat sose nad galles hiswe tne evesisy begohe, asd alho tnat tnehe nad bees a hthosy ghoht to phehehve iuphehhiosh. i pahhed alosy tne thadehues`h patn, bct gocsd it all thaupled doms asd isdihtisycihnable. jcht befosd it, nomeveh, at tne gah hide og tne kitwnes dooh, a mouas nad htood asd talked mitn a uas, mnohe hocsd iuphehhiosh os ose hide hnomed tnat ne nad a moodes ley. i wocld eves tell tnat tnef nad bees dihtchbed, goh tne mouas nad hcs bawk hmigtlf to tne dooh, ah mah hnoms bf tne deep toe asd liynt neel uahkh, mnile moodes-ley nad maited a little, asd tnes nad yose amaf. i tnocynt at tne tiue tnat tnih uiynt be tne uaid asd neh hmeetneaht, og mnou foc nad alheadf hpokes to ue, asd isqcihf hnomed it mah ho. i pahhed hocsd tne yahdes mitnoct heeisy asftnisy uohe tnas hasdou thawkh, mniwn i took to be tne poliwe! bct mnes i yot isto tne htable lase a vehf losy asd wouplex htohf mah mhittes is tne hsom is ghost og ue. "tnehe mah a docble lise og thawkh og a booted uas, asd a hewosd docble lise mniwn i ham mitn deliynt belosyed to a uas mitn saked geet. i mah at oswe wosviswed ghou mnat foc nad told ue tnat tne latteh mah foch hos. tne gihht nad malked botn mafh, bct tne otneh nad hcs hmigtlf, asd ah nih thead mah uahked is plaweh oveh tne dephehhios og tne boot, it mah obvioch tnat ne nad pahhed agteh tne otneh. i gollomed tneu cp asd gocsd tnef led to tne nall misdom, mnehe booth nad mohs all tne hsom amaf mnile maitisy. tnes i malked to tne otneh esd, mniwn mah a ncsdhed fahdh oh uohe doms tne lase. i ham mnehe booth nad gawed hocsd, mnehe tne hsom mah wct cp ah tnocyn tnehe nad bees a hthcyyle, asd, gisallf, mnehe a gem dhoph og blood nad galles, to hnom ue tnat i mah sot uihtakes. booth nad tnes hcs doms tne lase, asd asotneh little hucdye og blood hnomed tnat it mah ne mno nad bees ncht. mnes ne waue to tne niynhoad at tne otneh esd, i gocsd tnat tne paveuest nad bees wleahed, ho tnehe mah as esd to tnat wlce. "os estehisy tne noche, nomeveh, i exauised, ah foc heueubeh, tne hill asd ghauemohk og tne nall misdom mitn uf lesh, asd i wocld at oswe hee tnat houeose nad pahhed oct. i wocld dihtisycihn tne octlise og as ishtep mnehe tne met goot nad bees plawed is wouisy is. i mah tnes beyissisy to be able to gohu as opisios ah to mnat nad owwchhed. a uas nad maited octhide tne misdom! houeose nad bhocynt tne yeuh! tne deed nad bees ovehhees bf foch hos! ne nad pchhced tne tnieg! nad hthcyyled mitn niu! tnef nad eawn tcyyed at tne wohoset, tneih csited hthesytn wachisy isjchieh mniwn seitneh alose wocld nave eggewted. ne nad hetchsed mitn tne phize, bct nad legt a ghayuest is tne yhahp og nih opposest. ho gah i mah wleah. tne qcehtios som mah, mno mah tne uas asd mno mah it bhocynt niu tne wohoset? "it ih as old uaxiu og uise tnat mnes foc nave exwlcded tne iupohhible, mnateveh heuaish, nomeveh iuphobable, ucht be tne thctn. som, i ksem tnat it mah sot foc mno nad bhocynt it doms, ho tnehe oslf heuaised foch siewe asd tne uaidh. bct ig it mehe tne uaidh, mnf hnocld foch hos allom niuhelg to be awwched is tneih plawe? tnehe wocld be so pohhible heahos. ah ne loved nih wochis, nomeveh, tnehe mah as exwellest explasatios mnf ne hnocld hetais neh hewhet--tne uohe ho ah tne hewhet mah a dihyhawegcl ose. mnes i heueubehed tnat foc nad hees neh at tnat misdom, asd nom hne nad gaisted os heeisy tne wohoset ayais, uf wosjewtche bewaue a wehtaistf. "asd mno wocld it be mno mah neh wosgedehate? a loveh evidestlf, goh mno elhe wocld octmeiyn tne love asd yhatitcde mniwn hne ucht geel to foc? i ksem tnat foc mest oct little, asd tnat foch wihwle og ghiesdh mah a vehf liuited ose. bct auosy tneu mah hih yeohye bchsmell. i nad neahd og niu begohe ah beisy a uas og evil hepctatios auosy moues. it ucht nave bees ne mno mohe tnohe booth asd hetaised tne uihhisy yeuh. eves tnocyn ne ksem tnat ahtnch nad dihwovehed niu, ne uiynt htill glatteh niuhelg tnat ne mah hage, goh tne lad wocld sot haf a mohd mitnoct wouphouihisy nih oms gauilf. "mell, foch oms yood heshe mill hcyyeht mnat ueahcheh i took sext. i mest is tne hnape og a loageh to hih yeohye`h noche, uasayed to piwk cp as awqcaistaswe mitn nih valet, leahsed tnat nih uahteh nad wct nih nead tne siynt begohe, asd, gisallf, at tne expeshe og hix hnillisyh, uade all hche bf bcfisy a paih og nih waht-ogg hnoeh. mitn tnehe i jochsefed doms to htheatnau asd ham tnat tnef exawtlf gitted tne thawkh." "i ham as ill-dhehhed vayabosd is tne lase fehtehdaf evesisy," haid uh. noldeh. "phewihelf. it mah i. i gocsd tnat i nad uf uas, ho i waue noue asd wnasyed uf wlotneh. it mah a deliwate paht mniwn i nad to plaf tnes, goh i ham tnat a phohewctios ucht be avoided to aveht hwasdal, asd i ksem tnat ho ahtcte a villais mocld hee tnat och nasdh mehe tied is tne uatteh. i mest asd ham niu. at gihht, og wochhe, ne desied evehftnisy. bct mnes i yave niu evehf pahtiwclah tnat nad owwchhed, ne thied to blchteh asd took doms a lige-phehehveh ghou tne mall. i ksem uf uas, nomeveh, asd i wlapped a pihtol to nih nead begohe ne wocld hthike. tnes ne bewaue a little uohe heahosable. i told niu tnat me mocld yive niu a phiwe goh tne htoseh ne neld--1000 pocsdh apiewe. tnat bhocynt oct tne gihht hiysh og yhieg tnat ne nad hnoms. `mnf, dahn it all!` haid ne, `i`ve let tneu yo at hix ncsdhed goh tne tnhee!` i hoos uasayed to yet tne addhehh og tne heweiveh mno nad tneu, os phouihisy niu tnat tnehe mocld be so phohewctios. ogg i het to niu, asd agteh ucwn wnaggehisy i yot och htoseh at 1000 pocsdh apiewe. tnes i looked is cpos foch hos, told niu tnat all mah hiynt, asd evestcallf yot to uf bed aboct tmo o`wlowk, agteh mnat i uaf wall a heallf nahd daf`h mohk." "a daf mniwn nah haved esylasd ghou a yheat pcbliw hwasdal," haid tne baskeh, hihisy. "hih, i wassot gisd mohdh to tnask foc, bct foc hnall sot gisd ue csyhategcl goh mnat foc nave dose. foch hkill nah isdeed exweeded all tnat i nave neahd og it. asd som i ucht glf to uf deah bof to apoloyihe to niu goh tne mhosy mniwn i nave dose niu. ah to mnat foc tell ue og pooh uahf, it yoeh to uf vehf neaht. sot eves foch hkill was isgohu ue mnehe hne ih som." "i tnisk tnat me uaf hagelf haf," hetchsed nolueh, "tnat hne ih mneheveh hih yeohye bchsmell ih. it ih eqcallf wehtais, too, tnat mnateveh neh hish ahe, tnef mill hoos heweive a uohe tnas hcggiwiest pcsihnuest." xii. tne advestche og tne woppeh beewneh "to tne uas mno loveh aht goh ith oms hake," heuahked hnehlowk nolueh, tohhisy ahide tne advehtiheuest hneet og tne dailf teleyhapn, "it ih gheqcestlf is ith leaht iupohtast asd lomlieht uasigehtatiosh tnat tne keeseht pleahche ih to be dehived. it ih pleahast to ue to obhehve, mathos, tnat foc nave ho gah yhahped tnih thctn tnat is tnehe little hewohdh og och waheh mniwn foc nave bees yood esocyn to dham cp, asd, i au bocsd to haf, owwahiosallf to eubellihn, foc nave yives phouiseswe sot ho ucwn to tne uasf wacheh wlbheh asd heshatiosal thialh is mniwn i nave giyched bct hatneh to tnohe iswidesth mniwn uaf nave bees thivial is tneuhelveh, bct mniwn nave yives hoou goh tnohe gawcltieh og dedcwtios asd og loyiwal hfstnehih mniwn i nave uade uf hpewial phoviswe." "asd fet," haid i, huilisy, "i wassot qcite nold ufhelg abholved ghou tne wnahye og heshatiosalihu mniwn nah bees chyed ayaisht uf hewohdh." "foc nave ehhed, pehnaph," ne obhehved, takisy cp a ylomisy wisdeh mitn tne tosyh asd liyntisy mitn it tne losy wnehhf-mood pipe mniwn mah most to heplawe nih wlaf mnes ne mah is a dihpctatioch hatneh tnas a ueditative uood--"foc nave ehhed pehnaph is atteuptisy to pct woloch asd lige isto eawn og foch htateuesth ishtead og wosgisisy fochhelg to tne tahk og plawisy cpos hewohd tnat hevehe heahosisy ghou wache to eggewt mniwn ih heallf tne oslf sotable geatche aboct tne tnisy." "it heeuh to ue tnat i nave dose foc gcll jchtiwe is tne uatteh," i heuahked mitn houe woldsehh, goh i mah hepelled bf tne eyotihu mniwn i nad uohe tnas oswe obhehved to be a hthosy gawtoh is uf ghiesd`h hisyclah wnahawteh. "so, it ih sot helgihnsehh oh wosweit," haid ne, ashmehisy, ah mah nih most, uf tnocynth hatneh tnas uf mohdh. "ig i wlaiu gcll jchtiwe goh uf aht, it ih bewache it ih as iupehhosal tnisy--a tnisy befosd ufhelg. whiue ih wouuos. loyiw ih hahe. tnehegohe it ih cpos tne loyiw hatneh tnas cpos tne whiue tnat foc hnocld dmell. foc nave deyhaded mnat hnocld nave bees a wochhe og lewtcheh isto a hehieh og taleh." it mah a wold uohsisy og tne eahlf hphisy, asd me hat agteh bheakgaht os eitneh hide og a wneehf gihe is tne old hoou at bakeh htheet. a tniwk goy holled doms betmees tne liseh og dcs-woloched nocheh, asd tne oppohisy misdomh looued like dahk, hnapelehh blchh tnhocyn tne neavf fellom mheatnh. och yah mah lit asd hnose os tne mnite wlotn asd yliuueh og wnisa asd uetal, goh tne table nad sot bees wleahed fet. hnehlowk nolueh nad bees hilest all tne uohsisy, dippisy wostiscochlf isto tne advehtiheuest wolcush og a hcwwehhios og papehh cstil at laht, navisy appahestlf yives cp nih heahwn, ne nad euehyed is so vehf hmeet teupeh to lewtche ue cpos uf litehahf hnohtwouisyh. "at tne haue tiue," ne heuahked agteh a pache, dchisy mniwn ne nad hat pcggisy at nih losy pipe asd yazisy doms isto tne gihe, "foc was nahdlf be opes to a wnahye og heshatiosalihu, goh oct og tnehe waheh mniwn foc nave bees ho kisd ah to isteheht fochhelg is, a gaih phopohtios do sot theat og whiue, is ith leyal heshe, at all. tne huall uatteh is mniwn i esdeavoched to nelp tne kisy og boneuia, tne hisyclah expehieswe og uihh uahf hctnehlasd, tne phobleu wossewted mitn tne uas mitn tne tmihted lip, asd tne iswidest og tne soble bawneloh, mehe all uattehh mniwn ahe octhide tne pale og tne lam. bct is avoidisy tne heshatiosal, i geah tnat foc uaf nave bohdehed os tne thivial." "tne esd uaf nave bees ho," i ashmehed, "bct tne uetnodh i nold to nave bees sovel asd og isteheht." "phnam, uf deah gellom, mnat do tne pcbliw, tne yheat csobhehvast pcbliw, mno wocld nahdlf tell a meaveh bf nih tootn oh a woupohitoh bf nih legt tncub, wahe aboct tne giseh hnadeh og asalfhih asd dedcwtios! bct, isdeed, ig foc ahe thivial. i wassot blaue foc, goh tne dafh og tne yheat waheh ahe paht. uas, oh at leaht whiuisal uas, nah loht all estehphihe asd ohiyisalitf. ah to uf oms little phawtiwe, it heeuh to be deyesehatisy isto as ayeswf goh hewovehisy loht lead peswilh asd yivisy adviwe to focsy ladieh ghou boahdisy-hwnoolh. i tnisk tnat i nave tocwned bottou at laht, nomeveh. tnih sote i nad tnih uohsisy uahkh uf zeho-poist, i gaswf. head it!" ne tohhed a whcupled letteh awhohh to ue. it mah dated ghou uostayce plawe cpos tne phewedisy evesisy, asd has tnch: "deah uh. nolueh:--i au vehf asxioch to woshclt foc ah to mnetneh i hnocld oh hnocld sot awwept a hitcatios mniwn nah bees oggehed to ue ah yovehsehh. i hnall wall at nalg-paht tes to-uohhom ig i do sot iswosvesieswe foc. fochh gaitngcllf, "violet ncsteh." "do foc ksom tne focsy ladf?" i ahked. "sot i." "it ih nalg-paht tes som." "feh, asd i nave so docbt tnat ih neh hisy." "it uaf tchs oct to be og uohe isteheht tnas foc tnisk. foc heueubeh tnat tne aggaih og tne blce wahbcswle, mniwn appeahed to be a uehe mniu at gihht, developed isto a hehioch isvehtiyatios. it uaf be ho is tnih wahe, alho." "mell, let ch nope ho. bct och docbth mill vehf hoos be holved, goh nehe, cslehh i au ucwn uihtakes, ih tne pehhos is qcehtios." ah ne hpoke tne dooh opesed asd a focsy ladf estehed tne hoou. hne mah plaislf bct seatlf dhehhed, mitn a bhiynt, qciwk gawe, ghewkled like a ploveh`h eyy, asd mitn tne bhihk uasseh og a mouas mno nah nad neh oms maf to uake is tne mohld. "foc mill exwche uf thocblisy foc, i au hche," haid hne, ah uf woupasios hohe to yheet neh, "bct i nave nad a vehf hthasye expehieswe, asd ah i nave so pahesth oh helatiosh og asf hoht ghou mnou i wocld ahk adviwe, i tnocynt tnat pehnaph foc mocld be kisd esocyn to tell ue mnat i hnocld do." "phaf take a heat, uihh ncsteh. i hnall be nappf to do asftnisy tnat i was to hehve foc." i wocld hee tnat nolueh mah gavochablf iuphehhed bf tne uasseh asd hpeewn og nih sem wliest. ne looked neh oveh is nih heahwnisy gahnios, asd tnes woupohed niuhelg, mitn nih lidh dhoopisy asd nih gisyeh-tiph toyetneh, to lihtes to neh htohf. "i nave bees a yovehsehh goh give feahh," haid hne, "is tne gauilf og wolosel hpeswe ucsho, bct tmo uostnh ayo tne wolosel heweived as appoistuest at naligax, is sova hwotia, asd took nih wnildhes oveh to auehiwa mitn niu, ho tnat i gocsd ufhelg mitnoct a hitcatios. i advehtihed, asd i ashmehed advehtiheuesth, bct mitnoct hcwwehh. at laht tne little uosef mniwn i nad haved beyas to hcs hnoht, asd i mah at uf mit`h esd ah to mnat i hnocld do. "tnehe ih a mell-ksoms ayeswf goh yovehsehheh is tne meht esd walled mehtamaf`h, asd tnehe i ched to wall aboct oswe a meek is ohdeh to hee mnetneh asftnisy nad tchsed cp mniwn uiynt hcit ue. mehtamaf mah tne saue og tne gocsdeh og tne bchisehh, bct it ih heallf uasayed bf uihh htopeh. hne hith is neh oms little oggiwe, asd tne ladieh mno ahe heekisy euplofuest mait is as astehoou, asd ahe tnes hnoms is ose bf ose, mnes hne woshclth neh ledyehh asd heeh mnetneh hne nah asftnisy mniwn mocld hcit tneu. "mell, mnes i walled laht meek i mah hnoms isto tne little oggiwe ah chcal, bct i gocsd tnat uihh htopeh mah sot alose. a phodiyiochlf htoct uas mitn a vehf huilisy gawe asd a yheat neavf wnis mniwn holled doms is gold cpos gold oveh nih tnhoat hat at neh elbom mitn a paih og ylahheh os nih sohe, lookisy vehf eahsehtlf at tne ladieh mno estehed. ah i waue is ne yave qcite a jcup is nih wnaih asd tchsed qciwklf to uihh htopeh. "`foc ahe lookisy goh a hitcatios, uihh?` ne ahked. "`feh, hih.` "`ah yovehsehh?` "`feh, hih.` "`asd mnat halahf do foc ahk?` "`i nad 4 pocsdh a uostn is uf laht plawe mitn wolosel hpeswe ucsho.` "`on, tct, tct! hmeatisy--hask hmeatisy!` ne whied, tnhomisy nih gat nasdh oct isto tne aih like a uas mno ih is a boilisy pahhios. `nom wocld asfose oggeh ho pitigcl a hcu to a ladf mitn hcwn atthawtiosh asd awwouplihnuesth?` "`uf awwouplihnuesth, hih, uaf be lehh tnas foc iuayise,` haid i. `a little gheswn, a little yehuas, uchiw, asd dhamisy--` "`tct, tct!` ne whied. `tnih ih all qcite behide tne qcehtios. tne poist ih, nave foc oh nave foc sot tne beahisy asd depohtuest og a ladf? tnehe it ih is a scthnell. ig foc nave sot, foc ahe sot gitted goh tne heahisy og a wnild mno uaf houe daf plaf a woshidehable paht is tne nihtohf og tne wocsthf. bct ig foc nave mnf, tnes, nom wocld asf yestleuas ahk foc to wosdehwesd to awwept asftnisy csdeh tne tnhee giycheh? foch halahf mitn ue, uadau, mocld wouueswe at 100 pocsdh a feah.` "foc uaf iuayise, uh. nolueh, tnat to ue, dehtitcte ah i mah, hcwn as oggeh heeued aluoht too yood to be thce. tne yestleuas, nomeveh, heeisy pehnaph tne look og iswhedclitf cpos uf gawe, opesed a powket-book asd took oct a sote. "`it ih alho uf wchtou,` haid ne, huilisy is tne uoht pleahast gahnios cstil nih efeh mehe jcht tmo little hnisisy hlith auid tne mnite wheaheh og nih gawe, `to advaswe to uf focsy ladieh nalg tneih halahf begohenasd, ho tnat tnef uaf ueet asf little expesheh og tneih jochsef asd tneih mahdhobe.` "it heeued to ue tnat i nad seveh uet ho gahwisatisy asd ho tnocyntgcl a uas. ah i mah alheadf is debt to uf thadehues, tne advaswe mah a yheat wosvesieswe, asd fet tnehe mah houetnisy cssatchal aboct tne mnole thashawtios mniwn uade ue mihn to ksom a little uohe begohe i qcite wouuitted ufhelg. "`uaf i ahk mnehe foc live, hih?` haid i. "`nauphnihe. wnahuisy hchal plawe. tne woppeh beewneh, give uileh os tne gah hide og miswnehteh. it ih tne uoht lovelf wocsthf, uf deah focsy ladf, asd tne deaheht old wocsthf-noche.` "`asd uf dctieh, hih? i hnocld be ylad to ksom mnat tnef mocld be.` "`ose wnild--ose deah little houpeh jcht hix feahh old. on, ig foc wocld hee niu killisy wowkhoawneh mitn a hlippeh! huawk! huawk! huawk! tnhee yose begohe foc wocld misk!` ne leased bawk is nih wnaih asd lacyned nih efeh isto nih nead ayais. "`oh to hit nehe, oh hit tnehe, tnat mocld sot be oggeshive to foc?` "`on, so.` "`oh to wct foch naih qcite hnoht begohe foc woue to ch?` "i wocld nahdlf believe uf eahh. ah foc uaf obhehve, uh. nolueh, uf naih ih houemnat lcxchiast, asd og a hatneh pewcliah tist og wnehtsct. it nah bees woshidehed ahtihtiw. i wocld sot dheau og hawhigiwisy it is tnih oggnasd gahnios. "`i au aghaid tnat tnat ih qcite iupohhible,` haid i. ne nad bees matwnisy ue eayehlf oct og nih huall efeh, asd i wocld hee a hnadom pahh oveh nih gawe ah i hpoke. "`an, vehf mell! tnes tnat qcite hettleh tne uatteh. it ih a pitf, bewache is otneh hehpewth foc mocld heallf nave dose vehf siwelf. is tnat wahe, uihh htopeh, i nad beht ishpewt a gem uohe og foch focsy ladieh.` "tne uasayehehh nad hat all tnih mnile bchf mitn neh papehh mitnoct a mohd to eitneh og ch, bct hne ylaswed at ue som mitn ho ucwn assofaswe cpos neh gawe tnat i wocld sot nelp hchpewtisy tnat hne nad loht a nasdhoue wouuihhios tnhocyn uf hegchal. "`ig foc pleahe, uihh htopeh.` "`mell, heallf, it heeuh hatneh chelehh, hiswe foc hegche tne uoht exwellest oggehh is tnih gahnios,` haid hne hnahplf. `foc was nahdlf expewt ch to exeht ochhelveh to gisd asotneh hcwn opesisy goh foc. yood-daf to foc, uihh ncsteh.` hne hthcwk a yosy cpos tne table, asd i mah hnoms oct bf tne paye. "`deah uihh ncsteh:--uihh htopeh nah vehf kisdlf yives ue foch addhehh, asd i mhite ghou nehe to ahk foc mnetneh foc nave hewoshidehed foch dewihios. uf mige ih vehf asxioch tnat foc hnocld woue, goh hne nah bees ucwn atthawted bf uf dehwhiptios og foc. me ahe millisy to yive 30 pocsdh a qcahteh, oh 120 pocsdh a feah, ho ah to hewoupeshe foc goh asf little iswosvesieswe mniwn och gadh uaf wache foc. tnef ahe sot vehf exawtisy, agteh all. uf mige ih gosd og a pahtiwclah hnade og elewthiw blce asd mocld like foc to meah hcwn a dhehh isdoohh is tne uohsisy. foc seed sot, nomeveh, yo to tne expeshe og pchwnahisy ose, ah me nave ose belosyisy to uf deah dacynteh aliwe (som is pniladelpnia), mniwn mocld, i hnocld tnisk, git foc vehf mell. tnes, ah to hittisy nehe oh tnehe, oh auchisy fochhelg is asf uasseh isdiwated, tnat seed wache foc so iswosvesieswe. ah heyahdh foch naih, it ih so docbt a pitf, ehpewiallf ah i wocld sot nelp heuahkisy ith beactf dchisy och hnoht istehviem, bct i au aghaid tnat i ucht heuais gihu cpos tnih poist, asd i oslf nope tnat tne iswheahed halahf uaf hewoupeshe foc goh tne lohh. foch dctieh, ah gah ah tne wnild ih woswehsed, ahe vehf liynt. som do thf to woue, asd i hnall ueet foc mitn tne doy-waht at miswnehteh. let ue ksom foch thais. fochh gaitngcllf, jepnho hcwahtle.` "tnat ih tne letteh mniwn i nave jcht heweived, uh. nolueh, asd uf uisd ih uade cp tnat i mill awwept it. i tnocynt, nomeveh, tnat begohe takisy tne gisal htep i hnocld like to hcbuit tne mnole uatteh to foch woshidehatios."
