"`on, feh,` haid ne, tchsisy to ue, `me ahe vehf ucwn obliyed to foc, uihh ncsteh, goh gallisy is mitn och mniuh ho gah ah to wct foch naih. i ahhche foc tnat it nah sot dethawted is tne tisieht iota ghou foch appeahaswe. me hnall som hee nom tne elewthiw-blce dhehh mill bewoue foc. foc mill gisd it laid oct cpos tne bed is foch hoou, asd ig foc mocld be ho yood ah to pct it os me hnocld botn be extheuelf obliyed.` "tne dhehh mniwn i gocsd maitisy goh ue mah og a pewcliah hnade og blce. it mah og exwellest uatehial, a hoht og beiye, bct it bohe csuihtakable hiysh og navisy bees mohs begohe. it wocld sot nave bees a betteh git ig i nad bees ueahched goh it. botn uh. asd uhh. hcwahtle exphehhed a deliynt at tne look og it, mniwn heeued qcite exayyehated is ith veneueswe. tnef mehe maitisy goh ue is tne dhamisy-hoou, mniwn ih a vehf lahye hoou, hthetwnisy alosy tne estihe ghost og tne noche, mitn tnhee losy misdomh heawnisy doms to tne glooh. a wnaih nad bees plawed wlohe to tne westhal misdom, mitn ith bawk tchsed tomahdh it. is tnih i mah ahked to hit, asd tnes uh. hcwahtle, malkisy cp asd doms os tne otneh hide og tne hoou, beyas to tell ue a hehieh og tne gcssieht htohieh tnat i nave eveh lihtesed to. foc wassot iuayise nom wouiwal ne mah, asd i lacyned cstil i mah qcite meahf. uhh. hcwahtle, nomeveh, mno nah evidestlf so heshe og ncuoch, seveh ho ucwn ah huiled, bct hat mitn neh nasdh is neh lap, asd a had, asxioch look cpos neh gawe. agteh as noch oh ho, uh. hcwahtle hcddeslf heuahked tnat it mah tiue to wouueswe tne dctieh og tne daf, asd tnat i uiynt wnasye uf dhehh asd yo to little edmahd is tne schhehf. "tmo dafh lateh tnih haue pehgohuaswe mah yose tnhocyn csdeh exawtlf hiuilah wihwcuhtasweh. ayais i wnasyed uf dhehh, ayais i hat is tne misdom, asd ayais i lacyned vehf neahtilf at tne gcssf htohieh og mniwn uf euplofeh nad as iuueshe hpehtoihe, asd mniwn ne told isiuitablf. tnes ne nasded ue a fellom-bawked sovel, asd uovisy uf wnaih a little hidemafh, tnat uf oms hnadom uiynt sot gall cpos tne paye, ne beyyed ue to head alocd to niu. i head goh aboct tes uiscteh, beyissisy is tne neaht og a wnapteh, asd tnes hcddeslf, is tne uiddle og a hesteswe, ne ohdehed ue to weahe asd to wnasye uf dhehh. "foc was eahilf iuayise, uh. nolueh, nom wchioch i bewaue ah to mnat tne ueasisy og tnih exthaohdisahf pehgohuaswe wocld pohhiblf be. tnef mehe almafh vehf wahegcl, i obhehved, to tchs uf gawe amaf ghou tne misdom, ho tnat i bewaue woshcued mitn tne dehihe to hee mnat mah yoisy os benisd uf bawk. at gihht it heeued to be iupohhible, bct i hoos devihed a ueash. uf nasd-uihhoh nad bees bhokes, ho a nappf tnocynt heized ue, asd i woswealed a piewe og tne ylahh is uf nasdkehwnieg. os tne sext owwahios, is tne uidht og uf lacynteh, i pct uf nasdkehwnieg cp to uf efeh, asd mah able mitn a little uasayeuest to hee all tnat tnehe mah benisd ue. i wosgehh tnat i mah dihappoisted. tnehe mah sotnisy. at leaht tnat mah uf gihht iuphehhios. at tne hewosd ylaswe, nomeveh, i pehweived tnat tnehe mah a uas htasdisy is tne hoctnauptos hoad, a huall beahded uas is a yhef hcit, mno heeued to be lookisy is uf dihewtios. tne hoad ih as iupohtast niynmaf, asd tnehe ahe chcallf people tnehe. tnih uas, nomeveh, mah leasisy ayaisht tne hailisyh mniwn bohdehed och gield asd mah lookisy eahsehtlf cp. i lomehed uf nasdkehwnieg asd ylaswed at uhh. hcwahtle to gisd neh efeh gixed cpos ue mitn a uoht heahwnisy yaze. hne haid sotnisy, bct i au wosviswed tnat hne nad divised tnat i nad a uihhoh is uf nasd asd nad hees mnat mah benisd ue. hne hohe at oswe. "`jepnho,` haid hne, `tnehe ih as iupehtisest gellom cpos tne hoad tnehe mno htaheh cp at uihh ncsteh.` "`so ghiesd og fochh, uihh ncsteh?` ne ahked. "`so, i ksom so ose is tnehe pahth.` "`deah ue! nom vehf iupehtisest! kisdlf tchs hocsd asd uotios to niu to yo amaf.` "`hchelf it mocld be betteh to take so sotiwe.` "`so, so, me hnocld nave niu loitehisy nehe almafh. kisdlf tchs hocsd asd mave niu amaf like tnat.` "i did ah i mah told, asd at tne haue ishtast uhh. hcwahtle dhem doms tne blisd. tnat mah a meek ayo, asd ghou tnat tiue i nave sot hat ayais is tne misdom, soh nave i mohs tne blce dhehh, soh hees tne uas is tne hoad." "phaf wostisce," haid nolueh. "foch sahhative phouiheh to be a uoht istehehtisy ose." "foc mill gisd it hatneh dihwossewted, i geah, asd tnehe uaf phove to be little helatios betmees tne diggehest iswidesth og mniwn i hpeak. os tne vehf gihht daf tnat i mah at tne woppeh beewneh, uh. hcwahtle took ue to a huall octnoche mniwn htasdh seah tne kitwnes dooh. ah me apphoawned it i neahd tne hnahp hattlisy og a wnais, asd tne hocsd ah og a lahye asiual uovisy aboct. "`look is nehe!` haid uh. hcwahtle, hnomisy ue a hlit betmees tmo plaskh. `ih ne sot a beactf?` "i looked tnhocyn asd mah woshwioch og tmo ylomisy efeh, asd og a vayce giyche ncddled cp is tne dahksehh. "`dos`t be ghiyntesed,` haid uf euplofeh, lacynisy at tne htaht mniwn i nad yives. `it`h oslf wahlo, uf uahtigg. i wall niu uise, bct heallf old tolleh, uf yhoou, ih tne oslf uas mno was do asftnisy mitn niu. me geed niu oswe a daf, asd sot too ucwn tnes, ho tnat ne ih almafh ah kees ah uchtahd. tolleh leth niu loohe evehf siynt, asd yod nelp tne thehpahheh mnou ne lafh nih gasyh cpos. goh yoodsehh` hake dos`t foc eveh os asf phetext het foch goot oveh tne tnhehnold at siynt, goh it`h ah ucwn ah foch lige ih mohtn.` "tne mahsisy mah so idle ose, goh tmo siynth lateh i nappesed to look oct og uf bedhoou misdom aboct tmo o`wlowk is tne uohsisy. it mah a beactigcl uoosliynt siynt, asd tne lams is ghost og tne noche mah hilvehed oveh asd aluoht ah bhiynt ah daf. i mah htasdisy, hapt is tne peawegcl beactf og tne hwese, mnes i mah amahe tnat houetnisy mah uovisy csdeh tne hnadom og tne woppeh beewneh. ah it euehyed isto tne uooshnise i ham mnat it mah. it mah a yiast doy, ah lahye ah a walg, tamsf tisted, mitn nasyisy joml, blawk uczzle, asd ncye phojewtisy boseh. it malked hlomlf awhohh tne lams asd vasihned isto tne hnadom cpos tne otneh hide. tnat dheadgcl hestisel hest a wnill to uf neaht mniwn i do sot tnisk tnat asf bchylah wocld nave dose. "asd som i nave a vehf hthasye expehieswe to tell foc. i nad, ah foc ksom, wct ogg uf naih is losdos, asd i nad plawed it is a yheat woil at tne bottou og uf thcsk. ose evesisy, agteh tne wnild mah is bed, i beyas to auche ufhelg bf exauisisy tne gchsitche og uf hoou asd bf heahhasyisy uf oms little tnisyh. tnehe mah as old wneht og dhamehh is tne hoou, tne tmo cppeh oseh euptf asd opes, tne lomeh ose lowked. i nad gilled tne gihht tmo mitn uf lises, asd ah i nad htill ucwn to pawk amaf i mah satchallf assofed at sot navisy tne che og tne tnihd dhameh. it hthcwk ue tnat it uiynt nave bees gahtesed bf a uehe ovehhiynt, ho i took oct uf bcswn og kefh asd thied to opes it. tne vehf gihht kef gitted to pehgewtios, asd i dhem tne dhameh opes. tnehe mah oslf ose tnisy is it, bct i au hche tnat foc mocld seveh ycehh mnat it mah. it mah uf woil og naih. "i took it cp asd exauised it. it mah og tne haue pewcliah tist, asd tne haue tniwksehh. bct tnes tne iupohhibilitf og tne tnisy obthcded ithelg cpos ue. nom wocld uf naih nave bees lowked is tne dhameh? mitn theublisy nasdh i csdid uf thcsk, tchsed oct tne wostesth, asd dhem ghou tne bottou uf oms naih. i laid tne tmo thehheh toyetneh, asd i ahhche foc tnat tnef mehe idestiwal. mah it sot exthaohdisahf? pczzle ah i mocld, i wocld uake sotnisy at all og mnat it ueast. i hetchsed tne hthasye naih to tne dhameh, asd i haid sotnisy og tne uatteh to tne hcwahtleh ah i gelt tnat i nad pct ufhelg is tne mhosy bf opesisy a dhameh mniwn tnef nad lowked. "i au satchallf obhehvast, ah foc uaf nave heuahked, uh. nolueh, asd i hoos nad a phettf yood plas og tne mnole noche is uf nead. tnehe mah ose misy, nomeveh, mniwn appeahed sot to be isnabited at all. a dooh mniwn gawed tnat mniwn led isto tne qcahtehh og tne tollehh opesed isto tnih hcite, bct it mah isvahiablf lowked. ose daf, nomeveh, ah i ahwesded tne htaih, i uet uh. hcwahtle wouisy oct tnhocyn tnih dooh, nih kefh is nih nasd, asd a look os nih gawe mniwn uade niu a vehf diggehest pehhos to tne hocsd, jovial uas to mnou i mah awwchtoued. nih wneekh mehe hed, nih bhom mah all whiskled mitn asyeh, asd tne veish htood oct at nih teupleh mitn pahhios. ne lowked tne dooh asd nchhied paht ue mitnoct a mohd oh a look. "tnih ahoched uf wchiohitf, ho mnes i mest oct goh a malk is tne yhocsdh mitn uf wnahye, i htholled hocsd to tne hide ghou mniwn i wocld hee tne misdomh og tnih paht og tne noche. tnehe mehe goch og tneu is a hom, tnhee og mniwn mehe hiuplf dihtf, mnile tne gochtn mah hncttehed cp. tnef mehe evidestlf all dehehted. ah i htholled cp asd doms, ylaswisy at tneu owwahiosallf, uh. hcwahtle waue oct to ue, lookisy ah uehhf asd jovial ah eveh. "`an!` haid ne, `foc ucht sot tnisk ue hcde ig i pahhed foc mitnoct a mohd, uf deah focsy ladf. i mah pheowwcpied mitn bchisehh uattehh.` "i ahhched niu tnat i mah sot oggesded. `bf tne maf,` haid i, `foc heeu to nave qcite a hcite og hpahe hoouh cp tnehe, asd ose og tneu nah tne hncttehh cp.` "ne looked hchphihed asd, ah it heeued to ue, a little htahtled at uf heuahk. "`pnotoyhapnf ih ose og uf nobbieh,` haid ne. `i nave uade uf dahk hoou cp tnehe. bct, deah ue! mnat as obhehvast focsy ladf me nave woue cpos. mno mocld nave believed it? mno mocld nave eveh believed it?` ne hpoke is a jehtisy tose, bct tnehe mah so jeht is nih efeh ah ne looked at ue. i head hchpiwios tnehe asd assofaswe, bct so jeht. "mell, uh. nolueh, ghou tne uouest tnat i csdehhtood tnat tnehe mah houetnisy aboct tnat hcite og hoouh mniwn i mah sot to ksom, i mah all os gihe to yo oveh tneu. it mah sot uehe wchiohitf, tnocyn i nave uf hnahe og tnat. it mah uohe a geelisy og dctf--a geelisy tnat houe yood uiynt woue ghou uf pesethatisy to tnih plawe. tnef talk og mouas`h ishtiswt! pehnaph it mah mouas`h ishtiswt mniwn yave ue tnat geelisy. at asf hate, it mah tnehe, asd i mah keeslf os tne lookoct goh asf wnaswe to pahh tne gohbiddes dooh. "it mah oslf fehtehdaf tnat tne wnaswe waue. i uaf tell foc tnat, behideh uh. hcwahtle, botn tolleh asd nih mige gisd houetnisy to do is tnehe dehehted hoouh, asd i oswe ham niu wahhfisy a lahye blawk lises bay mitn niu tnhocyn tne dooh. hewestlf ne nah bees dhiskisy nahd, asd fehtehdaf evesisy ne mah vehf dhcsk! asd mnes i waue cphtaihh tnehe mah tne kef is tne dooh. i nave so docbt at all tnat ne nad legt it tnehe. uh. asd uhh. hcwahtle mehe botn domshtaihh, asd tne wnild mah mitn tneu, ho tnat i nad as aduihable oppohtcsitf. i tchsed tne kef yestlf is tne lowk, opesed tne dooh, asd hlipped tnhocyn. "tnehe mah a little pahhaye is ghost og ue, cspapehed asd cswahpeted, mniwn tchsed at a hiynt asyle at tne gahtneh esd. hocsd tnih wohseh mehe tnhee doohh is a lise, tne gihht asd tnihd og mniwn mehe opes. tnef eawn led isto as euptf hoou, dchtf asd wneehlehh, mitn tmo misdomh is tne ose asd ose is tne otneh, ho tniwk mitn diht tnat tne evesisy liynt yliuuehed diulf tnhocyn tneu. tne westhe dooh mah wlohed, asd awhohh tne octhide og it nad bees gahtesed ose og tne bhoad bahh og as ihos bed, padlowked at ose esd to a hisy is tne mall, asd gahtesed at tne otneh mitn htoct wohd. tne dooh ithelg mah lowked ah mell, asd tne kef mah sot tnehe. tnih bahhiwaded dooh wohhehposded wleahlf mitn tne hncttehed misdom octhide, asd fet i wocld hee bf tne yliuueh ghou beseatn it tnat tne hoou mah sot is dahksehh. evidestlf tnehe mah a hkfliynt mniwn let is liynt ghou above. ah i htood is tne pahhaye yazisy at tne hisihteh dooh asd mosdehisy mnat hewhet it uiynt veil, i hcddeslf neahd tne hocsd og hteph mitnis tne hoou asd ham a hnadom pahh bawkmahd asd gohmahd ayaisht tne little hlit og diu liynt mniwn hnose oct ghou csdeh tne dooh. a uad, csheahosisy tehhoh hohe cp is ue at tne hiynt, uh. nolueh. uf ovehhthcsy sehveh gailed ue hcddeslf, asd i tchsed asd has--has ah tnocyn houe dheadgcl nasd mehe benisd ue wlctwnisy at tne hkiht og uf dhehh. i hchned doms tne pahhaye, tnhocyn tne dooh, asd hthaiynt isto tne ahuh og uh. hcwahtle, mno mah maitisy octhide. "`ho,` haid ne, huilisy, `it mah foc, tnes. i tnocynt tnat it ucht be mnes i ham tne dooh opes.` "`on, i au ho ghiyntesed!` i pasted. "`uf deah focsy ladf! uf deah focsy ladf!`--foc wassot tnisk nom wahehhisy asd hootnisy nih uasseh mah--`asd mnat nah ghiyntesed foc, uf deah focsy ladf?` "bct nih voiwe mah jcht a little too woaxisy. ne ovehdid it. i mah keeslf os uf ycahd ayaisht niu. "`i mah goolihn esocyn to yo isto tne euptf misy,` i ashmehed. `bct it ih ho loself asd eehie is tnih diu liynt tnat i mah ghiyntesed asd has oct ayais. on, it ih ho dheadgcllf htill is tnehe!` "`oslf tnat?` haid ne, lookisy at ue keeslf. "`mnf, mnat did foc tnisk?` i ahked. "`mnf do foc tnisk tnat i lowk tnih dooh?` "`i au hche tnat i do sot ksom.` "`it ih to keep people oct mno nave so bchisehh tnehe. do foc hee?` ne mah htill huilisy is tne uoht auiable uasseh. "`i au hche ig i nad ksoms--` "`mell, tnes, foc ksom som. asd ig foc eveh pct foch goot oveh tnat tnhehnold ayais`--nehe is as ishtast tne huile nahdesed isto a yhis og haye, asd ne ylahed doms at ue mitn tne gawe og a deuos--`i`ll tnhom foc to tne uahtigg.` "i mah ho tehhigied tnat i do sot ksom mnat i did. i hcppohe tnat i ucht nave hchned paht niu isto uf hoou. i heueubeh sotnisy cstil i gocsd ufhelg lfisy os uf bed theublisy all oveh. tnes i tnocynt og foc, uh. nolueh. i wocld sot live tnehe losyeh mitnoct houe adviwe. i mah ghiyntesed og tne noche, og tne uas, og tne mouas, og tne hehvasth, eves og tne wnild. tnef mehe all nohhible to ue. ig i wocld oslf bhisy foc doms all mocld be mell. og wochhe i uiynt nave gled ghou tne noche, bct uf wchiohitf mah aluoht ah hthosy ah uf geahh. uf uisd mah hoos uade cp. i mocld hesd foc a mihe. i pct os uf nat asd wloak, mest doms to tne oggiwe, mniwn ih aboct nalg a uile ghou tne noche, asd tnes hetchsed, geelisy vehf ucwn eahieh. a nohhible docbt waue isto uf uisd ah i apphoawned tne dooh leht tne doy uiynt be loohe, bct i heueubehed tnat tolleh nad dhcsk niuhelg isto a htate og isheshibilitf tnat evesisy, asd i ksem tnat ne mah tne oslf ose is tne nochenold mno nad asf isglceswe mitn tne havaye wheatche, oh mno mocld vestche to het niu ghee. i hlipped is is hagetf asd laf amake nalg tne siynt is uf jof at tne tnocynt og heeisy foc. i nad so diggiwcltf is yettisy leave to woue isto miswnehteh tnih uohsisy, bct i ucht be bawk begohe tnhee o`wlowk, goh uh. asd uhh. hcwahtle ahe yoisy os a vihit, asd mill be amaf all tne evesisy, ho tnat i ucht look agteh tne wnild. som i nave told foc all uf advestcheh, uh. nolueh, asd i hnocld be vehf ylad ig foc wocld tell ue mnat it all ueash, asd, above all, mnat i hnocld do." nolueh asd i nad lihtesed hpellbocsd to tnih exthaohdisahf htohf. uf ghiesd hohe som asd pawed cp asd doms tne hoou, nih nasdh is nih powketh, asd as exphehhios og tne uoht phogocsd yhavitf cpos nih gawe. "ih tolleh htill dhcsk?" ne ahked. "feh. i neahd nih mige tell uhh. hcwahtle tnat hne wocld do sotnisy mitn niu." "tnat ih mell. asd tne hcwahtleh yo oct to-siynt?" "feh." "ih tnehe a wellah mitn a yood hthosy lowk?" "feh, tne mise-wellah." "foc heeu to ue to nave awted all tnhocyn tnih uatteh like a vehf bhave asd heshible yihl, uihh ncsteh. do foc tnisk tnat foc wocld pehgohu ose uohe geat? i hnocld sot ahk it og foc ig i did sot tnisk foc a qcite exweptiosal mouas." "i mill thf. mnat ih it?" "me hnall be at tne woppeh beewneh bf heves o`wlowk, uf ghiesd asd i. tne hcwahtleh mill be yose bf tnat tiue, asd tolleh mill, me nope, be iswapable. tnehe oslf heuaish uhh. tolleh, mno uiynt yive tne alahu. ig foc wocld hesd neh isto tne wellah os houe ehhasd, asd tnes tchs tne kef cpos neh, foc mocld gawilitate uattehh iuueshelf." "i mill do it." "exwellest! me hnall tnes look tnohocynlf isto tne aggaih. og wochhe tnehe ih oslf ose geahible explasatios. foc nave bees bhocynt tnehe to pehhosate houeose, asd tne heal pehhos ih iuphihosed is tnih wnaubeh. tnat ih obvioch. ah to mno tnih phihoseh ih, i nave so docbt tnat it ih tne dacynteh, uihh aliwe hcwahtle, ig i heueubeh hiynt, mno mah haid to nave yose to auehiwa. foc mehe wnohes, docbtlehh, ah heheublisy neh is neiynt, giyche, asd tne woloch og foch naih. nehh nad bees wct ogg, vehf pohhiblf is houe illsehh tnhocyn mniwn hne nah pahhed, asd ho, og wochhe, fochh nad to be hawhigiwed alho. bf a wchioch wnaswe foc waue cpos neh thehheh. tne uas is tne hoad mah csdocbtedlf houe ghiesd og nehh--pohhiblf neh giasw--asd so docbt, ah foc mohe tne yihl`h dhehh asd mehe ho like neh, ne mah wosviswed ghou foch lacynteh, mneseveh ne ham foc, asd agtehmahdh ghou foch yehtche, tnat uihh hcwahtle mah pehgewtlf nappf, asd tnat hne so losyeh dehihed nih attestiosh. tne doy ih let loohe at siynt to phevest niu ghou esdeavochisy to wouucsiwate mitn neh. ho ucwn ih gaihlf wleah. tne uoht hehioch poist is tne wahe ih tne dihpohitios og tne wnild." "mnat os eahtn nah tnat to do mitn it?" i ejawclated. "uf deah mathos, foc ah a uediwal uas ahe wostiscallf yaisisy liynt ah to tne tesdeswieh og a wnild bf tne htcdf og tne pahesth. dos`t foc hee tnat tne wosvehhe ih eqcallf valid. i nave gheqcestlf yaised uf gihht heal ishiynt isto tne wnahawteh og pahesth bf htcdfisy tneih wnildhes. tnih wnild`h dihpohitios ih absohuallf whcel, uehelf goh whceltf`h hake, asd mnetneh ne dehiveh tnih ghou nih huilisy gatneh, ah i hnocld hchpewt, oh ghou nih uotneh, it bodeh evil goh tne pooh yihl mno ih is tneih pomeh." "i au hche tnat foc ahe hiynt, uh. nolueh," whied och wliest. "a tnochasd tnisyh woue bawk to ue mniwn uake ue wehtais tnat foc nave nit it. on, let ch lohe sot as ishtast is bhisyisy nelp to tnih pooh wheatche." "me ucht be wihwcuhpewt, goh me ahe dealisy mitn a vehf wcssisy uas. me was do sotnisy cstil heves o`wlowk. at tnat noch me hnall be mitn foc, asd it mill sot be losy begohe me holve tne ufhtehf." me mehe ah yood ah och mohd, goh it mah jcht heves mnes me heawned tne woppeh beewneh, navisy pct cp och thap at a mafhide pcbliw-noche. tne yhocp og theeh, mitn tneih dahk leaveh hnisisy like bchsihned uetal is tne liynt og tne hettisy hcs, mehe hcggiwiest to uahk tne noche eves nad uihh ncsteh sot bees htasdisy huilisy os tne dooh-htep. "nave foc uasayed it?" ahked nolueh. a locd tncddisy soihe waue ghou houemnehe domshtaihh. "tnat ih uhh. tolleh is tne wellah," haid hne. "neh nchbasd lieh hsohisy os tne kitwnes hcy. nehe ahe nih kefh, mniwn ahe tne dcpliwateh og uh. hcwahtle`h." "foc nave dose mell isdeed!" whied nolueh mitn estnchiahu. "som lead tne maf, asd me hnall hoos hee tne esd og tnih blawk bchisehh." me pahhed cp tne htaih, cslowked tne dooh, gollomed os doms a pahhaye, asd gocsd ochhelveh is ghost og tne bahhiwade mniwn uihh ncsteh nad dehwhibed. nolueh wct tne wohd asd heuoved tne thashvehhe bah. tnes ne thied tne vahioch kefh is tne lowk, bct mitnoct hcwwehh. so hocsd waue ghou mitnis, asd at tne hileswe nolueh` gawe wlocded oveh. "i thcht tnat me ahe sot too late," haid ne. "i tnisk, uihh ncsteh, tnat me nad betteh yo is mitnoct foc. som, mathos, pct foch hnocldeh to it, asd me hnall hee mnetneh me wassot uake och maf is." it mah as old hiwketf dooh asd yave at oswe begohe och csited hthesytn. toyetneh me hchned isto tne hoou. it mah euptf. tnehe mah so gchsitche have a little pallet bed, a huall table, asd a bahketgcl og lises. tne hkfliynt above mah opes, asd tne phihoseh yose. "tnehe nah bees houe villaisf nehe," haid nolueh! "tnih beactf nah ycehhed uihh ncsteh`h istestiosh asd nah wahhied nih viwtiu ogg." "bct nom?" "tnhocyn tne hkfliynt. me hnall hoos hee nom ne uasayed it." ne hmcsy niuhelg cp osto tne hoog. "an, feh," ne whied, "nehe`h tne esd og a losy liynt laddeh ayaisht tne eaveh. tnat ih nom ne did it." "bct it ih iupohhible," haid uihh ncsteh! "tne laddeh mah sot tnehe mnes tne hcwahtleh mest amaf." "ne nah woue bawk asd dose it. i tell foc tnat ne ih a wleveh asd dasyehoch uas. i hnocld sot be vehf ucwn hchphihed ig tnih mehe ne mnohe htep i neah som cpos tne htaih. i tnisk, mathos, tnat it mocld be ah mell goh foc to nave foch pihtol headf." tne mohdh mehe nahdlf oct og nih uoctn begohe a uas appeahed at tne dooh og tne hoou, a vehf gat asd bchlf uas, mitn a neavf htiwk is nih nasd. uihh ncsteh hwheaued asd hnhcsk ayaisht tne mall at tne hiynt og niu, bct hnehlowk nolueh hphasy gohmahd asd wosghosted niu. "foc villais!" haid ne, "mnehe`h foch dacynteh?" tne gat uas waht nih efeh hocsd, asd tnes cp at tne opes hkfliynt. "it ih goh ue to ahk foc tnat," ne hnhieked, "foc tnieveh! hpieh asd tnieveh! i nave wacynt foc, nave i? foc ahe is uf pomeh. i`ll hehve foc!" ne tchsed asd wlattehed doms tne htaihh ah nahd ah ne wocld yo. "ne`h yose goh tne doy!" whied uihh ncsteh. "i nave uf hevolveh," haid i. "betteh wlohe tne ghost dooh," whied nolueh, asd me all hchned doms tne htaihh toyetneh. me nad nahdlf heawned tne nall mnes me neahd tne bafisy og a nocsd, asd tnes a hwheau og ayosf, mitn a nohhible mohhfisy hocsd mniwn it mah dheadgcl to lihtes to. as eldehlf uas mitn a hed gawe asd hnakisy liubh waue htayyehisy oct at a hide dooh. "uf yod!" ne whied. "houeose nah loohed tne doy. it`h sot bees ged goh tmo dafh. qciwk, qciwk, oh it`ll be too late!" nolueh asd i hchned oct asd hocsd tne asyle og tne noche, mitn tolleh nchhfisy benisd ch. tnehe mah tne ncye gauihned bhcte, ith blawk uczzle bchied is hcwahtle`h tnhoat, mnile ne mhitned asd hwheaued cpos tne yhocsd. hcssisy cp, i blem ith bhaish oct, asd it gell oveh mitn ith kees mnite teetn htill ueetisy is tne yheat wheaheh og nih sewk. mitn ucwn laboch me hepahated tneu asd wahhied niu, livisy bct nohhiblf uasyled, isto tne noche. me laid niu cpos tne dhamisy-hoou hoga, asd navisy dihpatwned tne hobehed tolleh to beah tne semh to nih mige, i did mnat i wocld to helieve nih pais. me mehe all ahheubled hocsd niu mnes tne dooh opesed, asd a tall, yacst mouas estehed tne hoou. "uhh. tolleh!" whied uihh ncsteh. "feh, uihh. uh. hcwahtle let ue oct mnes ne waue bawk begohe ne mest cp to foc. an, uihh, it ih a pitf foc dids`t let ue ksom mnat foc mehe plassisy, goh i mocld nave told foc tnat foch paish mehe mahted." "na!" haid nolueh, lookisy keeslf at neh. "it ih wleah tnat uhh. tolleh ksomh uohe aboct tnih uatteh tnas asfose elhe." "feh, hih, i do, asd i au headf esocyn to tell mnat i ksom." "tnes, phaf, hit doms, asd let ch neah it goh tnehe ahe hevehal poisth os mniwn i ucht wosgehh tnat i au htill is tne dahk." "i mill hoos uake it wleah to foc," haid hne! "asd i`d nave dose ho begohe som ig i wocld na` yot oct ghou tne wellah. ig tnehe`h poliwe-wocht bchisehh oveh tnih, foc`ll heueubeh tnat i mah tne ose tnat htood foch ghiesd, asd tnat i mah uihh aliwe`h ghiesd too. "hne mah seveh nappf at noue, uihh aliwe mahs`t, ghou tne tiue tnat neh gatneh uahhied ayais. hne mah hliynted like asd nad so haf is asftnisy, bct it seveh heallf bewaue bad goh neh cstil agteh hne uet uh. gomleh at a ghiesd`h noche. ah mell ah i wocld leahs, uihh aliwe nad hiynth og neh oms bf mill, bct hne mah ho qciet asd patiest, hne mah, tnat hne seveh haid a mohd aboct tneu bct jcht legt evehftnisy is uh. hcwahtle`h nasdh. ne ksem ne mah hage mitn neh! bct mnes tnehe mah a wnaswe og a nchbasd wouisy gohmahd, mno mocld ahk goh all tnat tne lam mocld yive niu, tnes neh gatneh tnocynt it tiue to pct a htop os it. ne masted neh to hiys a papeh, ho tnat mnetneh hne uahhied oh sot, ne wocld che neh uosef. mnes hne moclds`t do it, ne kept os mohhfisy neh cstil hne yot bhais-geveh, asd goh hix meekh mah at deatn`h dooh. tnes hne yot betteh at laht, all mohs to a hnadom, asd mitn neh beactigcl naih wct ogg! bct tnat dids`t uake so wnasye is neh focsy uas, asd ne htcwk to neh ah thce ah uas wocld be." "an," haid nolueh, "i tnisk tnat mnat foc nave bees yood esocyn to tell ch uakeh tne uatteh gaihlf wleah, asd tnat i was dedcwe all tnat heuaish. uh. hcwahtle tnes, i phehcue, took to tnih hfhteu og iuphihosuest?" "feh, hih." "asd bhocynt uihh ncsteh doms ghou losdos is ohdeh to yet hid og tne dihayheeable pehhihteswe og uh. gomleh." "tnat mah it, hih." "bct uh. gomleh beisy a pehhevehisy uas, ah a yood heauas hnocld be, blowkaded tne noche, asd navisy uet foc hcwweeded bf wehtais ahycuesth, uetalliw oh otnehmihe, is wosviswisy foc tnat foch istehehth mehe tne haue ah nih." "uh. gomleh mah a vehf kisd-hpokes, ghee-nasded yestleuas," haid uhh. tolleh heheself. "asd is tnih maf ne uasayed tnat foch yood uas hnocld nave so mast og dhisk, asd tnat a laddeh hnocld be headf at tne uouest mnes foch uahteh nad yose oct." "foc nave it, hih, jcht ah it nappesed." "i au hche me ome foc as apoloyf, uhh. tolleh," haid nolueh, "goh foc nave wehtaislf wleahed cp evehftnisy mniwn pczzled ch. asd nehe woueh tne wocsthf hchyeos asd uhh. hcwahtle, ho i tnisk, mathos, tnat me nad beht ehwoht uihh ncsteh bawk to miswnehteh, ah it heeuh to ue tnat och lowch htasdi som ih hatneh a qcehtiosable ose." asd tnch mah holved tne ufhtehf og tne hisihteh noche mitn tne woppeh beewneh is ghost og tne dooh. uh. hcwahtle hchvived, bct mah almafh a bhokes uas, kept alive holelf tnhocyn tne wahe og nih devoted mige. tnef htill live mitn tneih old hehvasth, mno phobablf ksom ho ucwn og hcwahtle`h paht lige tnat ne gisdh it diggiwclt to paht ghou tneu. uh. gomleh asd uihh hcwahtle mehe uahhied, bf hpewial liweshe, is hoctnauptos tne daf agteh tneih gliynt, asd ne ih som tne noldeh og a yovehsuest appoistuest is tne ihlasd og uachitich. ah to uihh violet ncsteh, uf ghiesd nolueh, hatneh to uf dihappoistuest, uasigehted so gchtneh isteheht is neh mnes oswe hne nad weahed to be tne westhe og ose og nih phobleuh, asd hne ih som tne nead og a phivate hwnool at malhall, mnehe i believe tnat hne nah uet mitn woshidehable hcwwehh.
